# Builderforce.ai — Roadmap & Gap Register

> Single source of truth for **outstanding** work (TODO · In Progress · Partial) and deferred issues for the Builderforce.ai sub-project. The [README](./README.md) documents what exists today; completed/shipped/resolved items live in **[DONE.md](./DONE.md)**; this file tracks only what's next and what's broken. Deferred issues found during work are appended to the **Consolidated Gap Register** below.

---

## Platform Roadmap (umbrella — Builderforce.ai · BuilderForce Agents · MambaCode.js · SSM.js)

> **Vision**: Human as the manager — developers supervise, prioritize, approve, and steer AI agents rather than writing code themselves.

### 🌟 North Star — "Define a need, the agentic system solves it"

> **The platform lets any human define a need in any modality, and compiles it into an agent that runs on the right surface.** The need can be: *review a team's SOPs and share a more efficient process flow*; *train an agent on a company's proprietary data and stand up a custom support agent*; *a custom agent that executes in the IDE, on the desktop (on-prem), or in the cloud*; or *a manager defining workflow / process charts and embedding those steps into an agent to execute*. The modality (prose · dataset/docs · process chart · persona · diagnostic findings) and the surface (IDE · desktop · cloud · workflow step) vary — the spine does not.

The unifying primitive is the **compile primitive**: `compile(need, modality) → AgentSpec → deploy(AgentSpec, surface)`. Today the platform has **four separate "need → executing agent" front doors** (diagnostic run · train+publish · workflow builder · persona builder), each compiling a different need-representation into a different artifact with **no shared spec and no shared deploy step**. The North-Star work is to rehome those four onto one `AgentSpec` spine so persona params, trained memory, and policy gates reach **every** surface, and so plain-language and diagnostic findings become first-class need front doors. Full design: **[PRD-agent-compile-primitive.md](./PRD-agent-compile-primitive.md)**. Honest pillar-by-pillar delta logged in the Gap Register (**"VISION GAP AUDIT — define-a-need → executing-agent"**).

## Key Metrics

**Acquisition:** GitHub stars (target 10K by Q2 2026) · npm weekly downloads (5K by Q2 2026) · Discord members (2K by Q2 2026)

**Activation:** Projects with `.builderforce/` initialized (500 active projects) · workflows executed/day (1K/day by Q2 2026) · MCP connections (200 by Q3 2026)

**Retention:** DAU/MAU ≥ 30% · weekly active agents connected to Builderforce · average sessions/user/week

## Next Milestones

The items below are the next high-impact milestones, ordered by business priority. Items marked **P0** are blocking shipped features; **P1** are required for full enterprise readiness.

### P0 — Blocking Today

| Item | What it unlocks |
| ---- | --------------- |
| **Remote task result streaming** | Multi-agent orchestration actually returns results. Today `remote:<id>` steps complete but return empty output, making dependent workflow steps non-functional. Fix: `correlationId` round-trip on `ClawRelayDO` so the originating agent awaits the `remote.result` frame. |
| **Execution WebSocket streaming** | Replaces 2-second polling loop in `clawlink-adapter.ts` with a server-push stream; cuts execution latency and load on the Builderforce relay. |
| **Live Orchestration Workspace** (Builderforce SPA) | Real-time DAG view of running agents — task status, role, model, streaming output. Required to demo and sell the multi-agent story; Devin and Windsurf Cascade both ship this. |
| **BuilderForce Agents as MCP Provider** | Exposes `project_knowledge`, `codebase_search`, `git_history`, and `workflow_status` via the `/mcp` endpoint on the local gateway. Cursor and Continue.dev users can call BuilderForce Agents tools without switching to the BuilderForce Agents TUI — this is a distribution multiplier. |

### P1 — Enterprise Readiness

| Item | What it unlocks |
| ---- | --------------- |
| **Diff staging & inline approval API** | Agent file edits buffered for human review before landing on disk. Risk-averse teams (the highest-value buyer segment) require this. `/diff`, `/accept`, `/reject` commands are already in the TUI; the Builderforce-side `pending_diffs` table and relay frame complete the loop. |
| **Spec & workflow storage API** | `/spec` workflow outputs (PRD, arch spec, task list) pushed to Builderforce and queryable by goal/status/project. Turns ephemeral planning runs into auditable, reviewable artifacts with a lifecycle. |
| **Spec review + workflow portal SPA** | Web UI for product owners to view, review, and approve agent-generated specs, then trigger implementation workflows. |

### P2 — Observability & Unit Economics

| Item | What it unlocks |
| ---- | --------------- |
| **Token usage dashboard** | Historical context pressure, token spend, and compaction events per session. Required before any usage-based pricing model can be built. |
| **Agent run audit trail** | Immutable, queryable log of every tool call (name, args, result, duration) per run. Required for SOC 2 / compliance-sensitive buyers. |
| **Fleet capability management SPA** | Per-agent online status, reported capabilities, and declared capabilities — UI for the `remote:auto[caps]` routing already implemented in the orchestrator. |
| **Persona registry API** | Team-shared agent personas synced from Builderforce to all agents via heartbeat response; no more manual YAML file distribution. |

### P3 — Future Moat

| Item | What it unlocks |
| ---- | --------------- |
| **Model cost tracking** | Per-session cost estimate, monthly budget alerts, per-project breakdown. Foundation for COGS control and chargeback. |
| **Approval workflow API** | Agent requests human approval before destructive operations (`rm`, force-push, deploy). Relay frame triggers browser notification; execution is suspended until approved/rejected. |
| **Spec import (GitHub Issues / Linear / Jira)** | `/spec import <url>` converts an issue tracker ticket into a Builderforce spec and starts the planning workflow. |
| **Cross-agent memory sharing** | Opt-in memory sync between agents with tenant-scoped access control, deduplication by content hash, and `#private` tag filtering. |

---

## Known Implementation Gaps (Builderforce.ai API)

Gaps found during audit on 2026-03-28. Severity reflects impact on shipped user flows.

| Gap | Location | Severity | Resolution |
|-----|----------|----------|------------|
| Agent channels endpoint always returns `[]` — stub with no DB query | `clawRoutes.ts:1103` | **HIGH** | Documented gap — no channel registry table exists; needs schema design |
| Helcim checkout creates no recurring billing schedule — subscriptions are one-time charges | `HelcimProvider.ts:78` | **HIGH** | Documented — requires Helcim recurring billing API call after `APPROVED` webhook |
| Helcim webhook mapping is a placeholder — all `APPROVED` events become `subscription.activated` | `HelcimProvider.ts:130` | **HIGH** | Documented — requires Helcim webhook payload schema from dashboard |

## Risk Register

| Risk | Probability | Impact | Mitigation |
|------|------------|--------|------------|
| Anthropic/OpenAI ships multi-agent IDE tool | High | High | Double down on self-hosting + open source moat |
| Cursor/Windsurf adds MCP + multi-agent | Medium | High | Ship live workflow DAG and agent mesh — unique differentiators |
| Model API costs too high for free tier | Medium | Medium | Aggressive rate limiting + BuilderForce AgentsLLM margin |
| Enterprise sales cycle too long | High | Low | Focus on SMB Teams plan first; use as reference for enterprise |
| Community fragmentation (forks) | Low | Medium | Engage contributors early; offer ClawHub as incentive |

## Consolidated Gap Register

### 🧠 Unified Brain chat experience — web + VS Code — follow-ups (SHIPPED 2026-06-29; consolidation + gap-closing passes 2026-06-29, VSIX `2026.6.38`)

**Closed this pass (the three substantive follow-ups):**
- **DONE — Brain webview now exposes the full platform catalog, not just local file tools.** The webview mounts `brain-embedded`'s `useMcpExtensions()` — the EXACT hook the web Brain uses — fetching `/llm/v1/mcp/tools` and relaying `/llm/v1/mcp/call` directly from the `vscode-webview://` origin (CORS already trusts the scheme, app-wide). So the IDE Brain can manage tasks/projects/OKRs/specs, not just edit files: one brain, one tool catalog, zero duplicated list. On any catalog write it posts `platform.write` to the host, which invalidates the task cache + repaints Project & Tasks live (`BrainWebview.configure({ onPlatformWrite })`).
- **DONE — two chat surfaces consolidated onto the unified Brain; legacy `ChatPanel` retired.** Deleted `src/chatPanel.ts`, `media/main.js`, `media/main.css`, `src/sessionStore.ts` (and the now-dead `bfApi.loadTaskConversation`/`getExecution`/`BfConversationMessage`). The Sessions sidebar (`sessionsTree.ts`) now lists the SAME server-side `/api/brain` chats (new `bfApi.listBrainChats`/`renameBrainChat`/`deleteBrainChat`, 5s-cached); clicking/renaming/deleting a row drives the singleton Brain panel via a buffered `intent` channel (`new`/`focus`/`task`). `startTaskSession` + `runTask` open the Brain seeded for the task (it can act via the platform tools). The native `agent.ts` loop is KEPT (still backs the stable `@builderforce` chat participant + the proposed-API session tab, per the follow-up's "retire only if chatParticipant is also migrated").
- **DONE — VS Code webview is localized.** Added a `vscode.l10n` bundle (`l10n/bundle.l10n.{json,zh-cn,es,fr,de}.json`, `"l10n": "./l10n"`); the host translates the `<BrainTimeline>` + composer labels (display language) and forwards them through `init.labels` (the webview ships no i18n stack — next-intl is web-only). New host command prompts (rename/delete chat) route through `vscode.l10n.t` too.

**Remaining / accepted:**
- **"Thought for Xs" uses the full LLM-turn duration**, not true time-to-first-token (the gateway streams no reasoning tokens; thinking is off). Acceptable approximation; revisit if the gateway later exposes reasoning/first-token timing.
- **Runtime smoke-test still pending:** the extension builds + typechecks + packages (`2026.6.38`) but was not launched in an Extension Development Host this pass (no interactive VS Code). Verify: sign-in handshake, streaming transcript, a local file-edit tool round-trip (approve gate), a platform-tool write (e.g. `tasks.create`) refreshing the tree, the Sessions-sidebar → focus-chat intent, and an image attachment end-to-end.

### 🧠 Brain chat triage + web/VS Code parity (2026-06-29, VSIX `2026.6.39`)

**Closed this pass:**
- **DONE — re-added Copy-chat + Diagnostics buttons to the VS Code Brain header.** New `webview/src/transcript.ts` serializes the live conversation (turns + tool input/output + errors) by reusing the shared `buildTimeline`/`formatPayload` view-model, so the copied text matches the rendered timeline. The header `⧉` button posts `copy` → host writes the transcript to the clipboard (a sandboxed webview can't); the `🩺` button posts `diagnose` → runs the existing `builderforce.diagnose` connection-diagnostics command. Localized in all five `bundle.l10n.*` catalogs.
- **DONE — fixed the broken `build-and-deploy` (next-on-pages Edge Runtime).** `/blog`, `/compare/[competitor]`, and `/pricing` were flagged as not configured for the Edge Runtime, failing the Cloudflare Pages build — **why production web still showed the pre-`BrainTimeline` chat bubbles** (the unified-timeline commit `75d14513` never deployed). `/blog` and `/pricing` are dynamic (cookie-i18n) → added `export const runtime = 'edge'`; `/compare/[competitor]` is fully static (`generateStaticParams` + `dynamicParams = false`, which Next 15.5 forbids combining with `runtime='edge'`) so it stays prerendered, mirroring `/integrations/[tool]`. Web Brain already renders the same shared `<BrainTimeline>` as VS Code; once this deploys, both surfaces match.
- **DONE — fixed image paste → "No response" (root cause: vision capability mis-declared).** The direct-Google `googleai/gemini-2.5-flash|flash-lite|pro` catalog entries declared NO `capabilities`, so the gateway shape-router (`reorderPoolByShape`/`capabilitiesForModel`) treated the user's own top model as non-vision and demoted it below the small declared vision models on an image request — which returned an empty turn that surfaces as the literal "No response." fallback. Declared `['tools','structured_output','vision']` on all three Gemini 2.5 entries (natively multimodal + tool-capable; the strict-`json_schema` ceiling stays handled by `isLowSchemaCeilingModel`). Regression test in `reorderPoolByShape.test.ts`; gateway + SDK bumped to `2026.6.31`.
- **CLOSED (gap-closing pass 2026-06-29) — IDE Brain can now monitor a dispatched run.** The gateway catalog already advertises the full `executions.*` READ suite (`get` / `trace` / `list_for_task` / `list_active` / `list_recent` / `task_file_changes`, tenant+segment-scoped — `builtinMcpService.ts`), which the IDE Brain receives via `useMcpExtensions`. To make it *usable*, `runTask` now opens the Brain with a `dispatched` task intent and the seed nudges the Brain to "check the latest execution's status and trace, then help me follow up" (localized `app.taskSeedDispatched` ×5). The IDE both dispatches AND monitors the run via the shared tools — no bespoke trace panel.
- **CLOSED (gap-closing pass 2026-06-29) — extension `package.json` chrome is localized.** Added `package.nls.{json,zh-cn,es,fr,de}` and routed every manifest string through `%key%`: `description`, the 3 view names, both `viewsWelcome` bodies, all 26 command titles, the chat-participant description, all config property/enum descriptions (39 keys × 5 locales). The display language now covers the command palette, view headers, welcome views, and Settings UI — not just the runtime webview.
- **CLOSED (gap-closing pass 2026-06-29; prompt half) — the IDE system prompt is ONE shared source.** Extracted `src/idePersona.ts` (`ideSystemPromptBase` + `withWorkspaceMap` + `WORKSPACE_MAP_INTRO`, pure strings); both the native participant (`prompt.ts` → `ChatMessage[]`) and the Brain webview (`webview/src/systemPrompt.ts` → string) import it, so the persona can't drift (imported across the esbuild host + Vite webview bundles).
- **GAP (loop half, narrowed) — unify the agent LOOP across surfaces.** Tool catalog + transcript UI + system prompt are now shared; what remains is the run loop — the webview Brain runs on `brain-embedded` (React-coupled, persists to `/api/brain`) while the `@builderforce` participant runs the native `agent.ts` loop streaming to a `ChatResponseStream`. Truly one loop = extract a framework-free `runBrainLoop()` from `brain-embedded` (`brainRunStore` + hooks) that the participant can drive, injecting transport + client-local tools + a stream sink. Lower-priority now (host adapters, not duplicated logic). Fold in: the native loop injects the limbic affect block, which the webview Brain does NOT (the brain-embedded `resolveSystemPrompt` is sync, so a per-turn async limbic fetch isn't wired).

### 🎯 VS Code editor agent — northstar feature gaps (analysis 2026-06-30)

> Northstar: an AI agent in the editor that **ships code** AND **runs your team's actual work** (projects/tasks/OKRs, dispatch + follow runs) without context-switching to a dashboard. Today the editor agent can EDIT files (`read/list/write/edit/delete_file`) and READ/WRITE work items via the shared catalog, but the "ship" half is missing its core primitives and the "no dashboard" promise still breaks for PR/CI. Prioritized:

**Tier 1 — "ship code" primitives (DONE 2026-06-30, VSIX `2026.6.40`):**
- **DONE — `run_command` tool** (`fileTools.ts`, `mutating` → approval gate, shows the exact command line in the webview confirm). The agent runs tests/build/lint/typecheck/install in the workspace root (2-min timeout, output clamped) and reads failures to fix them, and runs `git`/`gh` to commit/push/open a PR — so an edit goes idea → verified → shipped without leaving the editor. Lights up BOTH surfaces (webview Brain + native participant) via the shared `TOOL_DEFS`.
- **DONE — `search_code` tool** (`fileTools.ts`, read-only, bounded JS walk: skips node_modules/.git/build dirs + binaries, caps matches/files). Regex search returns `path:line: text` so the agent finds the right code before editing on large repos.
- **REMAINING (enhancement) — dedicated git/PR tools.** `run_command` already lets the agent drive `git`/`gh`, but a first-class "Open PR" action (reusing the repos/GitHub integration + a structured PR form) would be richer and need no `gh` on PATH. Lower priority now that the raw capability exists.

**Tier 2 — "run your team's work" without leaving the editor:**
- **GAP — PRs + CI status not in the editor.** The platform syncs GitHub PRs, fails CI → ticket, and generates code-review reports, but the editor can't surface "your open PRs / failing CI / review requests." The "no dashboard" promise breaks here. Add a PR/CI panel (or catalog tools) so review/triage happens in-editor.
- **GAP — no proactive work inbox.** Assigned tasks, human-in-the-loop approval requests (`humanRequests` is a manual quick-pick, not proactive), and review requests should be a live inbox with notifications, not pull-only. Unblocks: the agent/editor tells you what needs you, matching the "run your team's work" half.
- **GAP — production error → fix loop not surfaced.** The Quality pillar groups errors → one-click agent fix; the editor doesn't surface "errors in your service → fix here." Add an errors panel that opens the Brain seeded to fix a fingerprinted error group.

**Tier 3 — polish / risk:**
- **GAP — per-file Apply/Skip only; no changeset diff review.** A multi-file turn can't be reviewed as one diff before applying. Add a changeset/diff review surface.
- **RISK — extension never launched in an Extension Development Host** (carried from the 2026.6.38 pass): sign-in handshake, streaming transcript, file-edit approval round-trip, platform-tool write refreshing the tree, focus-chat intent, and image attach are unverified end-to-end in a live editor.

### 🤖 Swimlane autonomous-agent trigger — Brain bypass + ownership clobber — remaining gaps (FIXED 2026-06-29; write-up in [DONE.md](./DONE.md))

**Remaining adjacent gaps (NOT fixed this pass):**
- **Other direct `TaskService` status-writers still bypass the lane trigger:** `repoAnalysisRoutes.ts:85` (`updateTask {status: IN_PROGRESS}`) and the create paths in `qualityRoutes.ts:545` / `QaFindingRouter.ts:152` call `TaskService` directly without invoking `maybeAutoRunOnLaneEntry`. Niche internal flows, but a ticket they move/create into a staffed lane won't auto-run. Fixing = same one-line trigger call from each (or route them through the canonical route via `replayRoute`).
- **Silent no-op is undiagnosable to the dragger:** when a staffed lane doesn't fire because its gate is `human` (the default `in_review` gate), its agent has a null `agentRef` (legacy free-text role assignment), or the swimlane `key` ≠ the task status, the user sees nothing. Only the capability-mismatch case logs a warning. Surface a board-side signal ("lane gated to human" / "no runnable agent") so a mis-configured lane is visible.
- **Resident tickets don't fire:** the trigger fires on lane ENTRY only. Tickets already sitting in a lane before an agent is configured (or before the gate flips to `auto`) get no entry event and never auto-run. A "run lane now" / backfill action would cover them.
- **`maybeAutoRunOnLaneEntry` board lookup is unordered:** `boards.where(projectId).limit(1)` with no `orderBy` — harmless under the `UNIQUE(project_id)` constraint, but for legacy duplicate-board data it could read a different board's lanes than `findOrCreateBoard` (which tiebreaks on `createdAt`). Align the tiebreak.

### 🧱 Frontend `next build` blocked by missing `mp4-muxer` dep (added 2026-06-29)

`npx next build` fails to compile: `@seanhogg/builderforce-studio-embedded` (→ its nested `@seanhogg/builderforce-studio/dist/index.mjs`) does `import { Muxer, ArrayBufferTarget } from 'mp4-muxer'`, but `mp4-muxer` is **not installed and not declared** in `frontend/package.json`. Reached via `src/app/ide/[id]/page.tsx → IDE.tsx → IDENew.tsx`. Pre-existing and unrelated to marketing-page work (surfaced while running build verification of the marketing i18n pass). Fixing it (add `mp4-muxer` to deps, or make the studio export lazy/optional) unblocks `next build` / `cf-build` and any CI that builds the frontend. Note: `tsgo --noEmit` typecheck passes — only the webpack/module-resolution build step is blocked.

### 🔀 Platform Migration & Integration Hub — Jira/Monday/Rally/GitLab/Bitbucket → BuilderForce — open gaps (added 2026-06-29; write-up in [DONE.md](./DONE.md))

- **GAP — no custom-field / comment / attachment migration:** only title/body/type/status/story-points/assignee transfer; Jira custom fields, comments, and attachments are dropped. Extending staging with a field map + a per-provider comments/attachments pull is a large follow-on, intentionally out of this pass's scope.
- **GAP — webhook auto-registration still manual:** ongoing-sync connections poll on the cron sweep; real-time webhooks must still be configured by hand per provider (unchanged from pre-existing boardsync behaviour). Rally/GitLab/Bitbucket are poll-only (no `supportsWebhook`).

### 🧠 One brain, one tool catalog — web Brain + VS Code share the gateway MCP catalog — open items (added 2026-06-29; write-up in [DONE.md](./DONE.md))

- **REMAINING (enhancement, NOT duplication) — port the residual heavy/computed/auth tail into the catalog so the surfaces are byte-identical:** executions writes (submit/cancel/post_message), decks, repo_analysis, integrations writes, repos git writes, llm/dashboard/analytics reads, my_sessions/security/api_keys, project_files, channels, workspace, agent_host_config/skills, dispatch, board_data, marketplace_stats. Web-only today (in `platformActions`, NOT duplicated); best ported via **in-process Hono route replay** (`buildApp` exported + `app.request(path, init, env, ctx)` + forward the caller JWT or mint via `signJwt`; reuses route logic AND role-gate authz). Also: at ~130 flat tools, add **tiering** to the catalog path (advertise a core subset or a server-side dispatcher) since useMcpExtensions registers all-tools-always-on (the reason the old manifest used Tier-1/Tier-2).
- **GAP — `pmo.tree` / `pmo.rollup` not yet in the catalog:** the web manifest has them; the IDE chat must use `portfolios.list` + `initiatives.list` to discover scope ids for now. Add `pmo.tree` (simple multi-select) and `pmo.rollup` (reuse the rollup computation in `pmoRoutes.ts`, which must be extracted to a service first) when porting reads.
- **GAP — unify the agent LOOP + system prompt across surfaces too:** the tool catalog is now shared, but the agent loop (`frontend` brain hook vs `clients/vscode/src/agent.ts`) and the persona/system prompt are still separate implementations. Truly "one brain" = extract the loop + prompt into a shared workspace package both clients import (each injecting transport + client-local tools). Larger follow-on.

### 🎯 Brain can create real OKRs (objectives + key results), not fake "Epic" OKRs — open gaps (added 2026-06-29; write-up in [DONE.md](./DONE.md))

- **GAP — pre-existing orphan "OKR" epics are user data, not auto-migrated:** the five epics the Brain already created (tasks 134–138, keys `…-065`..`-069`) still sit on the board as fake OKRs. There is no backfill that converts an `taskType="epic"` titled like an OKR into a real `objectives` row + linked epic. Fixing it = a one-off helper (or a Brain prompt) that creates the objective, re-parents/links the epic via `objectives.add_link`, and renames the epic back to its delivery title. Until then the operator should delete/repurpose those epics and re-ask the Brain to create the OKRs (now wired).
- **GAP — modality Brain system prompts (`frontend/src/lib/modality.ts`) say nothing about strategy/OKRs:** steering currently rides entirely on tool descriptions (the DRY single source sent every request), which is sufficient for the observed failure, but the designer/video/llm/voice personas remain code/media-generation framed. Optional hardening = a shared "you also manage strategy: portfolios▸initiatives▸OKRs" line if OKR mis-selection recurs.

### 🌐 Brain can read external URLs/files/websites — open gap (added 2026-06-29; write-up in [DONE.md](./DONE.md))

- **GAP — no rate-limit / abuse cap on `POST /api/brain/fetch-url`:** the endpoint is tenant-authed but uncapped — a tenant could drive arbitrary outbound GETs through the gateway. SSRF literal-IP/internal-name blocking is in place, but DNS-rebinding (public host → private IP) is NOT caught (same residual as the MCP guard; Workers exposes no pre-fetch IP pinning), and there's no per-tenant request budget. Fixing it = add a rate-limit (reuse `rateLimitMiddleware`) and consider a consumption meter for outbound fetches.

### 📊 Project health + deadline parity across Card/List/Calendar/Details — open gap (added 2026-06-28; write-up in [DONE.md](./DONE.md))

- **GAP — legacy self-hosted IDE worker doesn't persist the project deadline:** `worker/src/routes/projects.ts` PUT (the `isWorkerForProjects()` path, a separate text-`id`/`owner_id` projects table with no tenant) ignores `dueDate` and its table has no `due_date` column, so on self-hosted-worker deployments the new deadline editor silently no-ops. Fixing it = add `due_date` to the worker's projects table + COALESCE it in the PUT and SELECT it in GET. The builderforce.ai (Hono `api`) path — what the report was about — is fully wired.

### 📈 Data-driven surfaces upgrade — AI / Delivery / Quality / catalogs — open gaps (added 2026-06-28; write-up in [DONE.md](./DONE.md))

- **GAP — Quality volume can't be broken down by source/provider:** `error_events` does not persist which adapter (native SDK / OTLP / Sentry / PostHog / LogRocket) produced an event — the normaliser drops it. So `QualityStatsPanel` breaks volume down by *collector*, not by *source*. Fixing it (add a `source` column to `error_events`, populate it in `ingestEngine`, and aggregate it in `/api/quality/stats`) unblocks a "data collected by source" donut on the collectors card — the one piece of the requested visual set not yet possible.
- **GAP — catalog pages still ship hardcoded English bodies:** Skills/Personas/Prompts pages were never localized; this pass localized only the NEW `CatalogInsightsBar` strip (and its `catalogInsights` namespace ×5). The surrounding page chrome (tab labels, buttons, table headers, empty/create-form strings) remains literal English. Fixing it = route those pages through `useTranslations` like the `/settings` reference.
- **GAP — catalog insights are snapshot-only (no adoption trend):** marketplace stats expose current `installs`/`likes`/`usageCount`/`starCount` but no time-series, so `CatalogInsightsBar` shows totals + breakdowns, not adoption-over-time. A per-entity `GET /api/{skills,personas,prompts}/analytics?window=30d` would unlock a `TrendChart` of adoption velocity.

### 📊 Evermind benchmarking capability — open gaps (added 2026-06-28; write-up in [DONE.md](./DONE.md)) — ✅ RESOLVED 2026-06-29

Resolved (1): the engine was republished (`@seanhogg/builderforce-memory-engine` is now `2026.6.35`, exporting the canonical `trainAndBenchmark`) and the frontend dep bumped to `^2026.6.35`, so [frontend/src/lib/evermind-benchmark.ts](frontend/src/lib/evermind-benchmark.ts) is now a thin delegate to the engine harness — the local metric-math duplicate is **deleted**. The stale `workflow.test.ts` `TRAIN_LLM` step list was corrected.
- **✅ DONE 2026-06-29 — benchmark UI now scores the user's ACTUAL trained artifact** (no engine change, no republish needed). The earlier "tokenizer-coupling blocker" diagnosis was over-pessimistic: the Studio publish flow ALREADY persists the model's tokenizer separately (`<ref>/tokenizer.json` next to `<ref>/model.evermind` in R2 — [evermindModelRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/evermindModelRoutes.ts) publish), and the server already loads both ([evermindRuntime.ts](api/src/application/llm/evermindRuntime.ts) `loadEvermindModel`). So scoring is done **server-side, reusing that loader** (DRY): new `benchmarkEvermind()` in `evermindRuntime.ts` → `benchmarkText(lm, tok, corpus)` (the model's own tokenizer, coherent ids) + a generation sample; exposed as `POST /api/studio/models/:slug/benchmark` (read-through cached on the immutable ref + corpus hash). Frontend: new `lib/studioModelsApi.ts` (`listEvermindModels` filters `evermind/*`; `benchmarkPublishedModel`) and a **"Score a trained model" mode** in [BenchmarkPanel.tsx](frontend/src/components/BenchmarkPanel.tsx) (published-model picker + held-out text → server scorecard; training-only metrics guarded; localized ×5, themed). api + frontend typecheck + eslint clean. The WebGPU `MambaModel` variant (scoring the raw training-job checkpoint vs the published `.evermind`) still needs `/vocab.json`+`/merges.txt` assets not deployed today — a separate, lower-value path; the published-artifact path above is the one users actually call.
- **ENV caveat (builderforce-memory, not Builderforce.ai code):** the pnpm-store `ts-jest` copy resolves an empty `dist/` (corrupted store) so a clean `pnpm install` re-breaks the jest suite (reinstall `ts-jest`); `workflow/steps.ts` line 397 (the `export` step's huggingface-without-tokenizer branch) remains uncovered.

### 📦 Evermind model export / Hugging Face publishing (added 2026-06-28) — ✅ IDE EXPORT WIRED 2026-06-30; remaining items external/credential-blocked

- **✅ DONE 2026-06-30 — the export subsystem is now wired into the Studio (was engine-only, no UI/endpoint).** A user can export a published `.evermind` model to a portable artifact from the LLM Studio: server `exportEvermindArtifact()` in [evermindRuntime.ts](api/src/application/llm/evermindRuntime.ts) reuses the R2 loader (DRY) and the engine `exportEvermind()` to emit safetensors / ONNX / GGUF or the full HF repo; exposed as `GET /api/studio/models/:slug/export?format=&fp16=` ([evermindModelRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/evermindModelRoutes.ts)) — single-file formats stream directly, the multi-file HF repo is zipped with `fflate`. Frontend: `lib/studioModelsApi.ts` (`exportPublishedModel` streams → Blob download) + a new **"Export your model" step** (`ModelExportPanel`, model+format+F16 pickers) in [LlmStudioPanel.tsx](frontend/src/components/LlmStudioPanel.tsx); localized ×5, themed. api+frontend typecheck + eslint clean; 3 new export tests green. **No credential needed** — the bytes are produced server-side; only the optional *push to a hub* below is token-gated.

The four items below still need an external credential or an upstream library change — none is closeable from this repo:
- **EXTERNAL (upstream transformers.js) — `pipeline()` auto-registration:** the ONNX runs via raw onnxruntime / transformers.js sessions, but `pipeline('text-generation', …)` won't auto-recognise `model_type: "evermind"` until an Evermind architecture class is upstreamed into transformers.js (custom shared-expert SSM has no existing class). Unblocks one-line `pipeline()` load.
- **EXTERNAL (upstream llama.cpp) — GGUF is container-only:** `general.architecture: "evermind"` is custom, so stock llama.cpp can't *run* the GGUF (it's still a valid, inspectable artifact for GGUF tooling). Unblocks llama.cpp execution once the arch graph is added there.
- **CREDENTIAL — live HF push:** `publishToHuggingFace` / `tools/export-hf.js --upload` need a write-scoped HF token (`HF_TOKEN` / `hf auth login`) and the optional `@huggingface/hub` dep (or the `hf` CLI). Code paths are tested with an injected fake client; a real push to `builderforce/Evermind` awaits an operator token.
- **ENV — committed tests can't run locally:** the workspace's `ts-jest` preset is broken (`Cannot find module '../dist/presets/all-presets'`) — pre-existing, affects ALL packages' jest. New `tests/export.test.ts` + `tests/publish.test.ts` were verified instead against the built `dist/` (71 + 12 checks green). Fix = repair the ts-jest install in the pnpm store.
- **CLOSED (verified 2026-06-29) — `packages/memory-engine/tools/export-hf.js`:** the file that surfaced during the original task is confirmed present, correct + working (`--demo` produces the full repo on disk; its ONNX loads in onnxruntime) and is kept as the terminal-side publish runner. Provenance noted; no action outstanding.

### 🧠 Evermind train→serve loop — serving endpoint missing (dogfood pass, added 2026-06-28) — ✅ RESOLVED 2026-06-29

Closed: the **serve + generate** half is wired (shared `evermindRuntime.ts` — `EvermindModelPackage.fromBlob(...).loadLM().generateText(...)` — backs both the `evermind/<ref>` gateway vendor and the Studio publish/test routes [evermindModelRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/evermindModelRoutes.ts), so a tenant's own trained Evermind is callable over the OpenAI-compatible API); foundation diagnostics shipped (`dataset-quality`/`convergence`/`generate-check`/`roundtrip` steps + the `TRAIN_RESUME_LLM` template, `workflow.test.ts` green). The "MISSING formal migrations" note was **stale** — `ide_datasets`/`ide_training_jobs`/`ide_training_logs` (+ `ide_agents` + indexes) are created by a formal migration, [api/migrations/0022_ide_tables.sql](api/migrations/0022_ide_tables.sql); the routes only read/write them (no inline DDL, columns match). Remaining is a non-defect caveat: a toy `dModel≈16–24` reference EvermindLM validates the *pipeline* but isn't sized for high-quality long-form output on its own — route long-form to a larger Evermind or an external frontier model via the gateway; currency/footprint/ownership are Evermind's edge, "not raw scale" (`project.evermind` / [[ssm-hippocampus-loop]]). Write-up in [DONE.md](./DONE.md).

### 🔌 Gateway/SDK schema-rejection handling (hired.video feedback, added 2026-06-28)
Still open / deferred:
- **Funded-premium-primary for FREE quality-critical traffic is intentionally NOT enabled.** Feature 2 is plan-respecting (free tenants get the best FREE models + the funded backstop, not premium-primary), because the `useCase` tag is caller-supplied — funding premium on the primary attempt for any free request tagged `resume_…` is an uncapped cost/abuse vector. Enabling it would need overflow-metering the primary premium attempt (reuse `paidOverflow` + `paid_overflow_daily_cap`) so it's capped per tenant. Unblocks: premium-primary quality for free tenants without unbounded spend. (added 2026-06-28)
- **[DONE 2026-06-28] Evermind is now a generation backend in the gateway — no longer memory-only.** An `evermind` `VendorModule` ([api/src/application/llm/vendors/evermind.ts](api/src/application/llm/vendors/evermind.ts)) loads a tenant's published `.evermind` artifact from R2 and runs the builderforce-memory `EvermindLM` on-CPU inside the Worker; the shared `evermindRuntime.ts` backs both the vendor and the Studio publish/test routes ([evermindModelRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/evermindModelRoutes.ts), mounted in `index.ts`). A request pinned to `evermind/<ref>` is served by Evermind itself — it is the cortex, not Claude/GPT. It is reached only via an explicit pin (`autoRoute:false`), so it never silently joins the FREE/PRO failover pools; external frontier models remain a routable choice, not a hard dependency. Remaining open: an eval gate that lets Evermind become an *automatic* quality default for a use case (today it must be pinned) — per [[evermind]] its edge is currency/footprint/ownership, "not raw scale," so auto-routing long-form writing to it still needs a competitiveness check. (added 2026-06-28)
- **Per-vendor strict-schema capability not advertised in the model catalog / `/v1/models`.** `deriveResponseFormat`'s vendor ceilings are SDK-side heuristics; the authoritative constrained-decoding limits aren't in `VendorModelEntry`/`capabilitiesForModel` yet, so SDKs can't pre-filter on real data (feedback item 4 "expose the limit / strict-schema-capable flag"). Fixing it: add a `strictSchema?: boolean | { maxComplexity?: number }` to `VendorModelEntry`, populate per vendor catalog, surface via `capabilitiesForModel` → `ModelInfo`. Unblocks: SDK pre-filtering keyed off the live catalog instead of a baked table. (added 2026-06-28)

- **VS Code extension cannot auto-publish — missing Marketplace/Open VSX tokens.** `.github/workflows/publish-vscode.yml` (triggered by a `vscode-v*` tag) requires repo secrets `VSCE_PAT` (VS Code Marketplace) and `OVSX_PAT` (Open VSX); neither is configured, so every tagged release fails at the publish step. Fixing it: add both secrets (Azure DevOps PAT with Marketplace→Manage for `VSCE_PAT`; open-vsx.org token for `OVSX_PAT`), then push a `vscode-v<version>` tag. Unblocks: shipping `clients/vscode` updates (the 2026.6.31 release is staged and waiting on this). Fixed in 2026.6.31: (a) the manifest's `enabledApiProposals: [chatSessionsProvider]` was hard-blocking Marketplace publish (proposed APIs can't ship to stable VS Code) — removed; (b) the old extension `builderforce.builderforce-vscode` was *removed* from the Marketplace and its name is permanently reserved (Marketplace policy — cannot be republished even by the same publisher), so the extension was renamed to **`builderforce.builderforce-ai`** (publisher + display name unchanged). NOTE: the new id is likewise permanently reserved once published; do not delete/remove it from the Marketplace — unpublish instead if ever needed. (added 2026-06-28)
- **Workforce agent cards lack the per-member stats strip** — `MemberStatsStrip` + `WorkforceMetricsProvider` (`components/workforce/`) now surface Performance + Contributors signals on human `MemberCard`s (keyed reliably on user id). The reusable strip is NOT yet wired into `AgentCard` (cloud/purchased) or the inline remote-host card. Host agents map cleanly (`scorecardFor('host_agent', String(host.id))`); cloud agents are blocked because the scorecard ref is the task's `assignedAgentRef`, whose equivalence to `PublishedAgent.id` is unverified. Fixing it: confirm the cloud-agent ref↔published-id mapping (or add the ref to `PublishedAgent`), then drop `<MemberStatsStrip>` into both card bodies. Unblocks: parity of the "Individual" view stats across people AND agents. (added 2026-06-28)

### 📖 Knowledge canvas-in-Brain + marketplace selling (added 2026-06-28, pass 2)
Still open / deferred:
- **No Stripe charge on install.** `price_cents` is stored + shown but install grants a free copy (same as the existing skills marketplace for free items). Paid checkout (Stripe payment intent → gated install) is unbuilt. Unblocks: actually charging for knowledge.
- **Public (logged-out) browse of knowledge listings.** `GET /api/knowledge/listings` is under tenant auth, so `KnowledgeMarketSection` only renders for signed-in users. A public read endpoint (like the personas marketplace) would surface listings to everyone. Unblocks: discovery before sign-in.
- **Canvas realtime still doc-granular; no block-CRDT multi-cursor; no upload/freehand-drawing blocks.** (video/file are URL-based; whole-model serialise over the existing Yjs text channel.)
- **`/content-manager` → Knowledge migration (not a redirect).** Content Manager is still live and the `/marketplace` content cards read its localStorage `sharedToMarketplace` blocks, so a naive redirect would break that. Replacing "content" means migrating content blocks → `knowledge_documents` and porting those marketplace cards onto `marketplace_knowledge`. Logged, not done.

### 📈 "Insights everywhere" coverage audit (added 2026-06-28)

Standing requirement (operator, 2026-06-28; saved as the `insights-everywhere-standard` memory): charts/graphs/actionable insights are the DEFAULT on almost every authenticated surface — anything used/viewed/last-modified is measurable and should be surfaced with a nudge to improve. Canonical primitives already exist (`components/charts/*`: BarChart, TrendChart, Sparkline, DonutChart, GaugeChart, BandedMetricBar) but are confined to the `insights/*` lenses, `pmShared`, `ProjectCard`, `knowledge`, `dashboards` and the usage cards. Full-frontend audit found the operational/catalog/ops surfaces are mostly metric-bare. Open gaps (each: surface — what's missing — signal that already exists → primitive that fits):

**Operational / delivery surfaces**
- **Tasks board** (`components/.../TaskMgmtContent.tsx`) — no WIP/velocity trend, no cycle-time, no per-task run-recency. Has `createdAt/updatedAt/dueDate`, `agentRunsByTask`, `latestExecByTask`. → header Sparkline (WIP/velocity), per-card "last run Xh ago" recency badge, cycle-time gauge per lane. Unblocks: at-a-glance board health.
- **Workflows list** (`WorkflowsContent.tsx`) — `runCount/lastRunStatus/updatedAt` shown as text only; no run-frequency sparkline, no success-rate trend on detail. → Sparkline (runs/4wk) per card, TrendChart (success rate) on run-detail, "last run Xh ago" badge. Unblocks: spotting failing/stale workflows.
- **Brainstorm / Brain chat list** (`BrainPanel.tsx`) — fully metric-bare; chats have `createdAt`, project scope, but no message-count / recency / outcome surfaced. → recency badge + message-count Sparkline per chat, "chats by project" DonutChart. Unblocks: finding active vs dead threads.
- **Ceremonies** (`CeremoniesContent.tsx` / `CeremonyStage`) — board-scoped round-table with no rollup (items completed per standup, plan-adherence trend). → metric cards + TrendChart (adherence over sprints). Unblocks: ceremony effectiveness signal.

**Workforce surfaces**
- **Workforce — Agents** (`WorkforceAgents.tsx`) — cards show only ONLINE/OFFLINE pill; no uptime/run-freq/cost trend, `updatedAt` unused. → per-card Sparkline (uptime % / runs-per-day), "last active Xh ago" badge. Unblocks: agent utilization at a glance.
- **Workforce — Teams** — no composition viz, no size/recency. Has `createdAt/updatedAt`, member + project counts. → BandedMetricBar/DonutChart (humans vs agents), size metric, "updated Xd ago". Unblocks: team-shape clarity.
- **Workforce — Performance** (`WorkforceMetricsContent.tsx`) — DORA tiles + scorecard table are text-only; no per-member trend, no DORA target-vs-actual. → per-row Sparkline (effectiveness/cycle-time trend), BandedMetricBar on DORA tiles. Unblocks: trend direction, not just point-in-time.
- **Workforce — LLM Usage** (`LlmUsageContent` + `ModelRoutingAnalytics`) — model ranking is a table; `bySource` fetched but unrendered. → BarChart (models by outcome score), TrendChart (spend), Sparkline (uptime). Unblocks: visual model/cost comparison.

**Catalog / entity surfaces** (cross-cutting: all show engagement metrics as TEXT badges, none as charts)
- **Skills** (`app/skills/page.tsx`) — `stats.likes/installs` as text. → Sparkline (install trend) + BandedMetricBar (install rank) on card; "Most installed" nudge.
- **Personas** (`app/personas/page.tsx`) — `stats.likes/installs` as text. → DonutChart (by source) on hub, install-rank bar + recency on cards.
- **Prompts** (`PromptsPageClient.tsx`) — `usageCount/starCount` as text. → Sparkline (7d usage) + BandedMetricBar (usage rank); "Trending" nudge.
- **Marketplace** (`MarketplacePageClient.tsx`) — `likes/installs/hire_count/eval_score` as text. → GaugeChart (agent eval) on cards, DonutChart (catalog by type), BarChart (top by installs).
- **Models** (`ModelsPageClient.tsx`) — rich specs, zero visual comparison. → BarChart (input/output cost), GaugeChart (context window), DonutChart (by tier).
- **Tools** (`ToolsHubClient.tsx`) — rollup uses `ToolResultView`, but individual tool cards have no run-count/recency. → StatCard (run count / "last run Xd ago"), GaugeChart (score) on card.
- **Integrations** (`app/integrations/page.tsx`) — static SEO grid, NO adoption data fetched. → needs backend adoption/activation signal first, then StatCard ("X teams using") + Sparkline. (Blocked on data, not just UI.)

**Ops / observability / admin surfaces**
- **Alerts** (`AlertsClient.tsx`) — rules+events table only; no fire-frequency trend or rule-health breakdown. Events are fetched with timestamps. → TrendChart (fires/day per rule), DonutChart (active/silenced/no-signal). Unblocks: noisy vs dead rules.
- **Logs** (`app/logs/page.tsx`) — audit table only (200-row cap). Has `createdAt` + `eventType`. → TrendChart (event volume by type), DonutChart (type distribution). Unblocks: spotting spikes.
- **Quality** (`QualityDashboard.tsx`) — summary counters + table; no error-volume/resolution-velocity trend. `eventCount` per group exists (needs date-windowed backend agg). → TrendChart (events by status over time), BarChart (top errors). Unblocks: is quality improving?
- **Admin — Health/Usage** (`app/admin/page.tsx`) — single-snapshot health cards + static model badges; no growth/error/LLM-usage trends. `byVendor`/`byModelSorted` computed but uncharted (growth trends need historical rollup). → TrendChart (users/tenants/executions/errors over time), BarChart (top models), GaugeChart (pool SLA). Unblocks: platform trajectory.
- **IDE Dashboard** (`app/ide/dashboard/page.tsx`) — project launcher grid; no modality distribution or staleness. `modality` + `containerProjectId` present. → DonutChart (projects by modality), "last opened" recency badge. Unblocks: IDE-project portfolio view.
- **Content Manager** (`app/content-manager/page.tsx`) — likes/downloads inline text only (also flagged elsewhere as nav-orphaned → may fold into Knowledge). → if kept: TrendChart (engagement) + BarChart (top blocks); else resolve via the `/content-manager` redirect decision above.
- **Dashboard home** (`app/dashboard/page.tsx`) — 4 stat link-cards (no trends) beside the existing `AiUsageCard`. Has tasks/projects/agentHosts/approvals already fetched. → Sparkline (7d agents online), TrendChart (task completion velocity), approval-age recency. Unblocks: home as a live pulse.

**Already covered (no gap — for reference):** Contributors (activity heatmap), Timeline/Logs-tab (ExecutionTimelineChart), Knowledge home (coverage gauge + by-type bar; minor: add freshness trend), Projects list (`ProjectCard` health gauge + %-done ring, shipped 2026-06-28), Finance/AI/Delivery insight hubs.

**Cross-cutting:** the recurring pattern is "metric fetched and shown as a text badge, never as a chart." A shared **`MetricBadge`/`InsightStat`** primitive (value + sparkline + recency + optional nudge, self-gating) would DRY most catalog/card cases instead of re-deriving per surface — candidate companion to `StatCard`. Several trend gaps (Quality, Admin growth, Alerts) need date-windowed backend aggregation + a cached read-through endpoint, not just UI.
### 📌 Unified pinnable-widget dashboard (shipped 2026-06-28)
Open / deferred (next passes):
- **The remaining "insights everywhere" surfaces are now a mechanical port.** Every text-badge surface in the audit above (Tasks, Workflows, Brainstorm, Ceremonies, Workforce Agents/Teams/Performance, Skills/Personas/Prompts/Marketplace/Models/Tools, Alerts, Logs, Quality, Admin, IDE dashboard) becomes a widget module like `deliveryWidgets.tsx`: write the `*_WIDGETS` array against the surface's existing data client, add the import+spread to `allWidgets.ts`, add `widgets.title.*`/`group.*` keys. No new infra — just per-surface decomposition. **Integrations stays blocked on a backend adoption signal** (no data fetched).
- **Brain bridge for widgets.** No `show_widget` / `pin_widget` Brain tool yet (the insight hubs have `show_*_insight`). Add a bridge so the Brain can surface/pin a registry widget. Unblocks: conversational dashboard building.
- **Pin reorder UI.** The API (`PUT /dashboard-pins/order`) + `usePins.reorder` exist but the home grid has no drag-to-reorder affordance yet.
- **Finance widgets ignore the dashboard `days` window** — the finance collector is month-keyed (`finance:<YYYY-MM>`), so finance cards pin fine but don't react to the shared 7/30/90 selector. Unblocks: consistent windowing once a day-windowed finance series exists.
- **More `series` metrics.** Only 3 metrics expose a series so far; the existing scalar metrics (DORA, finance, engineering) render scalar-only until a `series` is added (one-liner each via the shared helpers).

### 📖 Knowledge unification + reusable canvas (added 2026-06-28)
Open / deferred (next passes):
- **Sell knowledge items in the Marketplace.** Requested but NOT built: the marketplace today is skills-only (`marketplaceRoutes.ts` `/skills`, no generic `marketplace_listings` table). Listing a knowledge document (SOP/process/doc/canvas) for sale needs a new listing type + migration (price, visibility, buyer-tenant copy-on-purchase) + a "List in Marketplace" action on the published doc + checkout. Deliberately not half-wired (no dead button). Unblocks: monetising authored knowledge.
- **Canvas realtime is doc-level, not multi-cursor.** Canvas edits ride the existing `content` Yjs text channel (whole-model serialise on change), so two editors on the same board last-writer-win at the doc granularity rather than per-block CRDT with live cursors. A block-granular CRDT + presence layer is the richer follow-on. Unblocks: true simultaneous Miro-style co-editing.
- **Brain/Brainstorm don't yet generate a canvas.** `CanvasSlideOver` is built to be mounted by Brain/Brainstorm, but no `show_canvas` Brain tool / generator wiring exists yet (mirror the `show_*_insight` BrainBridge pattern). Plus a "Save canvas to Knowledge" action from the slide-out. Unblocks: AI-generated canvases shown in a side panel.

Decide: redirect `/content-manager` → `/knowledge`, or migrate any remaining "content" records into knowledge docs. Unblocks: removing dead surface.

- **Scenario Planner.** New pure `application/insights/deliveryScenario.ts` (`buildScenario`): linear what-if over the live delivery baseline — Developers × Attention% × Scope-delta → projected date, on-track/at-risk/late verdict vs target, days-vs-target, and effort in person-weeks. Route `GET /api/insights/delivery/scenario` (cached, dev-gated, single source of truth). Frontend `ScenarioPlanner` panel: debounced sliders, keyed per deliverable.
- **Lifecycle Explorer.** New `application/insights/lifecycleInsights.ts` **reusing** `bottleneckInsights.buildStageDurations` (DRY) — maps board statuses → canonical SDLC phases (Refinement → Work → Review → Deploy), avg/median dwell per phase + monthly end-to-end lifecycle trend. Route `GET /api/insights/delivery/lifecycle` (cached). Frontend `LifecycleExplorer`: phase bars + `TrendChart`.
- 24 unit tests (scenario 8, lifecycle 7, delivery +3 wired); api + frontend `tsc` clean; ~45 new `insights.deliv.{scenario,lifecycle,legend*}.*` keys localized across all 5 catalogs.

Follow-ups from the first pass — both CLOSED 2026-06-28 (same-day):
- 🔓 **Remaining (smaller) gap:** the lifecycle/value-stream views are at the *initiative* grain; a single-value-item swimlane (one ticket's flow requirement → … → adoption with timestamps) is still not drawn. The data seam (`taskStatusTransitions` + the `mapStatusToPhase` mapper in `lifecycleInsights.ts`) exists; it would just need a per-task timeline component.

### 📈 Capitalization Cost-Report Visuals (added 2026-06-28)
Open / deferred:
- **No downloadable/auditable report export.** Jellyfish ships a spreadsheet workbook (cover sheet, glossary, work-capitalization, monthly-summary, data-by-issue-by-contributor tabs). This pass is on-screen visuals only; a CSV/XLSX export of the capitalization report (the per-epic status + monthly FTE-month/cost facts) is unbuilt. Unblocks: the audit deliverable finance teams hand to auditors.
- **History cost is attributed to each task's "as-of" month, not the real spend month.** `summarizeAllocationHistory` buckets a task's whole-range LLM spend into the month it last moved (completedAt ?? updatedAt) — a faithful single-fetch approximation. A true spend-by-calendar-month series would bucket `llm_usage_log` rows by `created_at`. Unblocks: exact monthly cost trend (matters once spend is spread across months within one task).
- **Capitalized FTE-months inherit the cycle-time effort ESTIMATE.** FTE-months derive from `taskEffortHours` (cycle-time, capped) because there is still no first-class effort/time-tracking field on tasks (existing register gap); figures sharpen as `time_entries` coverage grows. Unblocks: timesheet-grade FTE-month accuracy.

### 🪧 Board Deck Generator (added 2026-06-27)
Open / deferred:
- **Deploy drift guard doesn't catch seed-data FK failures (process gap, surfaced by the 0243 outage above).** `release.yml`'s pre-deploy guard runs `check:schema` + `check:migrations`, but those only validate table/column existence and filename sequence — a seed `INSERT` that is guaranteed to violate an FK at runtime (like 0243's `tenant_id=0`) passes every check and then silently aborts `db:migrate`, blocking ALL deploys with no early signal. Fixing this — e.g. a CI step that applies every pending migration against an ephemeral throwaway Postgres before deploy, or a lint that flags seed INSERTs of sentinel FK values — would turn "all deploys silently broken for days" into a red CI check on the offending PR. Unblocks: deploy reliability / faster detection of the whole migration-runtime-failure class.
- **Pre-existing migration collision (NOT this work):** `0245_quality_group_users.sql` vs `0245_time_entries.sql` both claim 0245 — `npm run check:migrations` fails until the newer is renumbered. Two different tracks; renumber per the isolation-track bands. Surfaced while running the test gate; my migrations (0236-0243) are collision-free.
- **In-place fill runs in the Worker (fflate), not the Node container** (perf hedge, not a functional gap). If a large image-heavy custom template ever hits the Worker CPU ceiling, add a `POST /fill-deck` branch to `container/server.mjs` and dispatch from `inPlaceFiller`.
- **V2 — native chart re-data in uploaded templates.** In-place fill substitutes text + table-cell tokens only; re-dataing a NATIVE PowerPoint chart (editing nested `ppt/embeddings/*.xlsx` + `ppt/charts/chartN.xml`) is deferred. Built-in generative decks use pptxgenjs `addChart` (full data); table-driven KPI blocks fill in v1.
- **Verify pptxgenjs bundles under wrangler (deploy-time).** Renders fine in Node/vitest (smoke test) and `nodejs_compat` is on; the local `wrangler --dry-run` couldn't run here (a broken `unenv` link in this mixed npm/pnpm sandbox, unrelated to the code). Confirm on the next real `pnpm install && wrangler deploy`.
- **Live status-page / HRIS / payroll connectors (future, not blocking).** Uptime now derives from incidents and all manual datasets have CSV import; a dedicated Statuspage/BetterStack uptime connector or an HRIS/ATS feed remain nice-to-haves for full automation.

### 🧵 Isolation Tracks — parallel agent assignment

Dispatch **one agent per track**. Tracks are **file-disjoint by construction**, so agents run in parallel without stepping on each other. An agent assigned a track edits **only** files under that track's _Owns_ paths, works **only** the open gaps whose primary file lives there, and draws migration numbers **only** from its reserved band. Anything outside its paths belongs to another track — use the shared-hub rules below, never edit cross-track.

| Track | Owns (primary paths) | Gap focus | Mig band |
|---|---|---|---|
| **T1 · Marketing & SEO Web** | `frontend/src/app/{page.tsx,compare,integrations,marketplace/[slug],product,agents,blog,pricing,projects/[id],sitemap.ts}` · `frontend/src/lib/{seo,content,structured-data,og,marketplaceSeo,blogData,routeMarketing}.*` · `frontend/src/components/{PublicShell,MarketingHeader,AppFooter,PageContainer,RouteMarketing,QuickStart,blog/*}` · `frontend/public/{robots.txt,install.*}` · routes `pendingPromptRoutes.ts` | 🚀 Growth | — |
| **T2 · App UI & Brain** | all other `frontend/src/{app,components}/**` · `frontend/src/lib/brain/**` · `brain-embedded/**` · route `dashboardRoutes.ts` | 🛠️ Core (UI/UX) | 0180–0189 |
| **T3 · Gateway & LLM** | `api/src/application/llm/**` · `api/src/infrastructure/cache/**` · route `llmRoutes.ts` | 💰 Direct + LLM Core/Internal | 0130–0139 |
| **T4 · Cloud Runtime & PR loop** | `api/src/application/{runtime,repos}/**` · `api/src/infrastructure/relay/**` · routes `runtimeRoutes.ts`,`repoRoutes.ts`,`repoAnalysisRoutes.ts`,`taskRoutes.ts`,`agentRuntimeRoutes.ts` | 🛠️ Core (cloud agents) | 0140–0149 |
| **T5 · On-Prem Agent Runtime** | `agent-runtime/**` · `packages/**` | 🧹 Internal (engine/pi/tui) | — |
| **T6 · Studio & Voice** | `studio/**` · `studio-embedded/**` · `voice/**` · routes `studioVoiceCloneRoutes.ts`,`studioWeightRoutes.ts` · frontend `components/{LlmStudioPanel,VoiceClonePanel}`,`app/ide/voice` | 🛠️ Core (video/voice) | 0150–0159 |
| **T7 · Tenant · Embed · Governance** | `builderforce-embedded/**` · `frontend/src/{app,lib}/embed/**` · `api/src/application/seams/**` · `api/src/infrastructure/auth/segment*` · routes `tenant*`,`embedRoutes.ts`,`governanceRoutes.ts`,`segment*`,`seamRoutes.ts`,`webhookRoutes.ts`,`biRoutes.ts`,`mcpExtensionRoutes.ts`,`reportRoutes.ts` | 🛠️ Core + 🧹 Internal (multi-tenant) | 0160–0169 |
| **T8 · Workflows · Boards** | `api/src/application/{workflow,boardsync,swimlane}/**` · routes `workflow*`,`board*`,`integrationRoutes.ts`,`githubWebhookRoutes.ts` · frontend `components/workflow-builder/**`,`app/workflows/**` | 🛠️ Core (orchestration) | 0170–0179 |
| **T9 · Platform · DB · CI** _(steward)_ | `api/migrations/**` · `api/scripts/**` · `.github/workflows/**` · `frontend/eslint.config.js` · root tsconfig/lint · schema-drift allowlist | 🧹 Internal (migrations/drift/tests/lint) | 0190+ |
| **T10 · Docs & QA** | `docs-site/**` · `qa-e2e/**` · `api/src/application/qa/**` · route `qaRoutes.ts` · frontend `components/QaContent.tsx` | QA + docs | — |

**Shared hubs — append-only, never edit another track's block:**
- `api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts` — append new tables at the end; **T9 stewards** ordering + drift.
- `api/src/index.ts` — append route mounts only.
- `frontend/src/lib/builderforceApi.ts` — append API-client blocks only.
- `frontend/src/lib/content.ts` — **T1 owns**; other tracks request copy changes via T1.
- This **Consolidated Gap Register** — append entries; run the "organize + calculate gaps" pass only when no other agent is mid-edit (it rewrites section counts).

**Migration numbering is the one true serialization point** (duplicate numbers already bit us — see the `0109`/`0111` collision gap). Draw **only** from your band; **T9** issues any number outside a band. Next free single slot: **0227** (0226 = allocation_and_goals).

**Run each track in its own git worktree + branch** (`git worktree add ../bf-T2 -b track/T2`). File-disjoint paths only prevent *merge* conflicts — pointing two agents at the **same working copy** still lets their edits interleave mid-run (and a shared `tsc`/`pnpm` build clobbers). One worktree per track = one branch per track = truly parallel; merge the branches back when each track lands. Track boundaries are **convention, not enforced** — an agent that ignores its _Owns_ scope can still stray (the durable fix is a CI/pre-commit guard that rejects a branch touching files outside its declared track — logged in the register).

**Dispatch example:** _"Agent A → T1 (Growth) · Agent B → T3 (Gateway/Direct) · Agent C → T9 (Internal/DB),"_ each in its own worktree/branch. Three agents, zero file overlap.

### 🔓 Newly logged (open)

- 🔄 **COMPILE PRIMITIVE — SPINE COMPLETE (C2 + C4 + C5 shipped 2026-06-28).** The `compile()` and `deploy()` registries, all six modality adapters, `PolicyGate`, and the plain-language front door are live; this closes the "vision incomplete" framing the blog post used to carry. Built: `api/src/application/compile/` (`compileFromProse` — the previously-missing plain-language door, injected `LlmComplete` extractor; `compileFromDataset`; `compileFromGraph` reusing `compileDefinition`; `compileFromPersona`; `compileFromDiagnostic` — findings → chained `CompiledStep[]`; `compileFromPolicy`; `mergeSpecs` stacks modalities into ONE spec; `compile(need|need[])` dispatcher + `MODALITIES`). `api/src/application/deploy/` (`deploy(spec, surface)` → surface→transport map + engine resolution via shared `DEFAULT_ENGINE_ID` + `lowerAgentSpec`→`runInput` + `surfaces` allow-list enforcement + `DeployPlan`; `DEPLOY_SURFACES`). `packages/agent-tools/src/spec.ts` gained `PolicyGate`/`AgentSpecPolicy` (rendered into the prompt by `lowerAgentSpec` on every surface) + pure `evaluatePolicyGate` (block > require-approval > allow) for hard tool-seam enforcement. Front door: `POST /api/compile`, `POST /api/compile/run` ([compileRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/compileRoutes.ts), mounted `/api/compile`), the localized `/compile` page ([frontend/src/app/compile/page.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/app/compile/page.tsx), `compile` namespace × 5 catalogs), `compileApi` client. **Verified:** 18 new tests green (`compile.test.ts` + `deploy.test.ts`), api + agent-tools + frontend tsc clean for touched files. Blog post `define-a-need-the-agentic-system-solves-it` rewritten to present tense + 3 new SVG diagrams. **Remaining = enforcement DEPTH, not the spine (logged below).**
  - 🧰 **`cloud-container` executor still demotes to durable — INFRA, not code.** `chooseCloudExecutor` correctly falls back when `env.AGENT_CONTAINER` is unbound or its `/health` probe fails. Closing it needs a bound Cloudflare Container DO + a deployed image (deploy-time/infra), not a code change. (primary: `cloudDispatch.ts`, wrangler config)
  - 🧹 **Authoring policy gates onto a *published* agent has no UI/persistence yet.** Gate enforcement + propagation are fully live (gates flow whenever a run payload carries `policyGates` — e.g. via `deployAndDispatch`), but a board/runtime run of a stored agent has no gates because `ide_agents` has no `policy_gates` column and no publish-time editor writes them. Closing it = a migration + a gate editor on the publish/manage surface. (primary: `AgentPublishPanel.tsx`, `ide_agents`)

- 🔄 **(superseded) COMPILE PRIMITIVE — Phase C1 shipped; C2–C5 + data providers open (2026-06-27).** Built the spine keystone of the [compile primitive](./PRD-agent-compile-primitive.md): canonical `AgentSpec` IR + the single `lowerAgentSpec()` lowering in [packages/agent-tools/src/spec.ts](Builderforce.ai/packages/agent-tools/src/spec.ts) (pure, zero-dep, Worker/Node/VS-Code-safe), now the actual system-prompt assembler in [agentPrompt.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/agent/agentPrompt.ts) (`buildAgentSystemPrompt` + new `buildAgentInference` lower through it — live on all 3 inference paths: chat, validate, gateway), with `agent-runtime`'s `PsychometricExecParams` aliased to the canonical `AgentExecParams` (one exec-param type across the trait/limbic compilers + the spec). **Verified:** api 38 tests (16 new `agentPrompt.test.ts` + 24 llmRoutes) green + tsc clean for touched files; agent-runtime psychometrics 14 green. The lowering renders persona directives + recalled-memory context + persistent-state signal when present. **Remaining open (the data providers + remaining adoption):**
  - 💰 **No data provider yet feeds persona exec-params / recalled-context on the API gateway path.** `lowerAgentSpec` consumes `persona.directives`, `persona.execParams`, and `memory.recalledContext`, but `resolveWorkforceModel` (gateway) populates none of them — `ide_agents` has no psychometric-profile column and the Worker has no doc-ingestion/hybrid-recall backend. Fixing = store a profile on `ide_agents` (migration) + the `POST /api/ide/agents/:id/ingest` chunk→embed→store endpoint + Worker-safe recall (PRD Phase C3); unblocks "trained on your data" + persona-on-gateway. (primary: [agentPrompt.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/agent/agentPrompt.ts) `resolveWorkforceModel`, [ideRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/ideRoutes.ts), `builderforce-memory/packages/memory/src/retrieval/`)
  - 🛠️ **`compile()` / `deploy()` registries + remaining surface adoption not built (PRD C2/C4).** The IR exists and one consumer (api workforce inference) lowers through it; still to do: the `compile()` modality registry (prose/dataset/process-chart/persona/diagnostic adapters), the `deploy()` surface registry, and adopting `lowerAgentSpec` on the surfaces whose artifact actually matches the workforce-inference shape — the **VS Code `runAgent()`** built-in agent and the **cloud workforce inference**. NOTE (corrected 2026-06-27): the on-prem `buildPersonaSystemBlock`/`buildAssignedCapabilityAppend` block is a *distinct* artifact (`--- Agent Persona ---`: role/voice/perspective/decision-style/output-format/constraints + assigned skills/content + live limbic state), **not** the identity+skills+memory inference prompt — it already shares what matters (`buildPsychometricBlock`, the same psychometric compiler). It should NOT be force-fit through `lowerAgentSpec`; only the genuinely-shared workforce-inference shape unifies. (primary: new `api/src/application/{compile,deploy}/`, [clients/vscode/src/agent.ts](Builderforce.ai/clients/vscode/src/agent.ts))
  - 🔄 **PILLAR-2 / PRD-C3 (train-on-data) SHIPPED (2026-06-27).** Proprietary-doc ingestion + grounded recall is live end-to-end. Built: migration **0249** `agent_knowledge_chunks` (raw-SQL, FK→`ide_agents`, ON DELETE CASCADE; renumbered from 0247→0249 after a live collision with concurrent `time_entries`/`deliverable_updates`); [agentKnowledge.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/agent/agentKnowledge.ts) (`ingestAgentKnowledge` chunk→replace→single UNNEST bulk-insert→cache-invalidate; `recallAgentKnowledge` read-through-cached load + BM25 top-K → `recalledContext`; pure `selectRecallContext`/`chunkDocuments` reusing `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory/retrieval` `chunkText`/`bm25Search` — added as an `api` dep, resolves via the existing pnpm store, no duplication); `POST /api/ide/agents/:id/ingest` + recall wired into the `/agents/:id/chat` path (latest user message → recalled context → shared `lowerAgentSpec`); frontend `ingestAgentKnowledge` client + a localized ingest panel on `AgentPublishPanel` (7 keys × 5 catalogs). **Verified:** api 43 tests (7 new `agentKnowledge.test.ts`) green + tsc clean for touched files; migration-sequence + schema-drift checks pass; frontend tsc clean + catalog key-parity OK. **Residuals (logged, not blocking):**
    - 🛠️ **Recall is on the dedicated `/agents/:id/chat` path only — NOT the OpenAI-standard gateway** (`/v1/chat/completions` → `resolveWorkforceModel`). The gateway resolves the model before the recall query is threaded through; wiring recall there means passing the request's latest user message into `resolveWorkforceModel` (or a post-resolve recall step). Fixing unblocks grounded recall for stock OpenAI-SDK callers. (primary: [llmRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts), [agentPrompt.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/agent/agentPrompt.ts) `resolveWorkforceModel`)

A "Manage knowledge" control on the workforce/agent management surface would close it. (primary: [AgentPublishPanel.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/AgentPublishPanel.tsx), workforce management UI)
    - 🧹 **Dense/hybrid recall not used in the Worker — BM25-only** (the `HybridRetriever` dense path needs an embedding model not available in the Worker). Acceptable for keyword recall; a Worker-side embedding (or precomputed chunk embeddings) would enable hybrid. (primary: [agentKnowledge.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/agent/agentKnowledge.ts))

- 🚀 **VISION GAP AUDIT — "define-a-need → executing-agent" (2026-06-27).** Audited the platform against the North-Star vision (above) across its four operator pillars. Found four independent "need → agent" front doors with **no shared `AgentSpec` IR and no shared deploy step** — the [compile primitive](./PRD-agent-compile-primitive.md) (`compile(need)→AgentSpec→deploy(surface)`) is the proposed spine. Each gap below is a missing **edge** between things that already exist, not a greenfield build. **Already strong** (no action): visual workflow builder → compile → claim → relay dispatch is fully end-to-end (`workflowGraph.ts`, `instantiateRun.ts`, `workflowRoutes.ts`, `SwimlaneCoordinator.ts`); in-browser WebGPU training + publish + workforce model refs work (`webgpu-trainer.ts`, `AgentPublishPanel.tsx`, `ideRoutes.ts`, `resolveWorkforceModel`); the shared `AgentEngine` interface + DI registry already unifies cloud-durable + on-prem-relay (`packages/agent-tools/src/engine.ts`, `resolveEngineById`). **Open gaps below (one per fixing-unblocks):**
  - 🛠️ **PILLAR 1 — diagnostics score but never EMIT an improved process; no SOP/process ingestion or analyzer exists.** `/api/tools` + `agentic-maturity` (`ToolService.ts`, `toolDefinitions.ts`) compute a maturity score with **static, hardcoded** per-section recommendations; the Knowledge base (`knowledgeRoutes.ts`) stores SOPs for compliance but never analyzes them; nothing ingests a process doc / board snapshot / diagram and emits a more-efficient flow. There is no `compileFromDiagnostic` adapter turning a `tool_run`'s findings into a runnable `CompiledStep[]`. Fixing unblocks the literal pillar-1 promise "review SOPs → share a more efficient process flow." (primary: [ToolService.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/tools/ToolService.ts), [toolDefinitions.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/tools/toolDefinitions.ts), new `api/src/application/compile/compileFromDiagnostic.ts`)
  - 💰 **PILLAR 2 — trained agents have ZERO proprietary knowledge; dataset gen is LLM-synthetic only and memory recall is never wired to inference.** `/api/ide/datasets/generate` (`ideRoutes.ts`) produces synthetic examples from a capability prompt and never reads uploaded docs; `HybridRetriever` / `MemoryStore` / `chunk.ts` exist in `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory` but are not connected to publish or inference; `/api/ide/agents/:id/chat` never retrieves from `MemoryStore`; `mamba_state` is stored and surfaced only as a `[Memory: step=X]` signal glimpse in `agentPrompt.ts`. No `POST /api/ide/agents/:id/ingest` (chunk→embed→remember) and no recall-at-inference. Fixing unblocks the pillar-2 promise "train an agent on a company's proprietary data → custom support agent." (primary: [ideRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/ideRoutes.ts) `/datasets/generate` + `/agents/:id/chat`, [agentPrompt.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/agent/agentPrompt.ts), `builderforce-memory/packages/memory/src/retrieval/HybridRetriever.ts`)
  - 🛠️ **PILLAR 3 — surface parity incomplete: IDE loop is divergent, desktop has no agent path, container demotes to durable.** Cloud-durable + on-prem-relay share `AgentEngine`, but the VS Code agent (`clients/vscode/src/agent.ts` `runAgent()`) is a standalone ReAct loop **not** behind `AgentEngine`; native desktop apps (`apps/*`) have no TypeScript/relay agent-execution path; `cloud-container` is declared in `cloudDispatch.ts` but always falls back to the durable DO (executor not finalized); and the shell-less durable Worker has no git-write capability. Fixing unblocks "same custom agent runs in IDE, desktop, or cloud" — each is scoped as adding a `deploy()` target, not a rewrite. (primary: [agent.ts](Builderforce.ai/clients/vscode/src/agent.ts), [cloudDispatch.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/runtime/cloudDispatch.ts), `apps/*`)
  - 🛠️ **PILLAR 4 — persona exec-params + governance gates compile but never reach workflow agent dispatch.** `psychometrics.ts` compiles a profile to directives **and** `thinkLevel`/`reasoningLevel`/`temperature`, but those params are consumed only by IDE chat + workforce inference (`agentPrompt.ts`) — the workflow orchestrator dispatches agent nodes with `role`/`task`/`config` and never threads persona/psychometric context. Governance (`governanceRoutes.ts`) is CRUD/observability only: no `PolicyGate` is evaluated in `AgentEngine.run` (no approval/block/inject). Fixing unblocks "manager embeds steps into an agent that behaves to its persona and policy" on every surface. (primary: `agent-runtime/src/builderforce/psychometrics.ts`, [agentPrompt.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/agent/agentPrompt.ts), [governanceRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/governanceRoutes.ts))
  - 🛠️ **CROSS-CUTTING — no `AgentSpec` IR, no plain-language front door, `buildAgentSystemPrompt` consumed by only 2 of 4 paths.** The four front doors compile to four different artifacts; there is no canonical `AgentSpec` they lower into, no `compile()` modality registry, no `deploy()` surface registry, and no `compileFromProse` adapter so a human can describe a need in plain language. `buildAgentSystemPrompt()` is the de-facto shared lowering but only IDE chat + workforce use it. Fixing (Phase C1–C2 of the PRD) is the root that collapses the four pillar gaps above into shared edges. (primary: new `packages/agent-tools/src/spec.ts`, new `api/src/application/{compile,deploy}/`, [agentPrompt.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/agent/agentPrompt.ts))

- 🛠️ **KNOWLEDGE MANAGEMENT shipped — follow-up gaps (2026-06-27).** New SOP/Process/Doc knowledge base landed (mig `0227`, `knowledgeRoutes.ts`, `/knowledge` + `/knowledge/[id]`): documents with versioning, tags, read-acknowledgement audit (SOX/TISAX/ISO), training assignments + compliance rollup, AI-assisted authoring (`/api/knowledge/ai/draft` via `ideProxy`, metered through `logTrace`), and **per-document collaborators** (invite users to a page as editor/viewer; per-doc edit authz via `resolveAccess`, members author, managers own the audit). Remaining open edges:
  - 🟡 **CODE-COMPLETE, INFRA-BLOCKED — real-time co-editing.** Correctness fixes landed: the fragile seed-on-`sync` (which never fired for a lone editor against the dumb-relay `CollaborationRoom` DO → empty shared text → later joiners desynced from the visible content) is replaced with a connect-settle seed guarded by a deterministic, unit-tested `shouldSeed` tiebreak (smallest userId seeds; no double-insert on simultaneous open). Caret is now preserved across remote edits (best-effort, collab-path-only). Residual is purely operational and **cannot be done from code here**: (1) deploy the `worker/` `CollaborationRoom`, (2) set `NEXT_PUBLIC_COLLAB_WS_URL`, (3) run a 2-client live smoke test. A later polish item: the DO is a binary relay (not server-authoritative) — for production-grade multi-cursor, make the DO hold the Y.Doc (y-websocket server protocol) or bind via `y-prosemirror`. Default (env unset) stays solid single-user autosave. (primary: [useDocCollaboration.ts](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/hooks/useDocCollaboration.ts), `worker/src/durable-objects/CollaborationRoom.ts`)
  - 🛠️ **OPEN (separate epic, other track) — diagnostics-engine ingestion.** The *diagnostics* side (`ToolService.ts` / `agentic-maturity` / `compileFromDiagnostic`) still doesn't pull these SOPs into its scoring/compile path; that lives in the diagnostics track, not the knowledge build. The knowledge base now exposes the documents + the analyzer above as the ingestion source. (primary: [ToolService.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/tools/ToolService.ts), new `api/src/application/compile/compileFromDiagnostic.ts`)
