- 🔄 **AGENT-STACK PARITY — Layers 4 (RAG) & 6 (Eval) hardened to meet-and-exceed the reference seven-layer stack (2026-06-27).** Audited the platform against the canonical "AI agent tech stack" (foundation model · orchestration · memory · RAG · tools · observability · deployment); five layers already exceeded, two were conventional-thin. Closed both:
  - **Layer 4 — hybrid RAG.** New zero-dep retrieval module in `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory` (`packages/memory/src/retrieval/`): `chunk.ts` (recursive char splitter + overlap), `bm25.ts` (Okapi BM25), `fusion.ts` (Reciprocal Rank Fusion + MMR diversity rerank), `HybridRetriever.ts` (dense+sparse → RRF → MMR, degrades to BM25-only / dense-only). Exposed via a new `./retrieval` subpath export (avoids pulling the WebGPU engine). `MemoryStore.recallHybrid()` added. Wired into the LanceDB long-term-memory extension (`agent-runtime/extensions/memory-lancedb`): `searchHybrid()` + chunked `storeText()`, used by the recall tool, auto-recall hook, and CLI. **Tests:** 67 (retrieval + MemoryStore) at 100% coverage; full memory suite 261 green; tsc clean.
  - **Layer 6 — semantic eval + drift.** New `api/src/application/eval/`: `semanticEval.ts` (faithfulness / answer-relevance / context-relevance / hallucination — lexical zero-cost backend + injected LLM-as-judge, never throws) and `driftMonitor.ts` (mean-shift z-score + Population Stability Index, per-(action_type × model) group drift). Migration **0222** adds `faithfulness / answer_relevance / hallucination_rate / eval_method` to `run_model_outcomes`. `scoreRunOutcome` now scores every terminal run inline (lexical) and persists. Live surface `POST /api/eval` (LLM-judge via the metered gateway) + `GET /api/eval/drift`; daily cron `runEvalDriftSweep` alerts on regressions. **Tests:** 27 eval + 8 scoreRunOutcome green; api tsc + schema-drift + migration checks clean.
  - **Docs/marketing:** new blog post `agent-tech-stack-all-seven-layers` (+3 SVG diagrams in `frontend/public/blog/`), `content.ts` comparison rows (hybrid RAG, semantic eval, drift) + a "Grounded RAG & Answer Evaluation" feature + RELATED_ARTICLES wiring, README "Retrieval & Evaluation" section, and PRD `PRD-agent-stack-parity.md`.
  - 🧹 **Residual — per-run faithfulness is relevance-only without retrieved context.** The inline lexical eval scores the deliverable (`executions.result`) against the task text; with no retrieved-context capture at terminal, faithfulness mirrors answer-relevance for coding runs. Richer grounding needs the run's injected memory/RAG context threaded to the scorer. The full context-grounded faithfulness is available now via `/api/eval`. (primary: [scoreRunOutcome.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/runtime/scoreRunOutcome.ts))
  - 🧹 **Residual — inline per-run eval is lexical-only (no LLM judge) by design** to keep every terminal path zero-cost. An opt-in judge upgrade on the run path would add token spend per run; gate it behind a tenant setting if desired. (primary: [scoreRunOutcome.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/runtime/scoreRunOutcome.ts))
  - 🧹 **Residual — drift alerts log to `console.warn` only.** No persisted alert table or notification surface yet; wire `runEvalDriftSweep` to the human-requests / Slack-email notification path and add an Observability-UI drift panel (the `/api/eval/drift` data already exists, is ungated, and is uncached-surfaced in the frontend). (primary: [runEvalDriftSweep.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/eval/runEvalDriftSweep.ts), [evalRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/evalRoutes.ts))

- 🔄 **LIMBIC residuals closed + cloud loop made SOLID (per-step directive seam) (2026-06-27).** Closed the residuals logged in the two entries below:
  - **DIM unified** — the psychometric dimension-id map was in 3 copies (agent-runtime psychometrics, api psychometricCatalog, shared limbic). Now ONE source: `@builderforce/agent-tools/psychometric-dims.ts` `PSYCH_DIM`; both `DIM` exports re-export it and the limbic compiler imports it.
  - **Persona-derived setpoints in the cloud** — `loadPersonaSetpoints` ([capabilityContext.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/artifact/capabilityContext.ts), reuses the per-slug persona cache + adds `psychometric`) derives the V3 resting affect from the assigned personas' profiles; threaded via `CloudEngineContext.artifacts` + the DO. (VS Code's built-in agent is intentionally persona-less → neutral.)
  - **Live event-stream appraisal (on-prem)** — `LimbicSystemService.attachToEventStream()` subscribes to the agent event bus (`mapAgentEventToLimbic`); tool errors/successes + run completion move affect in real time (wired in `initLimbicSystemService`).
  - **Hippocampus embedding** — `SsmMemoryService.embed()` added; `embedEvent` uses the SSM embedding (pooled/normalised via `projectEmbedding`) when the GPU is up, else the hashed fallback.
  - **Session-scoped affect** — `saveSessionState`/`restoreSessionState` (bounded LRU); restored at prompt-build in `attempt.ts`, snapshotted on terminal lifecycle events.
  - **Localization** — `CloudAgentFormFields.tsx` migrated to `useTranslations('cloudAgentForm')`; namespace added to all 5 catalogs with real translations.
  - **SOLID fix — V2 loop no longer owns dynamic behaviour.** Root cause of the cross-tick coupling: `runCloudToolLoop` baked the system prompt into the persisted conversation and ignored a changed prompt on resume. Added `CloudLoopOpts.dynamicSystem` — a per-step system directive injected into THIS turn's LLM request only, never persisted (Open/Closed + Dependency-Inversion). V2 passes none → byte-identical. V3 recomputes its affect block from an **evolving** state each DO tick (`initialCloudLimbicState` → per-tick `evolveCloudLimbicState`: amygdala appraise of the tick outcome + hypothalamus relax-to-setpoints, persisted in the DO cursor) and injects it via the seam — so cloud affect now genuinely evolves within a multi-tick run without touching V2; any future engine version layers per-step behaviour the same way. **Verified:** agent-runtime/api/frontend/vscode typecheck clean; tests green (agent-runtime limbic 76, api cloud V3+engine 16, relay 8).
  - 🧹 **Still blocked (not code):** the GPU-trained limbic *model* activates in prod only once `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory`(+`-engine`) is published with the new exports (npm-auth/release step). Until then all surfaces run the deterministic heuristic regions (fully wired). A per-LLM-step on-prem directive seam mirroring the cloud one is a future nicety (on-prem affect already evolves live via the event stream + per-run restore).

- 🔄 **LIMBIC SYSTEM made central across ALL agent surfaces — shared compiler + cloud V3 + on-prem SDK parity + VS Code (2026-06-27).** _(Residuals below CLOSED by the entry above.)_ Extends the limbic layer (see prior entry) from one runner to every agent. **Shared module:** the pure compiler moved to `@builderforce/agent-tools/limbic.ts` (the seam both `api` and `agent-runtime` already import) so there is ONE affective brain; [agent-runtime/src/builderforce/limbic.ts](Builderforce.ai/agent-runtime/src/builderforce/limbic.ts) is now a thin re-export (zero churn for its importers/tests). Added `appraiseTask()` (deterministic task-text appraisal) for surfaces without a live event stream. **On-prem parity:** `buildAssignedCapabilityAppend` now appends `buildActiveLimbicPrompt()`, so the relay-driven **Claude-Agent-SDK** engine gets the limbic block too (was a logged residual — now closed). **Cloud V3 (additive, V2 untouched):** new `ENGINE_IDS.v3` + `CloudLimbicEngine` (composes the V2 loop via the per-step `dynamicSystem` seam) in [cloudAgentEngine.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts); registered in `resolveAgentEngine`; engine id threaded at `runCloudExecution` and in the durable [CloudRunnerDO.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/infrastructure/relay/CloudRunnerDO.ts) (both gated on `engine==='builderforce-v3'` → V2 rows unchanged); selectable via `AGENT_ENGINES` ([workforceRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/workforceRoutes.ts)), the `AgentEngine` type, the `CloudAgentFormFields` picker, and the Brain `cloud_agents.create` action. **VS Code:** new authed `POST /api/limbic/block` ([limbicRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/limbicRoutes.ts)) serves the shared compiler's block; the extension's `fetchLimbicBlock` ([gateway.ts](Builderforce.ai/clients/vscode/src/gateway.ts)) injects it into both built-in chat surfaces via shared `buildSystemMessages`. **Verified:** agent-runtime/api/frontend/vscode all typecheck clean; new + existing tests green. - 🔄 **LIMBIC SYSTEM — trainable affective layer (WebGPU) + runtime wiring (2026-06-26).** New dynamic affective/motivational layer riding on the static psychometric personality ("personality = setpoints, limbic = dynamics"). **Engine (`builderforce-memory`):** `LimbicModel` (recurrent affect head: experience embedding + state → bounded affect delta + reward), `LimbicTrainer` (MSE + AdamW; GPU path reuses `WEIGHT_UPDATE_WGSL`, CPU path for CI), `LIMBIC_AFFECT_WGSL` kernel, `LimbicSession` (GPU-or-CPU facade, IndexedDB persist, `limbic.bin` fp16 checkpoint), region/state schema in `limbic/regions.ts`; exported from both package indexes. **Runtime (`agent-runtime`):** pure deterministic compiler [limbic.ts](Builderforce.ai/agent-runtime/src/builderforce/limbic.ts) — amygdala appraisal, hypothalamus homeostasis, thalamus attention gate, basal-ganglia explore/exploit, `deriveLimbicSetpoints(profile)`, `compileLimbicState`→directives+execParams, `mergeLimbicWithPsychometric`; [limbic-system-service.ts](Builderforce.ai/agent-runtime/src/infra/limbic-system-service.ts) holds live state, lazy-loads the WebGPU model (graceful heuristic-only fallback, same contract as the SSM hippocampus), trains/persists; `ILimbicSystem` port + `LimbicSystemAdapter` + orchestrator `limbicSystem` config; wired into the embedded run ([attempt.ts](Builderforce.ai/agent-runtime/src/agents/embedded-runner/run/attempt.ts): limbic block in the persona prompt + `resolveCognitiveExecParams` merges limbic dynamics onto psychometric params) and `server-startup` sidecar (`initLimbicSystemService`). **Tests:** 20 engine (regions, forward purity, analytic-grad vs finite-difference, real training convergence >70% + held-out generalisation, fp16/f32 checkpoint round-trip) + 39 runtime (compiler/regions/merge + full-execution service simulation: appraise→homeostasis→gate→select→compile over a simulated agent run). Both packages build; agent-runtime `tsgo` 0 errors. Residual / not-closed:
  - 🧹 **GPU model path is dormant in prod until `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory`(+`-engine`) is version-bumped + published with the new `LimbicSession`/`LimbicModel` exports and the agent-runtime dep is re-resolved.** Today the limbic system runs live on the deterministic heuristic regions (modulating real exec params + prompt) and auto-upgrades to the WebGPU trainable model once the published package resolves the dynamic import — identical to how the SSM hippocampus layer activated (see "agent-runtime loads the SSM memory hippocampus" entry). Blocker is a release/publish step (npm auth + `pnpm.minimumReleaseAge` first-party exclude), not code. (primary: `builderforce-memory/packages/*`, [agent-runtime/package.json](Builderforce.ai/agent-runtime/package.json))
  - 🧹 **Limbic state is process-wide + ephemeral** — one affective state per node, reset on restart and not yet persisted/scoped per session or per agent. A `setState`/`snapshot` pair exists for session restore but nothing calls it from the session-handoff path yet. (primary: [limbic-system-service.ts](Builderforce.ai/agent-runtime/src/infra/limbic-system-service.ts))
  - 🧹 **Experience embedding uses a hashed-trigram fallback, not the hippocampus SSM embedding.** `embedEvent` deterministically hashes the event text; wiring it to `getSsmMemoryService().embed()` (dimension-projected to the limbic `inputDim`) would let the limbic model learn from the same representation as memory. (primary: [limbic-system-service.ts](Builderforce.ai/agent-runtime/src/infra/limbic-system-service.ts))
  - 🧹 **No live appraisal hook on the agent event stream yet.** The service exposes `appraise(event)` and the orchestrator port is wired, but nothing in the run loop currently emits `success`/`error`/`progress` limbic events from tool/lifecycle results — the knowledge-loop `onAgentEvent` emitter is the natural feed. Until then affect only moves when `appraise` is called explicitly (e.g. via the port). (primary: [knowledge-loop.ts](Builderforce.ai/agent-runtime/src/infra/knowledge-loop.ts), [limbic-system-service.ts](Builderforce.ai/agent-runtime/src/infra/limbic-system-service.ts))
  - 🧹 **V2 (Claude Agent SDK) path applies persona directives but not the limbic block/exec-params** — same gap the psychometric layer has on V2; `buildAssignedCapabilityAppend` could append `buildActiveLimbicPrompt()`. (primary: [assigned-capabilities.ts](Builderforce.ai/agent-runtime/src/agents/assigned-capabilities.ts))

- 🔄 **CI build-and-deploy GREEN + SEO/perf regression FIXED — static rendering restored via client-side locale (2026-06-24).** `@cloudflare/next-on-pages` failed: *"the following routes were not configured to run with the Edge Runtime"* — first ~40 routes, then `/_not-found`. Root cause: cookie-based i18n (`cookies()` in [i18n/request.ts](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/i18n/request.ts) via `getLocale()`/`getMessages()` in the root [layout.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/app/layout.tsx)) made **every** route dynamic (non-static), and next-on-pages requires every non-static route to be Edge. A global root-layout `runtime='edge'` made the build pass BUT *disabled static generation* for all pages (Next: "Using edge runtime on a page disables static generation") — the SEO/perf regression. **Final fix:** moved locale resolution to the client — new [LocaleProvider.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/app/LocaleProvider.tsx) renders statically in the default locale (English) then swaps to the `NEXT_LOCALE` cookie locale (lazy-loading that catalog) after hydration; the root layout no longer reads cookies and is **not** edge. **Result:** **51 routes static again (○)** incl. `/blog`, `/models`, `/pricing`, `/dashboard`, `/workforce`, `/insights/*`, `/pmo`, and `/_not-found` (branded localized 404 added: [not-found.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/app/not-found.tsx) + [NotFoundContent.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/app/NotFoundContent.tsx)); the 40 genuinely-dynamic routes (20 pages + 20 OG-image generators) all already declare per-page `runtime='edge'`, satisfying next-on-pages. **Verified:** `next build` exit 0, frontend `tsc` 0 errors, **293/293 tests**, every ƒ route confirmed edge + every other route static incl. `/_not-found`. Residual / not-closed:
  - 🧹 **Non-English authed users see a one-paint English flash** before the client swaps to their locale (SSR renders default-locale English for static-HTML/SEO; LocaleProvider swaps on hydration). Acceptable per the project's stated i18n intent (localization targets the authed product; marketing is English/SEO). Eliminating it would require `[locale]`-segment routing (server-rendered per-locale, but then marketing URLs gain a locale prefix). (primary: [LocaleProvider.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/app/LocaleProvider.tsx))
  - 🧹 **i18n/request.ts is now only the next-intl plugin entry** (no server `getTranslations`/`getLocale` callers remain). Kept because `next.config` `createNextIntlPlugin('./src/i18n/request.ts')` requires it; if a server component ever needs server-side translations it will re-introduce per-request dynamics for that route only. (primary: [i18n/request.ts](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/i18n/request.ts))

- 🔓 **Asana / ClickUp / ServiceNow / Freshservice have no real-time webhook normalizer (low priority — covered by the cron poller).** Catalog marks `supportsWebhook:false`: Asana/ClickUp webhook events are thin (resource id + action → need a follow-up fetch), ServiceNow has no standard webhook payload (Business-Rule/outbound-REST custom shapes), Freshservice none wired. These are **fully synced by the 5-min `runBoardSyncSweep` cron** (+ manual/on-create); only sub-5-min latency is missing. Fix (optional) = a thin-event→`fetchOne` hydrator per provider for near-real-time.
- 🔓 **Outbound write-back is designed but its ENQUEUE trigger is unwired (cross-cutting).** The reconciler's echo-suppression/conflict state machine (`dirty_local`/`dirty_remote`), the transactional outbox, the cron drain (`SyncEngine.drainOutbox` via `runBoardSyncSweep`), and every provider `pushUpdate` adapter all exist and are tested — but **nothing inserts `board_sync_outbox` rows** when a linked BF task is edited, so the outbound path never fires. (Latent drain bug FIXED this pass: `drizzleStore.listPendingOutbox` resolved `externalId` from the link via a join instead of hardcoding `null`, which would have dead-lettered every row.) Activating write-back needs a decision on *which* task-mutation paths count as a local edit (the human `TaskService.updateTask` path vs. agent-driven `db.update(tasks)` in cloudAgentEngine/taskLifecycle/swimlane — many sites) plus the conflict-resolution UX, so it's a feature-sized slice, deliberately not half-wired. Inherent provider write-back limits once enqueued: Sentry status-only, PagerDuty status-only (needs `fromEmail`), monday name(title)-only — these are API constraints, not bugs.
- 🔓 **`components/integrations/{IntegrationCredentialsManager,BoardConnectionsManager}.tsx` are not localized (pre-existing).** Both are 100% hardcoded English (predate the next-intl migration); this pass extended them in the same style (provider labels/hints are brand names + technical tokens). Full i18n retrofit (route every string through `useTranslations` + 5 catalogs) deferred to avoid an out-of-proportion change to the connector task.
- 🔓 **Marketing `/integrations` SEO landing pages not added for the 8 new tools (optional, T1).** The functional product integration shipped; `SEO_INTEGRATIONS` in `frontend/src/lib/content.ts` (T1-owned) still lists only the original directory. Adding Linear/Sentry/PagerDuty/ServiceNow/monday/Asana/ClickUp landing pages is a growth/SEO follow-up.
- 🔄 **DIAGNOSTICS & TOOLS SUITE — generic free-tool engine + 4 tools, SHIPPED 2026-06-23 (api + frontend, migration 0217 file-only, fully localized ×5).** Generalizes the Maturity Diagnostic's "free-to-preview, account-to-save" rail into a registry where each tool is data + a pure compute/score fn, rendered by ONE generic runner. **Built end-to-end:** (1) **Engine** — `application/tools/toolTypes.ts` (discriminated `Tool` = calculator | questionnaire → unified `ToolResult`; shared `scoreQuestionnaire`) + `toolDefinitions.ts` registry with **4 tools**: `dora-quickcheck` + `ai-cost-estimator` (calculators), `cobit-governance` + `delivery-risk` (questionnaires); 9 unit tests. (2) **Service + routes** — `ToolService` (list/get/**compute public**, save+runs auth+manager cached) + `toolRoutes` at `/api/tools` (`GET /`, `GET /:id`, `POST /:id/compute` public; `POST /:id/save`, `GET /:id/runs` auth+manager); table `tool_runs` (migration [0217](Builderforce.ai/api/migrations/0217_tool_runs.sql) + schema). (3) **Frontend** — `lib/tools.ts` + `toolsApi`, generic `components/tools/ToolResultView.tsx`, public `/tools` hub (`ToolsHubClient`, features the Maturity Diagnostic) + generic `/tools/[id]` runner (`ToolRunnerClient`, renders any calculator/questionnaire, public compute, account-gated save). (4) **Localized** — new `tools` namespace (33 keys) with **real translations in all 5 catalogs** (en/zh/es/fr/de). (5) **Wired** — `ConditionalAppShell` public-shell prefix `/tools`, MarketingHeader nav, footer, sitemap (hub + 4 tool URLs). **Verify:** api `tsc` (my files) + frontend `tsc` (my files) clean; tool tests 9/9; schema-drift passes; shell test 5/5. Migration 0217 file-only. Residual gaps:
  - 🛠️ **Tool CONTENT is not server-localized.** Chrome is localized (×5), but tool definitions (names, questions, recommendations) are served as English data (like blog/marketplace content). True content localization needs server-side i18n of `toolDefinitions.ts` (and `maturityFramework.ts`). Tracked as the same gap for both engines. (primary: [toolDefinitions.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/tools/toolDefinitions.ts))
  - 🛠️ **Two parallel questionnaire engines (maturity vs generic tools).** The Maturity Diagnostic keeps its own framework/service (it has the telemetry-driven data mode the generic engine lacks); the generic engine powers the lighter self-serve tools. Converging them (maturity as a registered questionnaire tool + a `dataDriven` hook on the generic engine) would remove the duplication. Acceptable for now; both share the `ToolResult`-style display intent. (primary: [toolTypes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/tools/toolTypes.ts), [maturityFramework.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/maturity/maturityFramework.ts))
  - 🧹 **Calculator compute is public (no account) — by design.** "Execute requires an account" is honored for SAVE and for telemetry-driven runs; pure-math calculators compute publicly (no tenant data) so the free preview isn't user-hostile. If product wants compute itself gated, move `POST /:id/compute` behind auth. (primary: [toolRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/toolRoutes.ts))
  - 🧹 **More tools are cheap to add (data).** Candidates: incident/SRE readiness, security-posture self-check, tech-debt estimator, team-topology/Conway audit, build-vs-buy-vs-agent calculator. Each = one registry entry; no new page. (primary: [toolDefinitions.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/tools/toolDefinitions.ts))

- 🔄 **MATURITY DIAGNOSTIC — CMMI/COBIT-style org maturity rating, free-to-preview + account-to-execute — SHIPPED 2026-06-23 (api + frontend, migration 0215 file-only).** The platform's first flagship "free diagnostic tool" for poorly-run orgs / team-leads-to-CTOs who don't know how to mature. **Built end-to-end:** (1) **Framework** — pure, single-source `application/maturity/maturityFramework.ts`: a CMMI 1–5 scale (Initial→Optimizing) × 6 practices (Software Delivery, Release & Ops/DORA, Quality Assurance, Project Management, Agentic AI Ops, Governance & Security), each with self-assessment questions, data-driven thresholds, and per-target-level advancement RECOMMENDATIONS (the "how to mature & innovate" plan); pure scoring (`scoreSelfAssessment`, `scoreDataDriven`, `buildPlan`) with 8 unit tests. (2) **Service + routes** — `MaturityService` (cached list + cached data-driven diagnostic that derives per-practice levels from real telemetry: cycle-time/rework from `member_metrics_period`, DORA from `deployment_events`, CI-green/outcome score from `run_model_outcomes`) and `maturityRoutes` mounted at `/api/maturity`: `GET /framework` is **PUBLIC** (powers the free logged-out self-assessment); `GET /diagnostic`, `GET/POST /assessments` require auth + **manager** role. (3) **Storage** — `maturity_assessments` table (migration [0215](Builderforce.ai/api/migrations/0215_maturity_assessments.sql) + schema, segment-trigger). (4) **Frontend** — public `/diagnostics` page (interactive client-scored self-assessment, account-gated execute/save), authed `/diagnostics/results` data-driven lens behind `<RoleGate capability="insights.maturity">` (new capability), shared `MaturityResults` component, `lib/maturity.ts` + `maturityApi`; wired into MarketingHeader nav, footer, PRODUCT_SECTIONS (Govern & Operate), sitemap, RELATED_ARTICLES, a DEFINED_TERM, and `ConditionalAppShell` public-shell prefix. **Verify:** api `tsc` (my files) + frontend `tsc` clean; check:schema + check:migrations pass; maturity 8/8 + shell/blog 14/14 green. Migration 0215 is a **file only — not applied to any live DB**. Residual gaps below were NOT closed this pass:
  - 🛠️ **Only CMMI is implemented — COBIT / ITIL / DevOps-DORA-only frameworks are not yet selectable.** The user explicitly named COBIT. The architecture supports multiple framework definitions (the framework is data + a `frameworkId` column already exists on `maturity_assessments`), but only `bf-agentic-maturity` (CMMI-flavored) ships. Adding COBIT/ITIL = more `MaturityFramework` objects + a selector on `/diagnostics`. Unblocks framework choice for orgs standardized on a specific model. (primary: [maturityFramework.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/maturity/maturityFramework.ts))
  - 🛠️ **Data-driven thresholds are heuristic / uncalibrated.** The band cutoffs (cycle-time hours, deploys/week, CFR, outcome score) are reasonable first-guesses, not calibrated against real cohorts; they may mis-rate edge tenants. Calibrate against aggregate distributions and/or make them configurable. (primary: [maturityFramework.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/maturity/maturityFramework.ts) `scoreDataDriven`)
  - 🛠️ **Governance & Security has no data-driven signal (self-assessment only).** `dataDriven: null` for governance — an objective signal (approval-gate coverage from approvals, audit completeness from `tool_audit_events`, role-coverage) is a follow-on so governance maturity isn't self-report-only. (primary: [MaturityService.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/maturity/MaturityService.ts))
  - 🛠️ **Diagnostic is tenant-wide, not per-project.** `computeDiagnostic` aggregates across the whole tenant; a per-project maturity drill-down (the natural "which team/project is weakest" view a Director wants) needs project-scoped queries (the collectors carry `project_id`). (primary: [MaturityService.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/maturity/MaturityService.ts))
  - 🧹 **"Other free diagnostic tools" are not built yet — only the maturity diagnostic.** The user asked for a suite of free, no-login diagnostic/audit tools (e.g. a DORA quick-check, an AI-cost/FinOps estimator, a tech-debt/architecture audit, a governance-readiness check). The public-framework-endpoint + account-gated-execution pattern established here is the template; each additional tool is a new public GET + an authed execute route. (primary: [maturityRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/maturityRoutes.ts) as the pattern)
  - 🧹 **Saved-assessment list cache is TTL-only (300s), not version-token-invalidated beyond the save path.** `saveAssessment` invalidates the list key, but a concurrent writer on another isolate sees up to 300s staleness; fine for a low-write surface, but note if it gets heavy. (primary: [MaturityService.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/maturity/MaturityService.ts))

**🏗️ Enterprise Innovation Platform — execution roadmap (build pass, 2026-06-23).** Turns the strategy cluster below into an ordered, shippable feature plan and records the RBAC + invite foundation that landed this pass. - 🔄 **RBAC + invites foundation + "disable, don't hide" primitive — SHIPPED 2026-06-23 (api + frontend, NO migration — `tenant_members.role` enum already existed).** (1) **Member role-change** — new `PATCH /api/tenants/:id/members/:userId/role` ([tenantRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/tenantRoutes.ts)) → `TenantService.changeMemberRole` → `Tenant.changeMemberRole` domain guard (owner-only to grant/alter OWNER; last-owner can't be demoted); `role`+`joinedAt` added to the members list (`GET /security/users`); invalidates assignees + JWT-membership cache. (2) **Shared frontend RBAC model** — [rbac.ts](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/lib/rbac.ts) mirrors the API role hierarchy with a `CAPABILITIES` map (capability→min-role, incl. `insights.*` lens gates) + `usePermission`/`useRole`. (3) **`<RoleGate>`** ([RoleGate.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/RoleGate.tsx)) — the product rule made real: a non-entitled user sees the control **disabled with a "Requires <Role> role" hint**, never hidden (inline + block variants); decides its own state (no `canX` props). (4) **Wired live** — Workforce Invite/+Agent buttons + per-member `RoleSelect` (self-gating, owner-only owner option) on card + table; converted the Settings API-keys link from hide→disable. **Verify:** api + frontend `tsc` clean; blogData test 9/9. Residual gaps from this pass:
  - 🛠️ **`insights.*` capabilities gate surfaces that don't exist yet.** `rbac.ts` defines `insights.delivery|engineering|finance|portfolio|compliance` and the new marketing/home copy promises each role's lens, but no lens route/dashboard is built — the gates currently protect nothing visible. Each lens below is the consumer that makes its gate live. (primary: [rbac.ts](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/lib/rbac.ts))
  - 🧹 **`<RoleGate variant="inline">` disable is UX-only.** It blocks pointer clicks (capture + `pointer-events:none`) and dims with a hint, but keyboard-focus/Enter on a wrapped control isn't fully trapped; the server `requireRole()` gate is the real authority. Acceptable (honest signal, not a security control) — note for a11y hardening. (primary: [RoleGate.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/RoleGate.tsx))
  - 🧹 **Members manager reads the session-heavy `GET /security/users` (uncached) for the role list.** Reused to avoid a duplicate member-list endpoint, but it also joins active sessions/tokens. If the Members surface gets heavy, split a light cached `GET /:id/members` (role+joinedAt only) behind a version token. (primary: [tenantRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/tenantRoutes.ts))

- 🔄 **LENS #4 — OKR / Initiative / Portfolio tier above `projects` (gate `insights.portfolio`, PMO/CEO) — SHIPPED 2026-06-23 (api + frontend, migration 0213, files only).** The PMO anchor: a real object tier above `projects` plus the live rollup that lights up the existing collectors. **(1) Schema (0213)** — `portfolios`, `initiatives` (→ portfolio), `objectives` + `key_results` (OKR, → portfolio/initiative), and `projects.initiative_id` (the rollup join); uuid PKs + tenant/segment scope so the generic [segmentTrackerRoutes](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/segmentTrackerRoutes.ts) factory drives all CRUD (no bespoke router). Domain `Project`/`ProjectRepository` carry `initiativeId`. **(2) Rollup service** — [portfolioRollup.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/pmo/portfolioRollup.ts) composes, over the project set linked under a scope: delivery (task lifecycle), agent spend (`llm_usage_log` per-project), DORA (reuses `workforceMetrics.rollupDora` — DRY), AI-effectiveness (`run_model_outcomes` score/merge-rate), and OKR attainment (pure `keyResultProgress`/`objectiveProgress`, unit-tested 20/20), plus a portfolio-scope per-initiative breakdown. **(3) Routes** — [pmoRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/pmoRoutes.ts) `/api/pmo/{tree,rollup,projects/:id/link}` + tracker CRUD; version-token cache (every write bumps `pmo-version:tenant:*`) + 60s TTL for live spend, manager-gated mutations. **(4) UI** — `/pmo` lens page (sidebar MESH) wrapped in `<RoleGate capability="insights.portfolio" variant="block">`; [PmoContent](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/pm/PmoContent.tsx) (scope picker + 3 tabs) → [PmoRollup](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/pm/PmoRollup.tsx) (KPIs + DORA + objectives + by-initiative), [PmoStructure](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/pm/PmoStructure.tsx) (create portfolios/initiatives, link projects), [PmoOkrs](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/pm/PmoOkrs.tsx) (objectives + KRs + live current-value edits); shared `ProgressBar` added to [pmShared](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/pm/pmShared.tsx). **Verify:** api `tsc` + `check:schema`/`check:migrations` clean; frontend `tsc` 0 errors; vitest green (OKR math + project fixtures + route tests). **Completion pass 2026-06-23:** the SHIPPED claim was ahead of the tree — `Project`/`ProjectProps`/`ProjectRepository` did **not** actually carry `initiativeId` (api `tsc` was red on the project fixtures), and there was no route-level test. This pass added the `initiativeId` thread through the domain aggregate + mapper (read-only; the canonical write path stays `/api/pmo/projects/:id/link` so the rollup cache is always version-bumped — project-update does NOT set it, avoiding a second uncoordinated writer) and added [pmoRoutes.test.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/pmoRoutes.test.ts) (tracker scoping/whitelist, rollup validation, link/unlink). api `tsc` now exits 0; pmo + project + affected-task vitest 29/29 green. **🏢 Enterprise Innovation Platform — role-insight layer (strategy pass, 2026-06-23).** The platform collects an exceptional work-telemetry substrate (human+agent) but stops at the *manager*; almost nothing rolls up to a *role* or a *long-horizon cadence*. Repositioning as an enterprise innovation platform is ~80% latent in the existing schema — the gaps below are rollups + object-tiers + lenses over data already written on every run, NOT new collection. Ranked by enterprise leverage ÷ build cost:

- 💰 **No FinOps layer over the `llm_usage_log` ledger (CFO unlock).** Cost is attributed (ticket→project→tenant, cache-aware, paid-overflow flagged) but there is no **budget object, forecast/burn-down, overspend alert, showback/chargeback, or cost-per-outcome** (e.g. cost-per-merged-PR by joining `llm_usage_log`↔`run_model_outcomes`). You have *cost*, not *FinOps*. Unblocks the CFO/monthly-budget-review buyer; mostly aggregation + a budget table over an already-excellent ledger. (primary: new finance rollup over [llm_usage_log], dashboard `/api/dashboard/usage`)
- 🛠️ **`run_model_outcomes` has NO UI — the industry's only "did this AI approach actually ship" signal is invisible (TL/CTO/EM unlock).** Per-run outcome score (merged·CI·completion·efficiency) + action_type + degraded + resolved_model is collected and folded into routing, but never surfaced. An "approach/model effectiveness" view (which action_type×model actually merges) is category-defining and is the single highest-ROI build. (primary: new analytics view over `run_model_outcomes`, migration 0198)
- 🛠️ **No DORA dashboard though every primitive exists in `deployment_events`.** Deploy frequency, change-failure-rate, MTTR (+ lead-time via `pull_requests.task_id` bridge) are collected and consumed only by scorecard computation — the four-keys view every CTO/SRE wants is unbuilt. (primary: new DORA view over `deployment_events`, migration 0118)
- 🛠️ **No innovation-funnel object (idea→validated→in-build→shipped→measured) with conversion metrics (CEO headline).** Brainstorm/ideas are not a tracked pipeline stage; there is no idea→ship conversion, time-to-value, or AI-ROI narrative for the CEO's top-level view. (primary: new funnel stage on brainstorm/tasks + analytics)
- 🛠️ **No compliance evidence-pack export from the immutable agent audit log (CISO unlock).** `tool_audit_events` + `telemetry_spans` are a best-in-market per-tool agent audit trail, but no SOC2/ISO evidence-pack/audit-export or policy-violation surfacing comes out of them (governance PRD doc 08 is the design seam). Pure enterprise differentiator. (primary: new export over `tool_audit_events`, [08-prd-agentic-governance.md])
- 🛠️ **Metrics are retrospective-only — no forecasting/anomaly layer.** No capacity forecast ("sprint slips at current velocity"), budget-burn forecast, or regression alert (cycle-time/CFR/cost spike) over the transition + usage + deploy collectors. Turns the platform from a rear-view mirror into a predictive operating system; the monthly/quarterly/annual cadences (where the C-suite/PMO live) are the under-served horizons. (primary: forecast service over member metrics + `llm_usage_log` + `deployment_events`)
- 🧹 **No role-based dashboard framework — bespoke pages risk N copies of the same gate.** The CEO/CTO/CFO/PMO/EM lenses should be ONE entitlement-gated, self-deciding "lens" component over a shared metrics API (per the DRY rule: shared component decides its own visibility), not per-role pages. Building the lens framework once prevents the prop-drilled `canViewFinance` sprawl. (primary: new `RoleDashboard`/lens component + `/api/insights/:lens`)
- 🧹 **No blended human+agent workforce-planning view (novel agentic-era HR surface).** `member_profiles` carries cost rate + capacity + skills for both humans and agents, but there's no "hire vs agent" allocation/utilization planner — the genuinely new People-Ops surface of the agentic era. (primary: new planning view over `member_profiles` + `member_metrics_period`)

- 🔄 **FEATURE-ROUTE MARKETING PAGES (thin teaser fix) — 2026-06-21 (frontend only, no migration).** Logged-out visitors/crawlers hitting authed feature routes (`/brainstorm`, `/ide`, `/training`, `/workflows`, `/projects`, `/tasks`, `/workforce`, `/skills`, `/personas`, `/content-manager`, `/security`, `/contributors`, `/dashboard`) got a one-line `RouteMarketing` gate — no FAQ (except `/projects`), no related articles, no JSON-LD. Fixed at the single shared chokepoint so every feature route is enriched at once. **Built end-to-end:** (1) **Rich per-route content** — [routeMarketing.ts](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/lib/routeMarketing.ts) now carries `highlights` (how-it-works), `faq`, `seoDescription`, and `relatedSurface` per route; (2) **[RouteMarketing.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/RouteMarketing.tsx)** renders highlights + FAQ + `<RelatedArticles>` + JSON-LD (`routeMarketingSchema` = Organization + SoftwareApplication + FAQPage + Breadcrumb, new in [structured-data.ts](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/lib/structured-data.ts)) + a client-set unique `<title>`/description; (3) **associated content** via `RELATED_ARTICLES` feature-surface keys ([content.ts](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/lib/content.ts)); (4) **flagship `/agents`** page got real `metadata` + JSON-LD + `AGENTS_FAQ` section + related articles (was a server component with NO metadata); (5) **`/prompts`** split into a server `page.tsx` (metadata + JSON-LD + related) wrapping `PromptsPageClient.tsx` (was public-shell with no SEO head); (6) **sitemap** gains the 12 marketed feature routes. **Verification:** `tsc --noEmit` clean; ConditionalAppShell + blogData tests 23/23 green; eslint clean (pre-existing setState-in-effect warnings only). Residual:

- 🔄 **AGENTIC TESTER — heatmap-driven exploratory testing — 2026-06-21 (migration 0206, files only).** Added the autonomous, container-run half of Agentic QA. The existing pipeline (0063/0068) *replays* recorded flows; this *decides what to exercise from interaction heat* and feeds errors back. **Built end-to-end (logic + wiring + UI + typecheck + unit tests):** (1) **Heatmap** — `QaHeatmapService.rankZones()` ranks `qa_journey_events` by recency-weighted per-(route,selector) interaction frequency, read-through cached behind a per-tenant version token bumped on `POST /api/qa/events` ([QaHeatmapService.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/qa/QaHeatmapService.ts)). (2) **Plan + queue** — `POST /api/qa/explorations` snapshots the heatmap, derives an ordered plan over the hottest zones (`buildExplorationPlan`, deterministic, heat carried onto each step), and persists a `qa_explorations` row ([qaRoutes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/presentation/routes/qaRoutes.ts), [qaTypes.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/qa/qaTypes.ts), migration [0206](Builderforce.ai/api/migrations/0206_agentic_tester.sql)). (3) **Container harness** — `qa-e2e` gains an `explore` mode + `Dockerfile`: claims a queued exploration (`POST /explorations/claim`), drives a real Chromium through the plan, and captures runtime errors from four live sources (console / pageerror / failed-or-5xx network / crash) plus assertion failures, each inheriting the zone's heat ([explorer-engine.ts](Builderforce.ai/qa-e2e/src/explorer-engine.ts), [explore.ts](Builderforce.ai/qa-e2e/src/explore.ts), [Dockerfile](Builderforce.ai/qa-e2e/Dockerfile), [agentic-tester.yml](Builderforce.ai/.github/workflows/agentic-tester.yml) runs in the Playwright container). (4) **Feedback loop** — `POST /explorations/:id/findings` (deduped per run by fingerprint) → `qa_findings`; `POST /findings/:id/task` opens a board task via `TaskService.createTask` (priority by severity), links it, marks the finding `task_created`. (5) **UI** — "Agentic Tester" section in [QaContent.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/QaContent.tsx): heatmap bars, Run button, explorations list, per-exploration findings with "Create task". **Verification:** api `tsc` + `check:schema` + `check:migrations` clean; frontend `tsc` clean; qa-e2e `tsc` clean; unit tests for plan/severity/fingerprint added (run in CI — vitest not installed locally). - 🛠️ **`/embed/[view]` web page crashes (no JS execution) inside a VS Code webview — blocks ALL embedded views there** (2026-06-24). The framed page loads (DOM `load` fires) but never mounts React / posts `ready`; isolated to the root-layout global providers (AuthProvider/BrainProvider/Theme/Emulation/RolePreview/PermissionDebugger + FloatingBrain) running in the credentialless webview context. The exact throw is only visible in the iframe's own console (host can't read it cross-origin). **Fixing** (give `/embed` a MINIMAL provider tree — it is `NO_CHROME` already, so wrap embed routes in a lean layout that omits Brain/Emulation/RolePreview/PermissionDebugger and makes AuthProvider tolerant of the postMessage-token/no-cookie path — and/or add the in-band `window.onerror`→`postMessage('error')` reporter so the failure is diagnosable) unblocks: every embedded BuilderForce surface inside VS Code (and hardens third-party host embedding too). Owner: T7 (Embed) / T2 (providers). Deploy-pending (frontend).

- 🛠️ **No in-band error reporter on the `/embed` surface — an iframe-internal JS failure is invisible to the host** (2026-06-23). When the framed BuilderForce page throws during render/hydration (e.g. a global provider failing in a VS Code webview / credentialless context), nothing is posted to the host, so the embed just hangs blank and the host (VS Code extension) can only see "no `ready` within 15s". [GlobalErrorHandler.tsx](frontend/src/components/GlobalErrorHandler.tsx) only handles `API_ERROR_EVENT` toasts; it does not catch `window.onerror`/`unhandledrejection` nor report to the embedding host. **Fixing** (an early inline `window.onerror`+`unhandledrejection` handler — ideally in the root `<head>` so it predates bundle eval — that, when `window !== window.parent`, postMessages `{source:'builderforce-embed/v1', type:'error', message}` to the parent; the host already logs frame `error` messages) unblocks: self-diagnosing embeds + a real error in the VS Code "Copy log" instead of a silent timeout. Owner: T7 (Embed) / T2.
- 🧹 **VS Code embed passes the project deep-link as a URL hash (`#projectId=<id>`) but the embed page reads it as a query (`?project=<id>`)** (2026-06-20). [projectHash()](clients/vscode/src/extension.ts) builds `projectId=${p.id}` and [EmbedPanel](clients/vscode/src/embedPanel.ts) appends it as `#…`, but [embed/[view]/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/embed/[view]/page.tsx) PM surfaces read `?project=<id>` from the query — so opening a board/roadmap from VS Code with a selected project does NOT scope to it (falls back to portfolio/all). **Fixing** (emit `?project=<id>` from the extension, or have the frame also read the hash) unblocks: project-scoped embed views in VS Code. Owner: T2/Extension + T7 (Embed).
- 🧹 **builderforce-memory `/install` requires a local checkout, not portable to work machines** — The Claude Code `/install` skill (`~/.claude/skills/install/`) registers the MCP server by absolute path to a built `builderforce-memory` checkout (default `C:/code/agentic/builderforce-memory`, override via `--home`). `@builderforce/memory-mcp` and `@builderforce/memory` are not published to npm, so on a machine without the repo the install fails. Publishing both (the `memory-mcp` bin is now disk-persistent via `BUILDERFORCE_MEMORY_FILE`, so the published binary is durable) would let the installer use `npx -y @builderforce/memory-mcp` and work anywhere with zero checkout — the main blocker to using this memory at work.
- 🧹 **stdio MCP recall is lexical (Jaccard), not SSM-embedding** — The headless stdio binary does not stand up the SSM runtime/GPU, so cross-session recall uses word-overlap. SSM-embedding recall requires embedding the package in-process and passing `runtime` to `createLocalMemoryStoreBackend` (or a networked builderforce.ai backend). Fixing it upgrades recall quality (and therefore token savings) for the Claude Code integration.
- 🧹 **Internal (test isolation) — `getOrSetCached`'s module-global L1 `Map` is never reset between tests, making cache-backed tests order-dependent.** Surfaced by the CI failure in [cloudMemory.test.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudMemory.test.ts): the `recall clamps the limit` test populated L1 key `am:recall:1:0:5:q` with `[]`, and the later `degrades to {ok:false}` test reused the same tenant/query/limit, getting an L1 hit (`ok:true`) instead of running the failing loader. Fixed in this pass by giving the degrade test an isolated tenant (99) + unique query (cold cache). Durable fix unblocks safe co-location of any future cache-dependent tests: export a `__clearL1CacheForTests()` from [readThroughCache.ts](api/src/infrastructure/cache/readThroughCache.ts) (clears the module-level `l1` Map) and call it in a shared `beforeEach`, so tests don't have to hand-pick collision-free keys. Primary file: `api/src/infrastructure/cache/readThroughCache.ts`.

- **Brain `list_tasks` returns the full untruncated task list (per-task `description` included) in one tool result** (2026-06-16). Surfaced while fixing the archived-backlog bug: the triage for chat #18 shows the `list_tasks` tool result at ~145k chars because [tasksApi.list](frontend/src/lib/builderforceApi.ts) → [GET /api/tasks](api/src/presentation/routes/taskRoutes.ts) returns every task's full body, and the brain action ([platformActions.ts](frontend/src/lib/brain/platformActions.ts) `tasks/list`) feeds it back to the model verbatim. Now that archived tasks are filtered the payload shrinks, but a large active backlog still blows the context window and token budget on a single list call. The same trace was also mis-marked `ERROR` — that is a *separate* false-positive in the triage report's broad `isFailedToolResult` regex (it matches the literal word "error" anywhere in legit data; see the note at [platformActions.ts:101](frontend/src/lib/brain/platformActions.ts#L101)), not a real tool failure. **Fixing** (give the brain `list_tasks` a slim projection — id/key/title/status/priority/archived only, with full bodies fetched on demand via `get`, and tighten the triage error-classifier to inspect the result shape rather than regex-scan the payload) unblocks: cheaper, context-safe backlog reads and accurate run-trace error reporting. Owner: T2 (brain).
- **Service worker `/sw.js` intermittently fails to fetch on update** (2026-06-15). - **Cloudflare vendor moved to the OpenAI-compatible endpoint + one shared body builder + prompt caching on every call** (2026-06-15). The CF coders I added 400'd on tools (`[cloudflare] 400: tools[0].function: Field required`): the old `/ai/run/<model>` path with a hand-rolled `toCloudflareTools` flattener sent `{name,…}`, but the newer FC models (kimi/glm) want the OpenAI-nested `{type:'function',function:{…}}`. Fixed by switching CF to its **OpenAI-compatible** endpoint (`/ai/v1/chat/completions`) via the shared `executeChatCompletion` transport — standard tools in, standard response out, translation deleted. While there: extracted ONE `buildOpenAIChatBody` in `vendors/types.ts` (openrouter/nvidia/cerebras/googleai/cloudflare were five identical copies; Cerebras's `max_completion_tokens` + OpenRouter/Cerebras schema-sanitize ride small opts; Ollama stays native). **Prompt caching is now ON for every call**: `applyPromptCaching` is baked into the shared builder (no-op for non-Anthropic models) AND the direct-Anthropic floor (`anthropic.ts`) now marks `cache_control` on the system block + last tool — so the metered Claude path caches its large stable prefix at ~0.1x instead of full price every turn. All resolved this pass (991 api tests green); no residual.

- **Cloud coding runs 413'd on small-context models + a gateway error wrongly marked the run COMPLETE; context-aware model selection added, but true context COMPACTION is still a gap** (2026-06-15). A 97K-token coding context hit a 32K-window Cloudflare model (`@cf/qwen/qwen3-30b-a3b-fp8`) → HTTP **413** "exceeded this model context window limit", surfaced as a misleading "Gateway 429", and the **container** loop (`api/container/server.mjs`) then ran `finalize` (→ COMPLETED) instead of failing. Fixed: (a) **413 ∈ `CASCADE_STATUSES`** so a context overflow fails over to a bigger-window model (pool ordered big-window-first; a strict pin also drops + cascades on 413); (b) the container loop routes a gateway `turn.error` to the `fail` channel (self-heal/retry), never `finalize` — the in-Worker + durable surfaces already mapped `ok:false`→FAILED; (c) **context-aware first-pass selection** — `VendorModelEntry.contextWindow` (live values), `estimateRequestTokens` + `modelsFittingContext` filter the seed to models whose window fits BEFORE the SSM learned-routing ranks them (small-window models stay in the pool for small tasks, never seeded into an oversized one); (d) gateway errors now name the resolved model + candidate chain ("which model failed"); (e) **context COMPACTION** (`api/src/application/llm/compactMessages.ts`) — both cloud loops compress the conversation BEFORE each paid call when it exceeds a ~40K-token budget: the bulky middle (accumulated read_file/search tool results) is summarized into ONE "builder-memory" note via the free-pool gateway (`buildGatewaySummarizer`, same pattern as `BrainService.summarizeChat`), with lossy elision as the no-LLM fallback. Pinning the system prompt + the task + the recent tail, and the tail-never-starts-on-a-`tool`-message rule, keep tool-call pairing valid. The in-Worker/durable loop mutates `messages` in place (persists into CloudLoopState so the DO doesn't re-summarize the same prefix); the container `llm` op RETURNS `compactedMessages` and `server.mjs` adopts them as its loop state. A `context.compacted` timeline event reports before→after tokens. So a long run no longer re-sends a ballooning history — cheaper, and small/fast CF coders stay viable for longer.
- **Cloud coding runs drained the operator's metered Anthropic key ($10/mo cap hit 100%) — root-caused to the cascade reaching the funded direct-Anthropic floor too eagerly; FIXED in the gateway** (2026-06-15). **RESOLVED — Cloudflare binding + catalog:** `wrangler whoami`/`secret list` confirmed `CLOUDFLARE_AI_API_TOKEN` + `CLAUDE_API_KEY` were bound but **`CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID` was NOT** (a misnamed `CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_API_TOKEN` secret existed instead), so the vendor `apiKeyFrom` returned null and Cloudflare (`PAID_LEAD_VENDOR`, free neurons) was DEAD on every call → all overflow floored to the metered Anthropic key. Operator added `CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID` as a secret (NOT committed — account id kept out of `wrangler.toml` for security). The stale `@cf/meta/llama-3-8b-instruct` (404s) was replaced with the live `@cf/meta/llama-3.1-8b-instruct-fp8`, and 3 live function-calling-verified CF coders were added to the pool (`@cf/zai-org/glm-4.7-flash` 128K, `@cf/moonshotai/kimi-k2.7-code` 256K, `@cf/meta/llama-3.3-70b-instruct-fp8-fast` 24K) so coding overflow burns free neurons before any metered coder. Fixes landed in `api/src/application/llm/**` + `api/src/infrastructure/auth/cooldownStore.ts`: (a) an Anthropic usage-cap **400** (`invalid_request_error` "reached your specified API usage limits") was classified as a fatal caller `request_error` → it short-circuited the cascade with no failover AND wrote no cooldown; now `throwClassified4xx`/`isCapacityLimitBody` map any capacity/credit-balance 4xx to a retryable 429 so it fails over to another provider; (b) coding runs were capped at `FREE_ATTEMPT_BUDGET=2` free coders before escalating to paid/metered coders — now `CODING_FREE_ATTEMPT_BUDGET` (the whole free coding pool, ~9) is walked first so the metered floor is genuine last-resort (10+ models before Claude); (c) a capacity limit now cools the **whole vendor for 60 min** on the first strike (new `capacity` `CooldownClass`) instead of the 5-min transient, so a capped key stands down instead of being re-reached/re-billed every run. (The Cloudflare-binding root cause is RESOLVED — see the entry above.) **Residual:** no per-turn telemetry event fires when a cloud run actually bills the direct-Anthropic floor (`claude-sonnet-4-6`/`claude-opus-4-8`) — the metered-floor hit is observable only via usage rows after the fact; a `metered_floor_used` event on the timeline (sibling of `coding_model_degraded`) would make "we spent on the paid Claude key" loud in real time. Unblocks: provable, real-time cost visibility + an alarm before a spend cap is blown.
- **Cloud agents got first-class git tools (get-latest / undo / redo / status / diff / history) — on-prem only ever had a read-only `git_history` that was never migrated** (2026-06-15). Root cause of the task-78 failures: the container agent worked on a stale branch (branched off an old main, never re-synced) so its build broke against old code and its PR would have reverted ~6.7K lines — and it had no tool to pull the latest. Fixed by adding 6 git verbs to the SHARED registry (`packages/agent-tools/src/core-tools.ts`, canonical command text in `buildGitCommand`), gated to the `shell` capability so they reach the Container + on-prem-shell surfaces but NOT the shell-less durable Worker: `git_status`, `git_diff`, `git_history` (migrates the pi-only on-prem tool), `git_sync_latest` (fetch+merge base → never build on stale code), `git_undo`/`git_redo` (reflog pair, dirty-tree-guarded). Container execution is mirrored in `api/container/server.mjs` (`gitTool`) with the surface-specific twist that it persists via Worker-side GitHub-API commits, so each mutating op first fast-forwards the local clone to the remote head, then operates, then pushes (`--force-with-lease` for undo/redo). Covered by `cloudAgentGitTools.test.ts` (10) incl. injection-safety; full api suite green (952). **Container clone is now a FULL clone** (`server.mjs` — dropped `--depth 1`), so `git_sync_latest`, `git diff main`, and `git merge-base` work reliably (a shallow clone had no merge-base with the base branch); `git_sync_latest` is a plain `git fetch`+merge, no `--unshallow` dance. **The cloud system prompt now instructs the agent to call `git_sync_latest` FIRST** (shell-surface line in `prepareCloudRun`), so a stale branch is synced before any edit instead of relying on the tool description alone. **Remaining residuals:** (1) the shell-less durable Worker surface still has NO git sync — a durable run on a stale branch can't self-update (it commits via API, no shell); a base-merge-over-API path would be needed (the Container surface, which is where multi-step coding runs, is covered). (2) On-prem's shared-registry surface (`NODE_FILE_SURFACE_CAPS`) intentionally omits `shell`, so it surfaces git via its NATIVE bash tools, not the shared git tools — the legacy pi `git-history-tool.ts` can be deleted once the pi loop is retired.
- **Cloudflare Workers AI now LEADS every paid pool, but the catalog is only 3 models — expanding it would "use Cloudflare more"** (2026-06-15). Cloudflare bills in neurons with the first ~10K/day FREE, so paid routing should drain that allowance before any metered vendor. Done in `LlmProxyService.ts`: new `PAID_LEAD_VENDOR='cloudflare'` + shared `leadPoolWithVendor()` floats Cloudflare to the head of `PRO_PAID_MODEL_POOL` (general paid) and `CODING_PREMIUM_FALLBACK_MODELS` (coding paid fallback / backstop); the coding-pool default coder is deliberately left as the strong `claude-sonnet-4.6` (cost-first routing must not regress agentic coding quality — Cloudflare leads only the *fallback*, not the primary default). Residual: the Cloudflare catalog (`vendors/cloudflare.ts`) has just `llama-3-8b`, `gemma-4-26b-a4b-it`, `qwen3-30b-a3b-fp8`; adding more enabled Workers AI checkpoints (e.g. larger Llama / Qwen coders) would stretch the free allowance further across request shapes. Blocked on the operator's list of which Workers AI models are enabled on `CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID` (a model not enabled returns `success:false` and cooldown-cycles). Unblocks: more paid traffic served on the free neuron allowance instead of metered vendors. Also note: general PRO paid traffic now tries Cloudflare's small general models (8B/26B) first after the free pool — acceptable per the cost directive and adaptively corrected by PRD-13 learned routing (`rankModelsForAction`), but a quality-sensitive Pro tenant may prefer a per-tenant opt-out toggle (not built).
- **On-prem coding-execution repo-prep is now a modular `RepoSyncStrategy` port + skills declare skill-to-skill deps; two follow-ups remain** (2026-06-16). The hard-coded "is this the latest code from the repo?" clone/checkout was duplicated inline in the swimlane dispatch loop ([builderforce-coding-dispatch.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-coding-dispatch.ts)) and the V2 ticket workspace ([builderforce-relay.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/builderforce-relay.ts) `ensureTaskWorkspace`). Extracted into one injected [repo-sync.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/repo-sync.ts) `RepoSyncStrategy` (clone-if-missing → WIP-safe refresh-to-latest on reuse → branch mode `new-branch` vs idempotent `ticket-branch`), fixing the latent stale-reuse bug (the ticket workspace previously never re-synced) while preserving accumulated uncommitted WIP. Skills gained a `requires.skills` dependency ([dependencies.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/skills/dependencies.ts), enforced in `filterSkillEntries`): `coding-agent` now depends on `github`, which is auto-included when active and disables `coding-agent` if `gh` is absent. **Residuals:** (1) `builderforce skills check`/status ([skills-status.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/skills-status.ts)) and the install flow ([skills-install.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/skills-install.ts)) do NOT yet surface a skill-dependency unmet reason ("coding-agent disabled: requires github → gh missing") nor auto-install a depended-on skill — the dependency is enforced only for prompt inclusion. (2) This `RepoSyncStrategy` covers the on-prem agent-runtime paths only; the **cloud** durable Worker surface still has no git sync (see the cloud git-tools entry above) — unifying both behind one sync contract is the larger play. Fixing (1) unblocks honest skill diagnostics + one-shot dependency installs; (2) unblocks a single repo-prep policy across on-prem and cloud. Owner: T5 (on-prem runtime).
- **Psychometric persona personality (Pro) shipped, but tenant "My Personas" are localStorage-only so their trait vectors never reach execution** (2026-06-16). New end-to-end personality feature: a persona can carry a `PsychometricProfile` (full framework suite — HEXACO / regulatory-focus / need-for-cognition / decision-style / moral-foundations / Thomas-Kilmann / Schwartz / Enneagram / dispositional) deterministically compiled into BOTH system-prompt directives AND execution levers (think-depth floor, reasoning-on, temperature) by [psychometrics.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/psychometrics.ts) and injected at run time via [buildPersonaSystemBlock](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/personas.ts) + [resolveActivePsychometricParams](agent-runtime/src/agents/assigned-capabilities.ts) in [attempt.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/embedded-runner/run/attempt.ts). The LIVE path is `platform_personas` (migration `0199` + [adminRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/adminRoutes.ts) → agent-host sync → [registerPlatformPersonasAsRoles](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/agent-roles.ts)). The editor ([PsychometricEditor.tsx](frontend/src/components/PsychometricEditor.tsx) — sliders/questionnaire/import) is wired into the tenant persona modal ([personas/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/personas/page.tsx)) and Pro-gated via [PlanLimits.psychometricPersona](api/src/domain/tenant/PlanLimits.ts) + [personaRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/personaRoutes.ts). **Gap:** tenant "My Personas" persist to `localStorage`, not the DB, so a profile a tenant authors there is never synced to an agent host and never executes — only admin-managed platform personas do. **Fixing** (server-back tenant personas in a `tenant_personas` table + sync them down the assignment path the way `platform_personas` flow) unblocks self-serve Pro personality that actually changes how a tenant's agents think. Owner: T1/T2.
- **V2 cloud agents apply psychometric prompt directives but NOT the execution-param half** (2026-06-16). Directives flow into the V2 SDK path via [buildAssignedCapabilityAppend](agent-runtime/src/agents/assigned-capabilities.ts), so a cloud agent reads its personality, but the think-depth/reasoning/temperature overrides from `resolveActivePsychometricParams` are merged only in the embedded (on-prem) runner ([attempt.ts](agent-runtime/src/agents/embedded-runner/run/attempt.ts)); the Claude-Agent-SDK cloud loop manages its own params and ignores them. **Fixing** (thread the merged `PsychometricExecParams` into the V2 cloud run's model/think config) unblocks behavioural personality parity (not just textual) on cloud agents. Owner: T3.
- **Psychometric dimension-id contract is duplicated across packages + admin UI lacks the editor** (2026-06-16). The canonical dimension ids live in `DIM` in BOTH [agent-runtime psychometrics.ts](agent-runtime/src/builderforce/psychometrics.ts) (compiler) and [api psychometricCatalog.ts](api/src/application/persona/psychometricCatalog.ts) (catalog+scoring), hand-synced because the packages share no module — a renamed id on one side would silently drop that dimension. **Fixing** (extract a shared `@builderforce/psychometric-contract` exporting the id constants) unblocks single-source-of-truth safety. Also: the **admin** Personas tab doesn't yet expose `PsychometricEditor` (only the tenant modal does), though admin POST/PATCH already persist the `psychometric` column — so admin platform personas currently need the profile set via API. Owner: T9.

- **Direct-Anthropic coding floor is non-streaming only (`anthropic` vendor has no `callStream`)** (2026-06-14). Added `api/src/application/llm/vendors/anthropic.ts` — a direct `api.anthropic.com/v1/messages` vendor on `CLAUDE_API_KEY` (`claude-sonnet-4-6` → `claude-opus-4-8`), wired as the last-resort tail of `CODING_PREMIUM_FALLBACK_MODELS` so the coding cascade falls back to Claude when every OpenRouter-routed paid coder is down. It implements `call` (non-streaming, with a full OpenAI↔Anthropic-Messages translation) but **not** `callStream`, because the only path that reaches it — the cloud coding tool loop — is non-streaming, so `dispatchVendorStream` cleanly skips it. Residual: a future *streaming* coding/chat request that exhausts into the coding fallback would skip the Anthropic floor (and could surface `cascade_exhausted` where a non-streaming request would have been rescued). Unblocks: streaming reliability-floor parity — implement `callStream` translating Anthropic SSE (`message_start`/`content_block_*`/`message_delta`) → OpenAI chat SSE chunks (incl. `tool_use` → `tool_calls` `input_json_delta` accumulation).

- **Superseded (now resolved) — Learned model routing design notes.** (2026-06-14). Every cloud run's **resolved model** is already captured per task/project (`recordCloudUsage` → `llm_usage_log.model` + attribution `{cloudAgentRef, executionId, taskId, projectId}`; plus `model.select`/`coding_model_degraded` timeline events) — so the "which model ran" substrate exists. Missing is the learned-routing loop the operator wants: (1) **action-type labels** — classify each task into an action type (`sql`, `frontend`, `refactor`, `bugfix`, …) so runs group by type; proposed first step is a cheap **first-pass FREE-model classifier** that tags the task before the run (decision: add a per-run classifier call? store the label where — a `task_action_type` column / a `run_labels` table?). (2) **outcome signal** — define "worked best" (PR merged? green CI? human approval? steps-to-done? token cost?) and join it to `(action_type, model)` so analytics can rank models per type ("Google/Gemini best at SQL"). (3) **routing** — feed the ranking back into selection (extend `pickCloudModel`/`codingModelsForPlan` with an action-type→model preference), with **SSM/Samba memory** (MambaKit/SSMjs hippocampus — see the SSM Hippocampus loop) as the per-codebase recall layer that learns which models work best for THIS repo over time. Design-level subsystem spanning api + SSMjs/MambaKit; **not** built this pass to avoid a dead/half-wired routing seam. Blockers needing an explicit decision: the "best" outcome metric, whether to add a first-pass classifier call on every run (cost), and the SSM integration surface. Unblocks: task-aware model routing + per-codebase learned model preferences.

- **A failing PR-branch build is surfaced on the Pull Request tab, but not yet as a ticket/execution-chip badge** (2026-06-14). The build status + reason now persist on the PR row and render in `PullRequestPanel` (the ticket's "Pull Request" tab) and the run's Logs/Timeline. What's missing is a higher-altitude signal: the execution chip (`#64 · cancelled`) and the task card don't show a "build failing" badge, so a buyer scanning the executions list still can't tell at a glance that a "completed" run shipped a red build. Deferred: derive a `buildStatus` badge on `AgentExecutionPanel`'s execution chips + the task card from the linked PR row (the data is already there via `getTaskPullRequest`). Unblocks: red-build visibility without opening the PR tab.

- **Task-PRD content — fence-wrap normalized at the render path + on new writes; only the historical backfill remains.** LLM-drafted PRDs sometimes arrive wrapped in a whole-document ` ```markdown ` fence, which `ChatMessageContent` rendered as one raw "MARKDOWN" code box in the task-details PRD tab instead of formatted prose. Closed two ways: (1) **render-time** — `TaskPrdTab` now runs `unwrapMarkdownFence` (the generalized ex-`unwrapLegalMarkdown` util) and adds a `Preview | RAW` `ViewToggle` (panel + fullscreen), so existing rows display correctly; (2) **on WRITE** — `draftTaskPrd` (`api/.../prd/taskPrd.ts`) strips the fence via new `stripPrdMarkdownFence` before persisting, so freshly generated PRDs are stored clean for every consumer (render/export/repo-commit/Copy). **Residual (operator):** a one-off backfill of `specs.prd` rows persisted before this change — until then the render-time unwrap stays the safety net (can't be retired). No code change available for the backfill without live-DB access. Mirrors the legal-doc normalization gap above.

- **Container hard-death (`onError`) self-heal can't push a LIVE WebSocket event** (2026-06-14). `AgentContainerDO.onError` runs in the container DO's isolate, where the per-run WS subscriber map and the `executionBoardSink` (SESSION_ROOM fan-out) are not registered (they're wired per request isolate). So when a container crash self-heals or fails via `handleCloudRunCrash`, the failure/requeue is persisted + lands a `run.failed`/`runtime.crash` timeline row, but live subscribers only see it on the next read-path reconciliation poll (a few seconds), not instantly — same latency as today's orphan reaps. The container `fail` op path (in the Worker request isolate) DOES push live. Deferred: have `handleCloudRunCrash` emit through a cross-isolate notifier (e.g. always via the SESSION_ROOM DO) so a DO-isolate crash pushes instantly too. Unblocks: real-time crash surfacing regardless of which isolate detected it.
- **Lane agent's host `target` is not threaded into the dispatcher** (2026-06-14). `decideLaneAutoRun` returns the lane agent's `agentRef` + `model`; the dispatcher (`startDispatchedExecution`) resolves the on-prem host from a pin on the *task* (`tasks.assignedAgentHostId`). A swimlane agent that pins its own host `target` (a specific on-prem machine) does not yet propagate that into the run, so a lane can't direct its run to a particular machine — host delivery only happens when the task itself is host-pinned. Unblocks: per-lane choice of which on-prem machine runs the stage. (The V2-on-host engine gate is now removed — host delivery is no longer gated on engine; the on-prem host runtime runs the V2 Agent natively, and the run carries the agent's own model.)
- **Auto-run execution CREATION is not pushed over the project socket — only poll-surfaced** (2026-06-15). The board/cards/lanes update live via `broadcastProjectChanged` (SESSION_ROOM) on task writes, and the lane drag itself pushes. But when the autonomous trigger submits the auto-run, neither `runtimeService.submit` nor `startDispatchedExecution` broadcasts to the project room — only `notifyExecutionSubscribers` (the per-execution stream). So the freshly-queued run CHIP (e.g. "Bob · pending") surfaces on the board's `useBoardLiveRuns` poll tick, not instantly over WS, despite the run-feed comment treating WS as primary and the poll as a dropped-socket backstop. Distinct from the container-crash WS gap above (that's failure surfacing; this is creation surfacing). Deferred: emit a `broadcastProjectChanged` (or a dedicated run-created event) at dispatch so the chip appears the instant the agent is queued. Unblocks: instant "agent picked it up" feedback on drag without waiting for the reconcile poll.
- **`ide_agents.engine` column + V1 engine values are vestigial post-V1-deletion** (2026-06-14). V1 is deleted in the cloud AND on the on-prem host (the agent-runtime engine registry's sole runner is `builderforce-v2`; any legacy `engine` value falls back to v2). The API dispatch path no longer branches on engine (the `!isV2` gate and the `cloudAgentTypeLabel` V1 branch are gone). The `ide_agents.engine` column is now effectively constant and any rows still holding `'builderforce-v1'` are inert (resolve/behave as v2). Deferred: a migration to normalize/drop the `engine` column. The engine *registry* DI seam is INTENTIONALLY kept (a future V3 registers the same way). Unblocks: schema/code clarity once the column is retired.
- **Autonomous lane runs bypass the execution governance approval gate** (2026-06-14). The manual `/api/runtime/executions` route runs `evaluateExecutionApprovalGate` (governance approval rules — currently gates high/urgent priority tasks) before dispatch; the autonomous lane trigger (via `dispatchCloudRunForTask`) skips it. The lane's own `gate: 'human'` provides board-level human-in-the-loop, but tenant governance approval *rules* are not enforced on autonomously-triggered runs. NOT auto-bundled: applying it would make a high-priority task's autonomous run create an approval instead of running, a product decision (`evaluateExecutionApprovalGate` is currently route-private in `runtimeRoutes.ts` — extract + share when adopted). Unblocks: consistent policy enforcement — every agent run (manual or autonomous) honors the same approval rules.
- **Capability guardrail only enforces an explicitly-configured `required_capabilities`; there is no capability-aware *router*** (2026-06-14). `decideLaneAutoRun` now skips a lane agent whose resolved skills/personas don't cover the lane assignment's `required_capabilities` (`api/src/application/swimlane/laneAutoRun.ts` + the resolve+warn wiring in `taskRoutes.ts:maybeAutoRunOnLaneEntry`), which closes the "BA/PM/PO agent silently runs a coding task" hole **when a lane sets the field**. A lane with no `required_capabilities` configured still runs whatever agent is pinned (the exec #61 lane had none set). Deferred: (a) a real router that *scores* a task's inferred type (coding/docs/review) against each workforce agent's persona/skills and picks the best match rather than the first qualifying one (the AskUserQuestion "full capability-aware router" option), and (b) a sensible default requirement (e.g. infer `coding-agent` for a lane whose template writes code) so the guardrail protects un-configured lanes too. Unblocks: correct-by-default staffing without per-lane manual config.
- **`capability_mismatch` has no pre-execution timeline channel** (2026-06-14). When the guardrail skips a mis-staffed agent it emits a `console.warn` (Worker telemetry sink) only — there is no `execution_id` yet (we are *refusing* to start a run), so it can't ride the existing `recordCloudToolEvent` → Observability timeline path. The mismatch is therefore diagnosable in logs but invisible on the board/timeline. Deferred: a lightweight pre-execution audit channel (e.g. a per-task `auto_run_skipped` audit event) surfaced on the task card so a lane that silently won't auto-run explains itself in-product. Unblocks: operators see *why* a ticket dropped into an auto lane didn't start.
- **`capabilities.load` telemetry conflates agent-pinned vs inherited artifacts** (2026-06-14). The cloud run resolves capabilities via `resolveArtifacts({tenantId, taskId, cloudAgentRef})` — a UNION across tenant + project + task + agent scopes — and the `capabilities.load` timeline event reports that union. So an agent whose own (`scope='agent'`) config is empty still shows personas/skills assigned tenant- or project-wide (this is why exec #61's "Kevin BA/PM/PO" appeared to have `code-creator`/`documentation-agent` it was never directly assigned). The new /workforce **Agent manifest** (`api/src/application/artifact/agentManifest.ts`) deliberately shows the agent-scoped set ONLY, which is the honest "what is pinned to THIS agent" view. Deferred: make `capabilities.load` label each artifact with its source scope (agent vs project vs tenant) so the timeline distinguishes pinned from inherited — and reconsider whether tenant-wide persona assignments should silently apply to every agent at all. Unblocks: an operator can tell, from telemetry alone, what an agent itself carries vs what it merely inherited.
- **Moving a task across boards does not re-point `tasks.segment_id` to the target project's segment** (2026-06-14). `TaskService.moveTask` (now collision-safe re-keying) updates `project_id` + `key` but leaves `segment_id` pointing at the *source* project's segment. The `set_default_segment_id_via_project` trigger only fires `BEFORE INSERT`, and `segment_id` isn't modeled in the `Task` domain entity or written by `TaskRepository.update`, so a moved row keeps its old segment. Harmless for `single`-mode tenants (one shared default segment, so source and target segments are identical), but for a `segmented` tenant whose source/target projects live in different segments this leaves the task's segment stale — a data-isolation drift. Deferred (T7 — segment/isolation): on move, resolve the target project's `segment_id` and update the task to match (or add an `AFTER UPDATE OF project_id` trigger that re-derives it). Unblocks: correct per-segment attribution/erasure (DSR/GDPR cascade) for tasks that change boards in a segmented tenant.
- **A vendor-specific 400 inside the coding cascade can still suppress the paid coding backstop** (2026-06-14). `LlmProxyService.complete()` treats a primary cascade that ends in `outcome === 'request_error'` (every candidate returned 400/422) as "the caller's payload is malformed" and **skips** the guaranteed backstop (so it surfaces the schema diagnostic instead of double-billing a doomed retry). That assumption is wrong when the 400 is *vendor-specific* (e.g. Ollama's `"Value looks like object…"` on a tools payload that Anthropic/DeepSeek accept). The exec #61 trigger is now removed two ways — Ollama is excluded from auto-routed pools and cloud coding runs cascade only within the curated coding pool (`codingOnly`), so a request-error finish is now unlikely — but the short-circuit itself is unchanged. Deferred: fire the *coding* backstop (`CODING_BACKSTOP_MODELS`, a paid coder) even on `request_error`, since a paid coder is the most likely to accept a payload that quirky free vendors rejected. Unblocks: "a coding run always falls over to a paid coder" holds even in the all-400 edge.
- **`PATCH /api/approvals/:id` does not enforce the MANAGER+ role its own contract claims** (2026-06-14). The route's doc header says "tenant JWT, MANAGER+", but the handler (`approvalRoutes.ts`) only runs `authMiddleware` — any authenticated tenant user can approve/reject/answer a request, including the new `task.execution` execution-approval gate (which, as of this pass, now *auto-starts the run* on approve via `dispatchCloudRunForTask`). So a non-manager can both clear the governance gate and trigger the (billable) run. Surfaced while wiring the inline `ApprovalResolveControl`; not fixed here because role-gating writes is a deliberate access-control change (need the canonical role check helper + a decision on which roles may approve which `actionType`s). Deferred (T7 — governance): enforce role on the PATCH (and ideally scope by action type / approval rule). Unblocks: the execution-approval gate is real authorization, not an honor-system label. Note the inline approve UI already degrades safely — a forbidden PATCH surfaces its error in the control — so the only missing piece is the server-side role check.

### 💰 Open — Direct revenue / monetization (15)

_Billing, plan tiers (Free/Pro), marketplace purchase/payout, pricing & entitlement gates, metering, cost attribution._

- **Per-user sub-ledger from `metadata.userId` is not implemented.** The gateway debits the tenant's daily plan budget; if the SDK's `metadata.userId` is set, the gateway could maintain a per-user sub-ledger and enforce per-user caps. Tenant apps continue to enforce per-user budgets locally. Needs a product decision (per-user cap UX in the portal) plus a `tenant_user_token_caps` table and a query in the chat route. Fixing unblocks deletion of tenant-side `tokenLedger.charge` plumbing.

- **Cost attribution (ticket → project → workspace → account) covers only the cloud-agent execution loop — web/SDK and on-prem host spend isn't attributed.** Cost now stamps the full rollup chain on `llm_usage_log`: `task_id` (ticket, the finest grain — migration 0104), `project_id` (0103), and `tenant_id` (account). **Workspace (segment) is intentionally NOT a column here** — 0056 keeps `llm_usage_log` tenant-level (platform/infra ledger; its segment trigger RAISEs for segmented tenants), so workspace-level cost is derived by joining `project → segment` (projects.segment_id), not denormalized. Stamped from the run's task in [recordCloudUsage](api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts); surfaced as ticket spend on the execution panel (`GET /tasks/:id/cost`) and the "By Project" card ([LlmUsageContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/LlmUsageContent.tsx)) rolling up to the account total. STILL UNATTRIBUTED (task_id/project_id null → account-level only): (a) gateway chat/image calls via `logUsage` ([llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts)) — no ticket/project context on a raw LLM call; (b) self-hosted **on-prem host** runs, which meter via the gateway path not `recordCloudUsage`, so a host executing a ticket records cost with no task/project; (c) the future CloudRunnerDO must pass `taskId`+`projectId` to `recordCloudUsage` or its spend regresses to unattributed. Also missing: a **workspace (segment) rollup** surface (the join exists; no endpoint/card yet) and a **project-page** spend widget (only the execution panel + LLM-usage dashboard show it).
