- **ID-type collision: spec uses `uuid String` PKs + a fresh `Tenant` model; platform `tenants.id`/`projects.id`/`tenant_members` are integer `serial`.** ([schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)). Two `tenants` tables can't coexist. Fixing (fold the spec's `Tenant` fields — `kind`, `idpIssuer`, `slug`, `settings` — into the existing `tenants` table as added columns; add `segments(tenant_id integer FK)`; new PM/Agile tables carry `tenant_id integer` + `segment_id uuid` and may be uuid internally) unblocks: the spec's domain model landing on the real tenant root instead of a parallel one.

- **No CI-level e2e covers the studio's actual in-browser ONNX execution — nine invariants are unit-tested, the rest needs a real GPU browser.** Nine layers locked by unit tests in [studio/src/engine/](studio/src/engine/): (1) ORT WASM/JS version match; (2) per-model UNet input names; (3) per-input dtypes (LCM `timestep`=float32, SD-Turbo=int64); (4) `reportProgress` fans out (silent-hang UX); (5) `buildOrtSessionOptions` pins `graphOptimizationLevel: 'basic'`; (6) `checkMemoryForModel` reports when probed memory < minimum (inert for WebGPU — `null` is honest); (7) `explainOrtError` translates std::bad_alloc, graph-fusion AND `DXGI_ERROR_DEVICE_HUNG` / `Device is lost` (Windows TDR) into actionable diagnostics; (8) `lighterModelHint` never suggests the failing model, and only suggests models that fit available memory; (9) `runSession` wrapper routes every `session.run` through the same translator (catches device-loss at runtime, not just at session create). Plus init-time `assertSessionMatchesSpec` + a `device.lost`-promise listener that emits a clear progress message when the GPU device is reset. Still needing a real WebGPU browser: (a) UNet output name (we pick first Float32); (b) `timestep_cond` embedding values match LCM training; (c) CLIP-L pad-id holds for SD-Turbo; (d) actual VRAM fit; (e) progress timeline end-to-end. Need a Playwright job on a GPU runner.

- **WebGPU doesn't expose actual VRAM — `approxMemoryMb` is `null` for the WebGPU device path, so the pre-flight memory check is effectively inert there.** [studio/src/engine/device-router.ts](studio/src/engine/device-router.ts) previously derived "memory" from `adapter.limits.maxBufferSize`, which is a SPEC LIMIT (2 GB default) — not memory. That falsely blocked 16GB GPUs as "insufficient." Honest fix in this pass: return `null`. The post-hoc `explainSessionCreateError` still translates a real `std::bad_alloc` into an actionable message, so the OOM case is still well-handled — just at the failure point, not predictively. A real predictive check would need a tiny calibration probe (allocate progressively larger GPUBuffers until one fails) at engine init — non-trivial and out of scope for this pass. Fixing (add the calibration probe behind a `prepFlight` option) unblocks: honest pre-download "you don't have enough" rather than a 5-minute download → OOM cycle.

- **Real-time collaboration WS is opt-in via `NEXT_PUBLIC_COLLAB_WS_URL` — no default, no spam, but also no collab in stacks without the worker.** [frontend/src/hooks/useCollaboration.ts](frontend/src/hooks/useCollaboration.ts) used to fall back to `${NEXT_PUBLIC_WORKER_URL}/api/collab` → `localhost:8787` (the api worker, no collab route) → infinite reconnect loop spamming the console. Hook now returns inert refs when the env var isn't set and logs once. Cost: developers who *do* want collab in dev must (a) deploy the `worker/` package's `CollaborationRoom` Durable Object, and (b) set `NEXT_PUBLIC_COLLAB_WS_URL=ws://localhost:PORT/api/collab`. Fixing (document the env var in [README.md Quick Start](README.md), add to `docker-compose.yml`, or wire a sensible default once the collab worker ships in dev compose) unblocks: collab works out of the box.

- **Two studio packages need (re)publishing + npm auth setup: engine `@seanhogg/builderforce-studio@0.2.0` (breaking — React layer removed) and the brand-new `@seanhogg/builderforce-studio-embedded@0.1.0`.** The engine was split: `0.1.x` carried `StudioPanel`; `0.2.0` is engine-only and the React layer moved to the new `-embedded` package. Both are built locally but unpublished — the publishing environment's `~/.npmrc` token is dead (a `404 PUT` on publish), so they need either a fresh `NPM_TOKEN` repo secret or OIDC trusted publishers. Operator steps: (1) Publish `@seanhogg/builderforce-studio@0.2.0` (`cd studio && npm publish --access public` from a logged-in machine, or set `NPM_TOKEN` and push to main — the `publish-studio` workflow handles it). (2) Publish `@seanhogg/builderforce-studio-embedded@0.1.0` likewise; the `publish-studio-embedded` CI job (`needs: publish-studio`) is wired in [release.yml](.github/workflows/release.yml). (3) For zero-secret CI thereafter, add trusted publishers at `https://www.npmjs.com/package/<name>/access` for each. Until (1)+(2), external `npm install @seanhogg/builderforce-studio` still resolves the old `0.1.x` (with the now-removed React exports) — the in-app IDE is unaffected since it consumes both via local `link:`.

- **`docker compose up` requires `NEON_DATABASE_URL` in `api/.dev.vars` — the stack cannot bundle Postgres because the api uses `@neondatabase/serverless` HTTP transport.** [api/src/infrastructure/database/connection.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/connection.ts) calls `neon(url)` which speaks Neon's HTTP `/sql` endpoint, not raw PG protocol. A bundled `postgres:16` service won't accept Neon HTTP queries; bridging requires a community proxy like `ghcr.io/timowilhelm/local-neon-http-proxy` plus a runtime `neonConfig` override to point the driver at it. Out of scope for v0 docker (free Neon signup is 30 seconds and gives the same shape as production). Fixing (add the proxy service + `neonConfig.fetchEndpoint` override gated on a `LOCAL_NEON=1` env var) unblocks: truly zero-prereq `docker compose up`, contributor onboarding without a Neon account.

- **README references `@seanhogg/ssmjs` as an installed dependency in two places, but it is not in `frontend/package.json`.** [README.md "AI Training Studio" bullet at line 35](README.md) claims `uses @seanhogg/ssmjs / Transformers.js with WebGPU` and the [On-Device AI Stack diagram at line 359-377](README.md) shows `SSM.js (@seanhogg/ssmjs)` as a layer over `mambacode.js`. [frontend/package.json](frontend/package.json) only ships `mambacode.js: github:SeanHogg/Mamba` and `@huggingface/transformers ^3.8.1` — the actual integration is `MambaModelProvider` in [frontend/src/lib/model-provider.ts](frontend/src/lib/model-provider.ts) and the in-tree [mamba-engine.ts](frontend/src/lib/mamba-engine.ts). The `ssmjs` and `mambakit` references are aspirational. Fixing (either publish `@seanhogg/ssmjs` and `add` it, or rewrite both README sections to reflect that `MambaModelProvider` + `mamba-engine.ts` is the actual orchestration layer) unblocks: documentation matches shipped code, prevents new contributors chasing imports that don't exist.

- **`0063_agentic_qa.sql` is authored but not applied to any live DB.** Drift check passes and types compile, but `npm run db:migrate` was not run (headless env, no DB connection). Until applied, every `/api/qa/*` route 500s with "relation does not exist." Fixing (run `npm run db:migrate` against each environment's Neon DB) unblocks: the QA endpoints actually working in prod. Mirrors the existing `0055_tenant_mcp_extensions` entry.

- **The whole QA pipeline was verified by typecheck + schema-drift only — never run end-to-end.** No live DB, no deployed app, and no Playwright browser in this env, so capture → aggregate → generate → run → report has not been exercised once. The generator's LLM-output parsing, the storageState auth injection (localStorage + cookie key names `bf_web_token`/`bf_tenant_token` were taken from a code read, not a live login), and the Playwright JSON→`/api/qa/runs` mapping in [qa-e2e/src/report.ts](qa-e2e/src/report.ts) are all unproven against real shapes. Fixing (seed a QA tenant, run `qa-e2e` against a preview deploy, confirm a green run lands in Observability ▸ Agentic QA) unblocks: confidence the pipeline works, not just compiles.

- **None of the per-project suite has been run end-to-end.** Typecheck (api + frontend + qa-e2e) + schema-drift pass, but migration 0068 isn't applied to any DB, the encryption round-trip / persona form-login / runner-bundle flow have never executed, and the storageState-injection + per-spec `test.use` path is unproven against a real Playwright run. Fixing (apply 0068, configure a project with a target + persona, run `BF_PROJECT_ID=… npm run ci` against a real site) unblocks: confidence the suite works, not just compiles.

- **Migration 0069 has not been applied to any DB and the calendar/library flows have never run end-to-end.** Typecheck (api + frontend) and schema-drift pass, but no DB has the new columns/tables, so the activity-calendar query, agent sync, and prompt publish/use/star paths are unproven against live data. Fixing (apply 0069, sync agents on a tenant with active claws + ingested git activity, publish and use a public prompt) unblocks: confidence the features work, not just compile.

- **Migration 0072 has not been applied to any DB; the pipeline has never run end-to-end against live data.** Type-check (api + frontend), schema-drift, and unit tests pass, but no DB has the `repo_analysis_*` tables and no real repo has been analyzed, so the DO alarm progression (`fetching → analyzing:* → writing_back → completed`), the provider API calls against real GitHub/Bitbucket/GitLab, the project-details write-back, and the `project_memories` seed are unproven live. The `ANALYSIS_RUNNER` DO migration tag `v3` in [wrangler.toml](api/wrangler.toml) is also unapplied. Fixing (apply 0072 + 0099 + `wrangler deploy` to register the DO, map a repo with a stored credential, run an analysis on a Pro and a Free tenant) unblocks: confidence the feature works, not just compiles.

- **Migration 0074 is authored but not applied to any live DB.** `integration_credentials.project_id` + the `gitlab` enum value exist in [schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts) + [0074_integration_project_scope.sql](api/migrations/0074_integration_project_scope.sql) and `check:schema` passes, but no `npm run db:migrate` ran (headless env). Until applied, project-scoped key creation and GitLab credentials 500 at runtime. Fixing (run `db:migrate` per environment) unblocks: the feature working in prod. Same caveat as the 0070/0071/0072 entries.

- **Yjs collab seeding can double-insert if the websocket sync lands after the local seed.** [CodeEditor.tsx](frontend/src/components/CodeEditor.tsx) now seeds an empty `ydoc.getText(filePath)` from the persisted file content on (re)bind so the binding never blanks a file. When `NEXT_PUBLIC_COLLAB_WS_URL` is set, the y-websocket provider may sync authoritative remote content *after* this local seed, producing duplicated text. Inert today (collab is opt-in and unset in prod). Fixing (gate the seed on `provider.synced`/`once('sync')`, or only seed when the room is known-empty) unblocks: safe content seeding once real-time collaboration is enabled.

- **Migration 0075 is authored but not applied to any live DB.** `ide_agents` gains nullable `project_id` + `tenant_id`/pricing/runtime/`published` columns and the `gitlab`-style additions, but no `npm run db:migrate` ran (headless env). Until applied, `POST /api/workforce/agents` + `/mine` 500 with "column does not exist". Fixing (run `db:migrate` per environment) unblocks: cloud-agent create/publish working in prod. Same caveat as 0070–0074.

- **Blocked — external ops that need credentials/access this environment does not have:**
  (1) **npm: `npm deprecate @seanhogg/coderclaw` (exists @ 2026.3.21) + publish
  `@seanhogg/builderforce-agents` (404, unpublished)** — BLOCKED: `npm whoami` returns **401**, no
  valid publish token here. The package now builds, so this is a one-command release once
  authenticated. (2) **`coderclaw.ai`→`builderforce.ai` DNS/301** + the install-script endpoint +
  Discord handle — need registrar/Cloudflare DNS access (app-level `_redirects` + Astro redirects
  are already in place). (3) The generated `docs-site/src/assets/install-script.svg` + the
  `credits.md` "CLAW + TARDIS" easter-egg still say "claw" — cosmetic, regenerate/reword when the
  mascot decision lands.

- **Migration `0100_human_request_kinds.sql` not yet applied to any live DB.** This pass generalized `approvals` into human-in-the-loop *requests* (the agent's `ask_human` bubble channel): added `kind` (`approval`/`question`/`feedback`), `response_text`, an `'answered'` value on the `approval_status` enum, and two `(tenant_id, …)` indexes ([schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts)). The migration is additive + idempotent (`ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS`, `ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS`) but, per project convention, was NOT auto-run against the operator's Neon DB. Note the `ALTER TYPE … ADD VALUE` runs as its own statement in the HTTP migration runner ([migrate.mjs](api/scripts/migrate.mjs)) — fine on PG12+ outside a txn. Until it's applied (`npm --prefix api run db:migrate`), the API's insert/update of `kind`/`response_text` will fail against the old shape and the Approvals & Q&A tab plus the `ask_human` tool can't persist. Running it unblocks: the whole question/feedback escalation feature going live.

- **IDE reference panel SHIPPED — `/ide/voice` Voice Studio validates the full UX end-to-end, on-device AND server.** New page ([ide/voice/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/ide/voice/page.tsx)) + [VoiceClonePanel.tsx](frontend/src/components/VoiceClonePanel.tsx) + api client ([voiceClones.ts](frontend/src/lib/voiceClones.ts)) + sidebar nav entry: create a clone (name + **file OR mic capture** + required consent), list voices, synthesize text, play audio with live word-highlighting, and an honest "Cloning unavailable — <reason>" banner (PRD §7). Frontend type-checks 0 errors. **On-device gap CLOSED:** the panel now prefers the FREE on-device WebGPU path — [captureAudio.ts](frontend/src/lib/captureAudio.ts) (`decodeAudioData` file→PCM + `MicRecorder`) feeds the studio `VoiceCloneEngine` to enrol a speaker embedding client-side, and synthesis routes through the package's own `VoiceClient.narrate` seam ([voiceEngine.ts](frontend/src/lib/voiceEngine.ts)) — on-device when an embedding is held, else the metered server — so the IDE dogfoods the exact contract hired.video consumes (DRY: no bespoke frontend resolver). The studio engine is dynamic-imported (lazy, client-only) so it degrades to server if absent/no-WebGPU; an engine badge surfaces which path is live. `@seanhogg/builderforce-voice` added as a frontend link dep. Superseded `voiceClones.synthesizeVoice`/`fetchVoiceoverObjectUrl`/`SynthesisUnavailable`/`listMarketplaceVoices` were deleted (zero refs). **Residuals:** (1) on-device embeddings persist in `localStorage` only (per-device, not synced — the server's no-leak contract means a new device must re-enrol or use the server path); (2) no in-IDE marketplace **browse** UI yet (the catalog route exists but buy/checkout backend doesn't — see voice residual #2 above).
- **`awaiting_workflow` parked tickets have no park-age timeout (T8 residual, 2026-06-14).** A ticket parked on a spawned `run_workflow` (migration 0171) waits indefinitely for the workflow to settle; if that workflow is dropped or never reports, the ticket is stuck in `awaiting_workflow` with no fallback (`resumeParkedWorkflows` only acts on a settle signal). Fixing (a park-age timeout that routes a stale parked ticket to `needs_attention`) unblocks: no permanently-stuck lane tickets.

- **Historical migration-prefix collisions are grandfathered, not renumbered (T9 residual, 2026-06-14).** `.migration-collisions-allowlist.txt` whitelists 8 long-applied duplicate prefixes (0009/0014/0018/0060/0064/0068/0075/0076) because renumbering applied migrations is a release-level ledger op. Fixing (a coordinated renumber + `_migrations` ledger update + redeploy) unblocks: a fully collision-free history with an empty allowlist.

- **No empty-DB `db:migrate` dry-run in CI — Neon-infra blocked (T9 residual, 2026-06-14).** `check-migrations.mjs` fails CI on duplicate prefixes, but nothing applies the full migration set to an ephemeral DB pre-deploy, so a missing-`CREATE`/ordering bug still surfaces only in prod. Blocked on a CI-provisioned ephemeral Neon/Postgres. Fixing unblocks: schema drift caught at PR time, not prod.

- **Isolation-Tracks README table and `.github/isolation-tracks.json` are hand-maintained — drift risk (T9 residual, 2026-06-14).** The `check-track-scope` guard reads the JSON manifest while the README renders the human table; the two can diverge. Fixing (a generator that renders the README table FROM the manifest in CI) unblocks: a single source of truth for track ownership (DRY).

### 📓 Archived thematic context (shipped subsystems — verbatim)

Roadmap entries that remain after this pass. Items closed in this pass have been removed (rather than marked done) — `git log` is the audit trail.

This pass renamed the project panel's **Capabilities** tab to **Agent / Capabilities** ([AgentCapabilitiesContent](frontend/src/components/AgentCapabilitiesContent.tsx) + [ProjectDetailsPanel](frontend/src/components/ProjectDetailsPanel.tsx)) — listing/adding both workforce and registered agents and letting skills/personas/content/governance be assigned project-wide **or** per agent — and consolidated the **Brain** + **Chat** tabs into one **Brain Chat** tab that embeds the docked [BrainPanel](frontend/src/components/brain/BrainPanel.tsx) pinned to the project. Per-agent scoping is real end-to-end: a new `project_agents` table (migration [0075](api/migrations/0075_project_agents_and_agent_scope.sql)) gives each attached agent a numeric id, and `artifact_assignments` gained an `agent` scope keyed on it. Remaining roadmap items:

### Cloud Agent Boards (added 2026-06-01 — migrations 0064–0068; swimlanes / board-sync / PRD / repos / agent dispatch)

Execution + autonomous advancement + in-browser coding are now wired and tested (migration 0068 `agent_dispatches`): `SwimlaneCoordinator.startTicket` compiles the lane's agents into dispatches and routes them (claw push via `ClawStageDispatcher`/`CLAW_RELAY`, or browser PULL); `reportDispatchResult` aggregates the stage and autonomously advances the ticket (or routes to needs_attention — never a silent advance). The user-facing worker tab ([frontend/src/app/agent-worker/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/agent-worker/page.tsx)) claims `browser` dispatches; for a repo-targeted task it CODES in-browser — the agent's model proposes file edits, which are applied and pushed through the server-side git-proxy via isomorphic-git (`frontend/src/lib/browserRuntime/{gitClient,coding,factory}.ts`), with an optional WebContainer build/test gate that blocks a push on failure. Backed by `POST /api/agent-runtime/claim` + `/result` and `POST /api/git-proxy/:repoId/...`. Orchestration is unit/render-tested; the live WebContainer boot + isomorphic-git↔git-proxy round-trip are integration-validated in a real tab only. Remaining roadmap items:

### Agentic Workflow Builder (added 2026-06-02 — migration 0060; visual IPAAS-style workflow authoring + LLM-logic nodes)

A drag-and-drop builder ([WorkflowBuilder](frontend/src/components/workflow-builder/WorkflowBuilder.tsx) on `@xyflow/react`, route `/workflows/builder`) lets tenants compose workflow graphs from a node palette that includes LLM-logic nodes — **memory** (recall/write), **knowledge base** (query/ingest), **train** — plus **agent-run** and ETL/trigger/output nodes. Graphs persist as reusable `workflow_definitions` (migration [0060](api/migrations/0060_workflow_definitions.sql), [schema.ts](api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts), [workflowDefinitionRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/workflowDefinitionRoutes.ts)) and compile through the shared contract ([domain/workflowGraph.ts](api/src/domain/workflowGraph.ts)) into orchestrator steps; CoderClaw's [orchestrator](../coderClaw/product/src/coderclaw/orchestrator.ts) now executes the LLM-logic/ETL node kinds in-process via dedicated handlers. The shape mirrors the existing execution-record + telemetry-graph surfaces, so a definition run appears in the monitoring UI for free.

The six original roadmap items were closed in a follow-up pass: **portal→host execution** (host-authed `POST /api/workflows/claim` + `/:id/host-result` in [workflowRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/workflowRoutes.ts), a [WorkflowPollerService](../coderClaw/product/src/infra/workflow-poller.ts) wired in [server-startup.ts](../coderClaw/product/src/gateway/server-startup.ts), and `orchestrator.createWorkflowFromTasks`); **memory-write / KB-ingest / train** (real delegates on [SsmMemoryAdapter](../coderClaw/product/src/infra/orchestrator-ports-adapter.ts) → `remember`/`learn`/`distillAndSave`, plus a `train` port); **ETL evaluation** ([node-eval.ts](../coderClaw/product/src/coderclaw/node-eval.ts) — safe, eval-free predicate/transform); **YAML isomorphism** (`definitionToYaml`/`yamlToDefinition` + `/:id/export` + `/import`); and **caching** (canonical [getOrSetCached](api/src/infrastructure/cache/readThroughCache.ts) L1+L2 on the definitions list). Residual items:

### BurnRateOS embed / identity-federation spec (doc 05) — security review 2026-05-31

Reviewed [specs/builderforce/05-integration-embed-and-identity.md](specs/builderforce/05-integration-embed-and-identity.md) against the implementation. The embed *transport* (postMessage token handoff, origin checks both ways, sandboxed iframe, `frame-ancestors` CSP, default-OFF enablement, `resolveSegment()` as the sole `(tenantId, segmentId)` entry, per-segment data scoping) was already solid. **Closed this pass (removed from the register — see git log):** embed `consentVersion` + consent modal; per-scope service tokens (`scopes` on `tenant_api_keys` + scope-check S2S middleware, migration 0070); `DELETE /api/segments/:id` DSR cascade; `resolveSegment` cache bound + invalidation; the copy-paste install snippet in Settings → Embedded Integration; and the channel-3 seams (`POST /v1/ingest/feedback`, `GET /api/bi/burn-rate` pull with graceful fallback, and HMAC+replay-nonce outbound webhooks `sprint.completed` / `roadmap.published`, migration 0071). The federation gap was accepted by design. Remaining roadmap items:

### Segment tier (tenant → segment → entity isolation for multi-tenant integrators)

Tenancy is two-tier today (tenant → entity); customers who are themselves multi-tenant (e.g. BurnRateOS as one tenant, serving their own end-clients) have no way to isolate their end-clients. Target model: a **segment** = (account, company) of the integrator's client, sitting between tenant and entity. **Segmentation is opt-in per tenant (not all customers are multi-tenant), but when a tenant is segmented, isolation is a HARD, non-bypassable rule** — a forgotten filter is a breach, not a bug. The following gaps were identified in the 2026-05-31 evaluation pass and are unbuilt:

#### Embed rail — re-embedding BuilderForce into BurnRateOS ([builderforce-embedded](builderforce-embedded/), [frontend/src/app/embed](frontend/src/app/embed/))

The host-side embed component + the frame-side transport LANDED this pass (built, type-checked, 11 tests green): `@seanhogg/builderforce-embedded` exports the single DRY `<BuilderForceEmbed view=… token=… />` (sandboxed iframe, secure postMessage JWT handoff — token never in the URL, auto-resize, deep-link sync); the BuilderForce frontend serves the iframe half at `/embed/[view]` ([useEmbedFrame](frontend/src/lib/embed/useEmbedFrame.ts) imports the protocol from the package so the two ends can't drift); and `middleware.ts` sets `frame-ancestors` for `/embed/*`. BurnRateOS can start swapping its `/product/*`,`/agile/*`,`/governance/*` pages to `<BuilderForceEmbed>` now. **Still open:**

#### Spec alignment — BurnRateOS PM/Agile extraction ([specs/builderforce/](specs/builderforce/))

The `specs/builderforce/` PRD set (docs 00–06) designs extracting BurnRateOS's Product-Management + Agile-Survival domains into BuilderForce as the system of record, re-embedded back via SSO + the embed rail. The tenancy design in the spec (Tenant→Segment→Entity, `resolveSegment` chokepoint, `(tenantId, segmentId)` on every entity) MATCHES the segment-tier plan above and is sound. But the spec is written greenfield (Prisma/uuid, BuilderForce-owns-nothing-identity) and collides with the platform that already exists. Reviewed 2026-05-31; the following alignment gaps are unbuilt:

### Agentic QA (added 2026-05-31)

The Agentic QA pipeline (capture → aggregate → AI-generate → run authenticated Playwright → report) landed this pass across [api/migrations/0063_agentic_qa.sql](api/migrations/0063_agentic_qa.sql), [api/src/presentation/routes/qaRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/qaRoutes.ts), [api/src/application/qa/](api/src/application/qa/), the frontend capture client ([frontend/src/lib/qa/telemetry.ts](frontend/src/lib/qa/telemetry.ts)) + Observability ▸ Agentic QA tab ([frontend/src/components/QaContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/QaContent.tsx)), the [qa-e2e/](qa-e2e/) harness, and [.github/workflows/qa.yml](.github/workflows/qa.yml). Deferred items:

### Cloud agents on /workforce (added 2026-06-02 — migration 0075)

repo renamed. The only items NOT done are external/credentialed ops (npm publish — `npm whoami` 401;

runtime-host entity `Claw` was renamed to **`AgentHost`** (NOT `Agent` — that persona entity

### Voice cloning (VibeVoice → SSM clone foundation) — Phase 1+2 in studio, server route #1994 shipped, IDE panel shipped; trained weights + marketplace-checkout remain

### Real-time project board (added 2026-06-14) — project room WebSocket push for the whole project surface

The project board/kanban/calendar/list + open task drawer are now live for concurrent humans + agents: a per-project room (`SessionRoomDO`, key `project:<id>`) pushes `{type:"changed"}` over `GET /api/projects/:id/stream`; the frontend subscribes via `useRealtimeRoom` and refetches. Task create/update/move/delete broadcast from `taskRoutes`; execution lifecycle broadcasts via the `setExecutionBoardSink` hook in `executionEvents` → `makeExecutionBoardSink` (resolves taskId→projectId). Card chips also resolve cloud agents by name and show agent run history (prior + queued). **Open residuals:**
- **Bypassed status writers:** execution status writes that do NOT route through `notifyExecutionSubscribers` (e.g. `staleExecutionReaper` raw SQL, some `CloudRunnerDO`/`AnalysisRunnerDO` direct `db.update(executions)`) won't push to the board — those transitions only surface via the `useBoardLiveRuns` reconcile backstop poll (8s/30s). Fixing = funnel all execution-status writes through one notifier (or add a DB-trigger/outbox fan-out) so every transition is real-time. Unblocks: drop the backstop poll entirely.
- **Dispatch feed still polled:** lane-header dispatch chips (`boardsApi.dispatches`) refetch on the room push, but `SwimlaneCoordinator` dispatch-only status changes that don't emit an execution `status_change` won't trigger a push. Low impact; covered by the backstop.
- **Cross-isolate WS loss:** the room DO fan-out is per-isolate like every other room here; the backstop poll is the intentional reconciliation (mirrors `useExecutionStream`). A missed frame self-heals within one poll interval.

---

### Autonomous lane chaining on agent completion (added 2026-06-14) — next lane's agent now kicks off after an auto-move

A cloud agent finishing a ticket advanced its lane via `RuntimeService.update` writing `tasks.status` directly, which bypassed the `maybeAutoRunOnLaneEntry` trigger that the human board-drag PATCH uses — so the next lane's configured agent never started (only human drags chained). Fixed by an injected `onLaneEntry` sink (wired in `buildRuntimeService`, shared by the Worker and `CloudRunnerDO`) that fires the SAME trigger when a COMPLETED run moves a ticket into a new non-terminal lane. Loop-safe: the auto-run dispatch stamps `laneKey` into its payload, and the trigger skips a same-lane re-entry (keyed on lane, not agent, so a genuine handoff to a different lane staffed by the same agent still runs). **Open residuals:**
- **No position-based stage routing on the execution path:** `RuntimeService` hardcodes `RUNNING→in_progress` and `COMPLETED→in_review`, so autonomous chaining is a single hop into `in_review` — it does NOT walk `backlog→todo→ready→in_progress` by swimlane position. A ticket whose agent completes in an early lane jumps straight to `in_review`, skipping intermediate lanes' agents. The richer position/`action_type`-driven advance lives only in the parallel `SwimlaneCoordinator` (agent_dispatches model), which the execution-based board does not route through. Fixing = unify the two advance models (or teach the execution path to resolve the next lane by swimlane position + action). Unblocks: true multi-stage BA→Dev→QA pipelines on the V2 cloud-agent board.
- **`in_review` default gate is `human`:** the loop-prone case only arises if an operator overrides `in_review` (or another completion-target lane) to `gate:'auto'` and staffs it; the same-lane guard covers that, but a mis-staffed auto-gated review lane is still a config smell worth surfacing in the lane editor.

---

### VS Code extension — coding agent + browser sign-in built; backend deploy pending (added 2026-06-17, updated 2026-06-20)
**Open residuals (specced in [specs/builderforce/14-prd-vscode-extension.md](specs/builderforce/14-prd-vscode-extension.md)):**
- **Device-code + editor-key backend not deployed** — the only blocker for browser sign-in working in prod: apply migration `0201` to Neon + deploy the API worker (`api && npm run deploy`) + deploy the frontend (`frontend && npm run cf-deploy`). The unified `/activate` page now serves BOTH device approval (`?code=`, auto-returns the key, no copy/paste) AND a copy-button editor key (no code) via `POST /api/auth/editor-key` (`DeviceAuthService.mintEditorKey`, NOT owner-gated). Root cause of the earlier bad fallback: `/settings/api-keys` returns early for non-owners (`if (!isOwner)`), so it shows no key button — the extension fallback now opens `/activate` instead. Until deployed, prod has none of this, so the extension's paste box opens `/activate` which will 404 against current prod. *(Infra/deploy — needs live env + secrets.)*
- **"Never leave VS Code": embed the real web pages in the editor (DRY, no rebuild; deploy pending)** — instead of reimplementing workforce/board/etc. natively, the extension opens the existing `/embed/<view>` pages as editor webview panels (`src/embedPanel.ts`) and bridges auth via the existing embed postMessage protocol (`builderforce-embed/v1` ready→auth), handing over a tenant JWT from `getTenantJwt` (bfk exchange). Commands **Open Board** / **Open Page…** (kanban/backlog/roadmap/sprints/retros/poker/velocity/prd/ideas/feature-roi) with the selected project deep-linked via `#projectId=`. **Frontend unlock (1 shared helper, both layers):** `embedTrust.ts` now trusts the `vscode-webview:` scheme (`isVsCodeWebviewOrigin`) for the inbound `auth` postMessage, and `middleware.ts` adds `vscode-webview:` to the `/embed` `frame-ancestors` CSP — without these, VS Code's random `vscode-webview://<guid>` origin is blocked by both the CSP and `isTrustedHostOrigin`. **Residuals:** (a) needs `frontend && npm run cf-deploy` to take effect (prod `/embed` still blocks `vscode-webview:` until then); (b) no `workforce` embed view exists in the registry (`builderforce-embedded/src/views.ts` is product/agile/security pillars only) — add `/embed/workforce` + a view entry to embed the people+agents grid; (c) embed views self-gate on tenant embed `capabilities` (`/api/embed/config` must be enabled for the tenant). *(T7 IDE client + T2 frontend.)*
- **VS Code as the 3rd agent runtime: project/task management + tracked human-in-the-loop connection (built; deploy pending)** — the extension is now a "local coder agent" alongside Cloud and On-Prem. **Backend (new, type-checks + drift pass; needs `api && npm run deploy`):** `POST /api/auth/tenant-api-key-token` exchanges the editor's `bfk_*` key for a tenant JWT minted AS the key's creator (so `/api/projects`+`/api/tasks` are reachable as the human — they require `authMiddleware`, which `bfk` keys can't satisfy directly); `vscode_connections` table (migration 0202) + `POST /api/vscode/connect` heartbeat + `GET /api/vscode/connections` to record/show which user has a live VS Code coder agent per tenant. **Extension:** a "Project & Tasks" tree (`src/projectsTree.ts`, `src/bfApi.ts`, `src/projectState.ts`) — Select Project → lists tasks → click/right-click to **start a chat session linked to a task** (session carries projectId/taskId, injected as agent context) or **set task status** (partial PATCH, which fires the server-side lane automation so a human can dispatch agents from the editor); connection heartbeat on sign-in + every 5 min. **Residuals:** (a) no `'vscode'` value in the `agent_type` enum yet, so tasks can't be *assigned to* the VS Code agent (only the human assignee links it) — add via a future migration + downstream handling; (b) the workforce/observability UI doesn't render `vscode_connections` yet (endpoint exists, no frontend card); (c) pending-changes/diff review is the standard editor (no per-task diff panel yet). *(T7 IDE client + T3 auth + T4.)*
- **IDE UX restructured to Claude-Code model (sidebar session list + center editor chat)** — the Activity Bar view is now a `TreeDataProvider` (`src/sessionsTree.ts`) of persisted sessions (`src/sessionStore.ts`, per-workspace `workspaceState`); **New Session** / clicking a row opens the chat as a webview **editor panel in the center** (`src/chatPanel.ts`, `createWebviewPanel` in `ViewColumn.Active`) so changes are reviewable side-by-side — all STABLE API, no proposed flag, publishable. The old in-sidebar `ChatViewProvider` was deleted; shared agent/run logic via `runAgent`+`buildSystemMessages`, model selection via `src/modelState.ts`, grounding via `src/grounding.ts`. Residual: sessions persist transcript only (not per-session model or tool history); no Local/Web toggle yet (Local only).
- **Native chat: participant DONE but needs a Copilot-Chat host to surface; dedicated tab blocked on proposed API** — BuilderForce registers as `@builderforce` via the STABLE Chat Participant API (`src/chatParticipant.ts`, reuses agent loop/tools/grounding; prompt+grounding shared via `src/prompt.ts`/`src/grounding.ts`). CONSTRAINT discovered: the `@`-participant only appears inside **GitHub Copilot Chat's** ask box — Claude Code / Codex / Roo bring their own chat UIs and do NOT host third-party participants, so on a machine without GitHub Copilot Chat the participant has no surface (it's registered but invisible). The dedicated agent-session TAB with a SESSIONS list (like CLAUDE CODE / CODEX) uses the `chatSessionsProvider`/chat-sessions controller API, which is **proposed** (`enabledApiProposals`, mid provider→controller migration) — not publishable, Insiders/`--enable-proposed-api` only. Options to actually match the CLAUDE CODE/CODEX tab UX: (a) keep the webview sidebar (works everywhere, no host needed — the recommended surface), or (b) adopt the proposed sessions API for a sideload-only build the user launches with the proposal flag (unpublishable + fragile until it stabilizes). Needs an explicit user decision. *(T7 IDE client.)*
- **`BrainPanel` not reused yet** — the webview is vanilla HTML/JS; reusing the real chat UI requires extracting the Brain UI into `@seanhogg/builderforce-brain-embedded/ui` (app couplings made injectable) and repointing the frontend, then deleting the app-resident copies. Unblocks one-source-two-hosts chat (no fork). *(T2 · App UI & Brain.)*
- **Learned routing (PRD 13) not consumed** — IDE runs should classify action type, read the cached `routing:<scope>` table, compute local SSM `routingBias` (Node host), seed via `rankModelsForAction`, and write outcomes back via a new `POST /llm/v1/run-outcome`; needs `run_model_outcomes` (now shipped via 0197) extended with `source`/`client_run_id` + nullable `execution_id`. Coordinate the migration with the PRD 13 owner so it lands once. *(T3 + T4.)*
- **Key-revoke endpoint missing** — `signOut`/`removeSession` clears the local key but no server-side `POST /api/auth/keys/revoke` invalidates the minted `bfk_*` gateway-side. Unblocks true sign-out/rotation.
- **Gateway chat 500 `invalid input syntax for type integer: "0.9"` (FIXED in code; deploy pending)** — `enforceDailyTokenCap` in `llmRoutes.ts` interpolated `1 - CACHE_READ_MULTIPLIER` (=0.9) and `CACHE_CREATION_MULTIPLIER - 1` as bare bound params next to integer token columns, so neon-http/Postgres inferred them as `integer` and rejected `"0.9"` — 500'ing every `/v1/chat/completions` and `/v1/messages` (our-models branch) call once a tenant had any usage rows. Fixed by `::float8` casts (Math.floor already re-integers the cap). Needs `api && npm run deploy` to clear in prod. *(T3.)*
- **Agent tool-calling assumes OpenAI-style `tools`** — models in the pool that don't support function-calling won't edit files (they'll just chat). Pick a tool-capable model via **Pick Model**. A non-tool fallback (fenced-action parsing) is a possible future hardening.
- **Grounding map (FIXED) + on-prem `.builderforce/` parity** — the scan summary previously listed only top-level workspace dirs, so the agent couldn't locate nested sub-projects (e.g. `Builderforce.ai/clients/vscode`) and walked the tree via `list_files`, burning tokens. Now `codebaseScan.ts` writes an on-prem-style `.builderforce/` (context.yaml, project-map.md, architecture.md, memory/, README, scan.json) and injects a COMPACT deterministic map (sub-project/manifest locations + directory tree) into the agent so it locates files without walking. Residual: no knowledge-loop yet (the extension doesn't append per-run session notes into `.builderforce/memory/` like the on-prem `KnowledgeLoopService` does) — adding it would compound grounding over time. *(T7 IDE client / T5 parity.)*
- **Superadmin capped by free-plan token limit (FIXED in code; deploy + cache TTL pending)** — `enforceDailyTokenCap` already bypasses the cap when `access.isSuperadmin`, but the `bfk` tenant-API-key resolution branch in `llmRoutes.ts` hardcoded `isSuperadmin: false` and never looked up the key's creator, so a superadmin-minted editor key (and the IDE editor key) authenticated with no superadmin status and got the free 10k/day cap. Fixed by `leftJoin(users)` on `tenantApiKeys.createdByUserId` → propagate `users.isSuperadmin` through the cached payload into `TenantAccess.isSuperadmin` (mirrors the JWT path). Needs `api && npm run deploy`; also the existing key's resolution may be cached in `AUTH_CACHE_KV` without the flag until its TTL expires (or mint a fresh key post-deploy). *(T3.)*
- **Free-plan token cap makes agentic coding impractical on free tier** — agent tool-loops resend context each turn, so a few rounds exceed the free plan's 10,000 tokens/day (`plan_token_limit_exceeded`, HTTP 429). The grounding map reduces burn (fewer list/read calls) but real in-IDE coding needs Pro. Surface a clear upsell in the extension when 429 hits (the gateway message is now shown verbatim). *(Product/plan — not a bug.)*

- **VS Code Projects/Tasks 401 "Token has been revoked or expired" (FIXED in code; deploy pending)** — `/api/auth/tenant-api-key-token` returned 200 but `/api/projects` 401'd. Confirmed via the new **Diagnose Connection** command: `signJwt` always stamps a `jti` (`payload.jti ?? crypto.randomUUID()`), and `authMiddleware` rejects any jti without a matching active `authTokens` row — the exchange never persisted one. Fix: the exchange now `persistToken(...)`s the minted token (mirrors `/api/auth/web/login` + `/tenant-token`) and requires `tenantApiKeys.createdByUserId` (FK → users.id; returns 400 if absent). Also hardened the extension: `bfApi.authed` throws `HTTP <status> <body>`, tree/selectProject show the real error, and `bfApi.diagnose` probes each hop. Needs `api && npm run deploy`. **Adjacent latent bug (same root cause):** `/api/auth/agentHost-token` also signs via `signJwt` (gets a jti) without persisting — agentHost tokens would 401 the same way on jti-checked routes; fix it the same way (persistToken) when next touched. *(T3 auth + T7 IDE client.)*

- **Acknowledgements "OpenAgentHost" upstream links — verified real, left as-is (logged for awareness)** — `frontend/src/app/agents/acknowledgements/page.tsx` (~L54, L62) links to `https://openclaw.ai` and `https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw` as the historical upstream ("BuilderForce Agents started as a fork of OpenAgentHost"). Web-checked during the 2026-06-21 public-page gap pass: both resolve to a **real, active** project (OpenClaw — a local-first personal AI assistant with the same multi-channel/skills narrative), so they are a genuine external acknowledgement, not a dead placeholder — left untouched per instructions. Note only: the prose names the project "OpenAgentHost" while the links/URLs say "openclaw" — a naming inconsistency (likely a rebrand-rename artifact across this app's copy), not a broken link. No fix applied. *(Public copy / acknowledgement.)*

- **Marketing header dropdowns are CSS-only (no JS aria-expanded / touch toggle)** — the new `frontend/src/components/MarketingHeader.tsx` Product mega-menu + Resources dropdown open on `:hover`/`:focus-within` only. Keyboard users can open them (focus-within) and mobile uses the separate hamburger drawer, so no flow is broken, but the `<button>` triggers never reflect a live `aria-expanded` state and there is no click-to-toggle for hybrid touch+pointer devices. Fixing it (small `useState` open-index + click/Escape handling + `aria-expanded`) would make the desktop menus fully WCAG-conformant. *(T1 · Marketing & SEO Web.)*

- **Hero forest backdrop is stylized vector, not photoreal (asset-blocked)** — `frontend/src/components/WaveBackdrop.tsx` renders a canvas fly-through forest that draws sprite images from `/public/hero/*.svg` (procedural triangle tree as fallback). The SVG sprites are richer now (organic scalloped tiers, gradients, a light side, an feTurbulence texture filter) but hand-coded vector cannot match contextqa.com's painted/photographic trees. The render pipeline already draws ANY image from `SPRITE_SRCS`, so reaching contextqa-grade is purely an ASSET swap: drop high-res transparent tree PNGs (licensed or AI-generated) into `/public/hero/` and list them in `SPRITE_SRCS` — zero code change. Alternatively replace the whole canvas with a looping `<video>` of a forest fly-through (also un-gated by reduce-motion). Blocked only on sourcing the art. *(T1 · Marketing & SEO Web.)*

- **Hero backdrop pivoted to a procedural solar-system fly-through (supersedes the forest/water art-blocked entries)** — `frontend/src/components/WaveBackdrop.tsx` is now a canvas+rAF deep-space flight: warp starfield + procedurally-shaded planets (rings, bands, glow) that approach from centre, grow, and fan off to the sides, with occasional meteor clusters. Procedural spheres render well with NO external art, so the earlier "needs photoreal tree/water PNGs" blockers no longer apply to the hero. Hero text is forced light in both themes (dark space backdrop). Residual polish: the scene is dark in light-mode too (intentional), and planet variety/pacing can be tuned. *(T1 · Marketing & SEO Web.)*

### Agentic Tester — platform-native schedulable agent (added 2026-06-21)

Made the Agentic Tester a fully platform-driven, schedulable agent and **deleted the GitHub-Action surface** (`qa.yml` + `agentic-tester.yml` removed). **Built this pass:** machine-token auth ([qa-e2e/src/bf.ts](qa-e2e/src/bf.ts) — `BF_AGENT_TOKEN` decodes its `tid`; operator login is dev-only, fixing the `npm run explore` "Missing BF_QA_PASSWORD" break); per-project **schedules** (`qa_schedules`, migration [0209](api/migrations/0209_qa_schedules.sql)) configured in the UI ([QaContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/QaContent.tsx) `SchedulesSection`); a **sweep** ([runQaExplorationSweep.ts](api/src/application/qa/runQaExplorationSweep.ts)) on the `*/5` cron that enqueues a heatmap exploration per due schedule + re-arms `next_run_at`; **managed container dispatch** — the runner is now a Cloudflare Container ([QaRunnerContainerDO.ts](api/src/infrastructure/relay/QaRunnerContainerDO.ts) + `[[containers]]` binding `QA_RUNNER_CONTAINER`, image the self-contained in-tree [api/qa-container/](api/qa-container/) `server.mjs` — wired like `api/container`, not a cross-dir path); **token minting + dispatch** ([dispatchQaRunner.ts](api/src/application/qa/dispatchQaRunner.ts) — `signJwt` `claw:qa-tester` tenant token, proxied `POST /run`) wired into both the sweep and the manual "Run" endpoint; marketing copy ([content.ts](frontend/src/lib/content.ts)). Residual gaps:

- **QA runner container deploy: binding provisions, image now slimmed to fit — pending a green deploy + first live run.** The `QA_RUNNER_CONTAINER` binding provisions fine (confirmed in a 2026-06-22 deploy log). The first deploy FAILED on `Image too large: needs 2760MB, limited to 2000MB` because the full `mcr.microsoft.com/playwright` image bundles chromium+firefox+webkit. FIXED: [api/qa-container/Dockerfile](api/qa-container/Dockerfile) now starts from `node:22-bookworm-slim` and installs **only** chromium via `npx playwright install --with-deps chromium` (+ cache cleanup), which should land ~0.8–1.2GB; `server.mjs` launches chromium with `--no-sandbox --disable-dev-shm-usage` for root-in-container. Still UNVERIFIED until the next `wrangler deploy` confirms the slim image is < 2000MB and a first exploration actually drives a browser end-to-end (Chromium boot under the CF firecracker sandbox is the remaining unknown). If it's still over, fall back to `chromium-headless-shell`. *(T9 · Platform / T4 · Cloud Runtime.)*
- **One-shot container model vs. Cloudflare's persistent-server expectation is unproven.** `QaRunnerContainerDO` keeps a warm server (`sleepAfter='10m'`); `server.ts` acks `/run` then runs the exploration in-process and self-reports — but this exact lifecycle (one DO instance per `qa-exec:<id>`, browser launch inside the CF container, `enableInternet` egress to the site-under-test) has never executed. Risk areas: Chromium boot under the CF container sandbox, and whether a long run outlives the DO's request budget. Fixing: a live dispatch against a real exploration. *(T4 · Cloud Runtime.)*
- **Agentic Tester isn't a first-class `ide_agents` registry entry / not in the unified `workflow_triggers` builder.** It's scheduled via its own `qa_schedules` surface, not selectable as a Workforce agent. Fixing (register an `ide_agents` row `agent_subtype='agentic_tester'`; route a `workflow_triggers` schedule to it) unblocks: one consistent "pick an agent → schedule it" UX. *(T8 · Workflows / T10 · QA.)*
- **Migrations 0206/0209 + all the above verified by typecheck + schema-drift only — not applied to any live DB, never run end-to-end.** Fixing: apply migrations, provision the binding, configure a schedule, watch the sweep enqueue → dispatch → drain. *(T9 · Platform.)*

### Repo-backed Designer + tenant "LLM" object (added 2026-06-21)

Turned the web Designer into a repo-backed IDE and introduced the tenant **"LLM"** (a named, reusable model config). **Built this pass:** migration [0211](api/migrations/0211_designer_repo_and_tenant_models.sql) (`projects.origin`, `project_repositories.last_synced_*`, new `tenant_models` table) + Drizzle schema; tenant-model service + the single `resolveTenantModel` resolver ([tenantModelService.ts](api/src/application/llm/tenantModelService.ts)) wired into BOTH the gateway `/v1/chat/completions` ([llmRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts)) and the cloud agent loop `runCloudToolLoop` ([cloudAgentEngine.ts](api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts)); CRUD routes ([tenantModelRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/tenantModelRoutes.ts), mounted `/api/llm/models`); the Designer↔repo bridge ([repoBridge.ts](api/src/application/ide/repoBridge.ts) — import/commit/create-repo/status, reusing the cloud-native repo read/write helpers, no on-prem host) + IDE routes + auto-import-on-open ([ideRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/ideRoutes.ts)); frontend shared `ModelSelect` + `useLlmModels` tenant-model loader + My-LLMs UI (`/llms`) + `RepoSyncControl` + `IdeAgentPanel` (new IDE "🤖 Agent" tab embedding `RunAgentControl` + `AgentExecutionPanel`) + `ProjectOriginBadge`. Residual gaps:

- **Tenant-model sampling `params` (temperature/top_p) are applied at the gateway path only, NOT inside the V2 cloud agent loop.** The Brain / on-prem / external `/v1/chat/completions` callers honour `params`; the cloud agent loop honours the model + system prompt + persona but `@builderforce/agent-tools`' `AgentRunInput` doesn't carry generation params, so a tenant model's temperature is ignored on cloud V2 runs. Fixing (thread params through `AgentRunInput` → the proxy completion call) unblocks consistent sampling behaviour across every surface. *(T3 · Gateway / T5 · agent-tools.)*
- **No persona picker in the My-LLMs editor.** `tenant_models.persona_id` is supported server-side and composed by `resolveTenantModel`, but the editor only sets name/base-model/system-prompt/temperature/visibility — there's no UI to attach a marketplace persona. Fixing (a persona `<select>` fed by `/api/personas/mine`) unblocks persona-backed LLMs from the UI. *(T2 · App UI.)*
- **Trained SSM model not yet selectable as a tenant-model base.** `tenant_models.trained_model_ref` exists as the seam but nothing writes it or runs against it; the `llm`-modality trained model can't yet be the base of an LLM config. Planned (config-now/trained-later per the approved plan). Fixing unblocks "train your own model, then use it as an LLM everywhere." *(T6 · Studio / T3 · Gateway.)*
- **`createRemoteRepo` is GitHub-only; GitLab/Bitbucket return unsupported.** Import + commit-back work for all three providers (shared RepoSource + commit helpers), but creating a clean repo from the IDE is implemented only for GitHub (`POST /user/repos`). Fixing (GitLab `POST /projects`, Bitbucket repo create) unblocks the create-repo on-ramp for non-GitHub tenants. *(T4 · Repos.)*
- **Designer commit-back has no concurrency/merge guard.** `commitWorkspaceToRepo` force-updates each workspace file onto the branch and deletes base files absent from the workspace; a concurrent change to the same branch could be overwritten (no rebase/conflict detection). Acceptable for v1 single-editor flow. Fixing (compare against `last_synced_sha`, refuse/merge on drift) unblocks safe multi-actor editing. *(T4 · Repos.)*
- **`project_repositories.last_synced_sha` is added but never populated** (import stamps `last_synced_ref` + time only; commit diffing reads the base tree live). Fixing (capture the head sha at import) unblocks the concurrency guard above. *(T4 · Repos.)*
- **Migration 0211 verified by typecheck only — not applied to any live DB, never run end-to-end.** Same standing caveat as 0209. Fixing: apply the migration, then exercise create-LLM → run; connect-repo → open-in-IDE (auto-import) → edit → commit/PR; create-repo-from-IDE. *(T9 · Platform.)*

### IDE/Brain agent reliability — create_file crash, googleai 400, auto-approve modal (added 2026-06-23)

Root-caused and fixed a cluster of IDE-coding-agent failures (project 12 / Brain chat #19 triage). **Built this pass:** (1) `create_file` crashed with `t.trim is not a function` whenever the model emitted a file body — notably `package.json` — as a JSON **object** instead of a string ([fileContentGuard.ts](frontend/src/lib/fileContentGuard.ts) `.trim()` of a non-string). Added `coerceFileContent()` (object→pretty JSON, null→'', scalar→String), applied at the IDE write seam ([IDENew.tsx](frontend/src/components/IDENew.tsx) `create_file`/`apply_code_to_active_file`), in the `project_files.save` platform capability ([platformActions.ts](frontend/src/lib/brain/platformActions.ts)), and defensively inside `validateFileContentForPath`. (2) `[googleai] 400 INVALID_ARGUMENT` after a long tool-loop: `windowed()` ([brainRunStore.ts](brain-embedded/src/brainRunStore.ts)) only dropped leading `tool` messages, so once the triggering user turn slid out of the last-80 slice the payload began with an `assistant` turn — which Gemini rejects (its `contents` must start with a user turn). Now anchors the window at a user turn (with a fallback to the most-recent user turn in the full transcript); also coerces an empty tool-call `arguments` string to `{}`. (3) Auto-approve still popped the `generate_tasks`/`generate_prd` review modal because those tools opened their own modal independent of `needsConfirm`; added a shared [autoApprove.ts](frontend/src/lib/brain/autoApprove.ts) (`isBrainAutoApprove`/`setBrainAutoApprove`, single source for the `brain.autoApprove` key) and a straight-through save path when it's on. Tests added (fileContentGuard, brainRunStore `windowed`); frontend + brain-embedded typecheck clean. Residual gaps:

- **No server-side file-content guard — the `coerceFileContent`/`validateFileContentForPath` protections are browser-only.** A direct write to the IDE files route (`PUT /ide/projects/:id/files/*`, [ideRoutes.ts](api/src/presentation/routes/ideRoutes.ts)) — from a non-IDE client, the VS Code extension, or a future server-side agent — bypasses both the object→string coercion and the JSON-structural check, so it can still persist `[object Object]` or CSS-in-package.json. Fixing (mirror the guard server-side at the write route) unblocks corruption-proof writes regardless of client. *(T4 · Cloud Runtime / T2.)*
- **Gateway has no message-shape sanitizer for strict vendors (defense-in-depth for the googleai 400).** The fix lives in the Brain client (`windowed`); the gateway still forwards `messages` to vendors after only `sanitizeRequestToolNames` ([LlmProxyService.ts](api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts) / [toolNameSanitizer.ts](api/src/application/llm/toolNameSanitizer.ts)). Any *other* client that sends a non-user-leading history, an empty tool-call `arguments`, or empty content can still trip a strict vendor (Gemini) with `INVALID_ARGUMENT`. Fixing (a complementary `sanitizeRequestMessages` applied for all vendors at dispatch) hardens every caller, not just the Brain. *(T3 · Gateway.)*

### 🌍 i18n / Localization (scaffold landed 2026-06-23) — T2 · App UI

Introduced `next-intl` (v4.13) into `frontend` for EN/ZH/ES/FR/DE: cookie-based locale (no `/[locale]/` URL segment — audience is international product users, not marketing SEO), `Accept-Language` auto-detect in `middleware.ts`, `NextIntlClientProvider` in `app/layout.tsx` (ships **only the active locale's** catalog), per-locale JSON catalogs in `src/i18n/messages/`, and a `LanguageSwitcher` wired live into `/settings` as the reference migration. Build + tsc + lint clean. Residual gaps:

- **String-extraction backlog — only `/settings` is migrated.** The other ~330 components still hold hardcoded English. Fixing (codemod-assisted per-route extraction into namespaced catalogs mirroring `app/` folders) unblocks a fully-localized product. *(T2 · App UI.)*
- **No CJK font coverage — `zh` renders via system fallback.** `JetBrains_Mono({ subsets: ['latin'] })` ([app/layout.tsx](frontend/src/app/layout.tsx)) has no Chinese glyphs. Fixing = add a `system-ui` CJK fallback stack with `font-display: swap` (do NOT ship a multi-MB CJK webfont — it would wreck edge perf). *(T2 · App UI.)*
- **Public/marketing pages now render dynamically.** The root-layout cookie read (`getLocale()`) opts the whole tree, including currently-static marketing routes, into dynamic rendering — losing per-route static optimization for `/`, `/pricing`, `/product`, etc. Fixing (if SEO/cache for those pages matters) = split a `/[locale]/` segment for the ~7 public pages only, leaving the authenticated app cookie-based. *(T1 · Marketing & SEO Web.)*
- **Client payload not namespace-scoped.** `NextIntlClientProvider` receives the full active-locale catalog. Fine while catalogs are tiny; at scale, pass only the route's namespaces to keep per-route JS lean. *(T2 · App UI.)*
- **No machine-translation pipeline (deferred by operator — scaffold-only).** EN→ZH/ES/FR/DE catalogs are hand-seeded for the `/settings` keys. Fixing = a script that translates the `en` base catalog via the in-house builderforce LLM gateway (near-zero marginal cost) then queues for human review. *(T2 · App UI + T3 · Gateway.)*

<!-- QA capabilities pass — 2026-06-23 -->
- **QA dashboard is not localized (next-intl).** [QaContent.tsx](frontend/src/components/QaContent.tsx) (incl. the new Quality-trend, Auto-route, and producer-table strings) renders hardcoded English — it predates i18n adoption (one of the ~330 un-migrated components). Fixing = extract a `qa.*` namespace into all five `frontend/src/i18n/messages/{en,zh,es,fr,de}.json` catalogs and route the strings through `useTranslations`, per the `/settings` reference. *(T2 · App UI.)*

<!-- Evermind / Write-Through Cognition — 2026-06-27 -->
- **Evermind knowledge tier is APPEND-only above the KV primitive (no supersession / no replace-on-write).** `MemoryStore.remember` ([builderforce-memory packages/memory/src/memory/MemoryStore.ts](../builderforce-memory/packages/memory/src/memory/MemoryStore.ts)) is correctly `put`-by-key, but the layer above accumulates: `KnowledgeLoopService.onRunComplete` ([agent-runtime/src/infra/knowledge-loop.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/knowledge-loop.ts)) writes `ssmSvc.remember(runId, …)` (unique key per run ⇒ logically-superseding facts never collide) and `appendKnowledgeMemory(…)` (append-only markdown), and `recallSimilar` does no contradiction/dedup (stale + fresh injected side-by-side). This is the drift that forces manual reconciliation — the exact failure mode Evermind exists to eliminate ([[evermind]], law = Write-Through Cognition). Fix = an **Evidence Evaluator + Reconciler** in front of the store: derive a STABLE subject key, recall incumbent, gather ground-truth evidence via tools, decide supersede|augment|confirm|reject, and on supersede `remember(stableKey)` (overwrite) + invalidate recall (version token). **✓ CORE BUILT (2026-06-27)** — the canonical fix shipped in `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory`: new `src/cognition/` (`EvermindCognition` = stable-subject-key + evidence-gated supersede|augment|confirm|reject + version-token recall cache; `workspacePresenceGatherer`), exported from the package barrel, tsc-clean, 6 jest tests + full suite **233/233 green**, eslint clean. Proof harness importing the *real built module* (stale `pkg:ssm-stack` → `list_files` evidence → supersede, count stays 1 → IDE `write_file` from corrected fact) passes headless against the real workspace. **✅ DONE 2026-06-29 — write-through belief layer wired.** Publish blocker cleared (`EvermindCognition` resolves in `agent-runtime/node_modules/@seanhogg/builderforce-memory`, and `SsmMemoryService` already exposes `commitFact(key, content, opts)` → `cognition.commit({subjectKey,…})` with the full Canonicalize → Recall → Evaluate → Reconcile supersede|augment|confirm|reject → write-through + recall-invalidation pipeline). [knowledge-loop.ts](agent-runtime/src/infra/knowledge-loop.ts) `onRunComplete` now records — alongside the (correctly append-only) activity event log — a per-FILE state belief keyed by the STABLE subject `file:<path>`, so the latest change to a file SUPERSEDES the prior note instead of accumulating beside it, eliminating the reconcile drift. Distinction kept deliberately: events accumulate (`remember`/`learn`); file-state facts are write-through (`commitFact`). Typechecks clean (agent-runtime). Unblocks: a self-updating model that never needs a reconcile pass. *(Evermind · Memory/Agent-runtime.)*
- **IDE agent has NO memory recall at all.** `runAgent`/`streamTurn` ([clients/vscode/src/agent.ts](clients/vscode/src/agent.ts)) builds the gateway `messages` with zero recall injection — the SSM/write-through memory only exists server-side (agent-runtime). The IDE agent is stateless across sessions. Fix (now that the core is built, above) = add `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory` to `clients/vscode/package.json` (publish-gated, same blocker), inject `await cognition.recall(userMsg)` as a system block in `streamTurn` before the gateway call, and route post-`runAgent` observations through `cognition.commit`. Behind the same surface-agnostic `EvermindCognition` so cloud/on-prem/browser reuse it. *(Evermind · IDE/App.)*
- **New Evermind marketing copy is English-only (next-intl not wired).** Evermind is now surfaced across the marketing site: the homepage hero brain animation [BrainBackdrop.tsx](frontend/src/components/BrainBackdrop.tsx) + an `EVERMIND` block, a FEATURES entry, a quotable, two DEFINED_TERMS, a HOMEPAGE_FAQ entry, a PRODUCT_SECTIONS surface (feeds the Product mega-menu + /product), and a `PRICING_PLANS` Free feature in [content.ts](frontend/src/lib/content.ts); a homepage Evermind section in [page.tsx](frontend/src/app/page.tsx); a dedicated **/evermind** marketing/landing page ([app/evermind/page.tsx](frontend/src/app/evermind/page.tsx) + opengraph-image + `evermindSchema()` in [structured-data.ts](frontend/src/lib/structured-data.ts) + `EVERMIND.seo`/`EVERMIND_FAQ` in content.ts, linked from the header `FLAT_LINKS`, Product mega-menu, footer Platform column, homepage section, the blog post, and the sitemap); an `Evermind self-updating model` row in the [PricingPageClient.tsx](frontend/src/app/pricing/PricingPageClient.tsx) `PLAN_FEATURES` comparison table; and a new blog post [evermind-self-updating-model.md](frontend/src/content/blog/evermind-self-updating-model.md). All follow the existing convention — the marketing pages, `content.ts`, the pricing table, and blog markdown are hardcoded English (one of the ~330 un-migrated surfaces, same class as the QA-dashboard gap above), NOT routed through `useTranslations`/the five `i18n/messages/*` catalogs. Fixing = migrate `content.ts` marketing copy + `page.tsx` + `app/evermind/page.tsx` + `PricingPageClient` to next-intl namespaces with real zh/es/fr/de translations, per the `/settings` reference. Unblocks: localized marketing/SEO for the platform's headline feature. *(T2 · App UI / Marketing.)*

- **Dashboard + Projects list now honor the global project scope; Workforce/Insights per-project filtering is backend-blocked.** Bug: `/dashboard?project=11` showed the project in the TopBar but the stats (all projects, all tasks) and the project grid still showed everything. **Fixed:** the Dashboard (`frontend/src/app/dashboard/page.tsx`) reads `useProjectScope` — the Tasks stat re-fetches scoped via `tasksApi.list(currentProjectId)`, and the Projects stat + tab count + preview grid narrow to the selected project; `ProjectsContent` (`frontend/src/components/ProjectsContent.tsx`) filters its card/table/calendar/gantt views to the scoped project, reports the scoped count, syncs the global list on create/delete, and its three duplicated delete handlers were collapsed into one shared `removeProject` (DRY). **Determination for the remaining tenant-wide pages (NOT yet done — needs backend):** (1) **Workforce** (`/workforce` + dashboard Workforce tab) — should filter the roster/metrics to the selected project, but the list/metrics endpoints (`/api/members/metrics|dora|engagement`, agent/host lists) take only `days`, no `projectId`; needs a `projectId` query param + SQL filter (or cross-reference `/api/project-agents`). <!-- Stack diagnostic button / execution-output — 2026-06-27 -->
- **"Run Stack Check" button → 7-layer execution-output timeline (UI consumer of the shared diagnostic).** Core BUILT in `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory` (commit 3ddea78): `runStackDiagnostic(steps, {onStep})` + `buildEvermindStackSteps()` run the seven layers as ordered steps and emit per-step `{layer,label,status,ms,error}` rows — the exact shape an execution-output timeline renders, with the breaking step localized. The jest e2e consumes the SAME steps (DRY). **REMAINING (Builderforce.ai, coordination-gated — frontend + api + agent-runtime):** (1) an api endpoint that calls `runStackDiagnostic` with the Evermind default steps PLUS agent-runtime real implementations injected for L2 (real `agent-loop`), L5 (real tool registry), L6 (real `traceLogger`), and L7-cloud (Workers/DO) — so the button checks the LIVE stack, not just the harness; (2) stream `onStep` over the existing execution relay (reuse [[execution-output-send]] / [[execution-steering-relay]] `execution.message` channel) so rows appear live; (3) render via the workflow/execution-output timeline component (each step = a node row, pass/fail/ms/error), next-intl-localized, behind a "Run Stack Check" button on the diagnostics/observability surface; reuse `getOrSetCached` for the last result. Unblocks: a one-click visual "is the whole agent flow healthy, and which step is breaking?" for operators — the same evaluators as the tests. *(Stack · Diagnostics UI.)*

<!-- Configurable workflow engine + builder UI — 2026-06-27 -->
- **Configurable workflow engine BUILT; the visual builder + template picker is the UI consumer.** Core in `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory` (commit 26da5e0): `WorkflowConfig` (data) + `StepTypeRegistry` (type→factory, extensible) + `compileWorkflow`/`validateWorkflow`/`runWorkflow`; templates `AGENTIC_SEVEN_LAYER` (the 7-layer diagnostic) and `TRAIN_LLM` (train-tokenizer→train-model→evaluate→package, outputs a deployable `.evermind` + tokenizer in `result.artifacts`); custom workflows via `cloneTemplate`/authoring with per-step params; 9 tests. **REMAINING (Builderforce.ai — coordination-gated):** (1) wire into the visual workflow builder ([[agentic-workflow-builder]]) — palette from `defaultStepRegistry.types()`, the two templates pre-loaded, persist a `WorkflowConfig` (JSON column/migration); (2) a "Run" button → api `runWorkflow(config,{onStep})` injecting real agent-runtime impls for L2/L5/L6 via `registry.register`, streaming `onStep` over the execution relay into the execution-output timeline; (3) the "Create an LLM" surface — run a TRAIN_LLM-derived workflow, take `artifacts.evermind`, push to R2, list in the marketplace (ties the earlier marketplace-plumbing gap). next-intl + `getOrSetCached` for templates/last-run. *(Stack · Workflow builder.)*
- **`.evermind` package does not embed its tokenizer (optional portability nicety — no longer blocks anything).** `EvermindModelPackage.fromLM` bundles only the model; the publish/workflow flow already persists the tokenizer alongside it (`<ref>/tokenizer.json` in R2 / `artifacts.tokenizer`), and every consumer (the `evermind/<ref>` gateway vendor, the Studio test route, and now the published-model benchmark) loads the two together via `loadEvermindModel`. Folding the tokenizer descriptor INTO the manifest would only make the artifact a single self-contained blob (model + text I/O in one file) — a convenience, not a functional gap. Downgraded from the benchmarking blocker it was mistaken for. *(Evermind · Engine — minor, needs an engine republish.)*

<!-- IDE projects as a first-class child of Project (0224) — 2026-06-27 -->
- **Legacy `worker/` (localhost dev path) keys R2 files under `{projectId}/` while the auth `api/` uses `ide/projects/{projectId}/` — a PRE-EXISTING split (not introduced by 0224).** The IDE-projects feature is auth-API-only by design (the dashboard never calls the worker for it), so the **production path is fully correct**; only `NEXT_PUBLIC_WORKER_URL`-on dev hits the worker's separate R2 namespace for file open. Resolution is an infra decision — make the worker share the `ide/projects/` prefix, or drop the worker file path in dev in favour of the auth API. *(T9/T2 — dev-env only, opt-in.)*
- **0224 backfill maps EVERY project to an ide_project, including non-IDE work projects.** A tenant with many board-only projects will see them all as "Ungrouped" IDE projects in the dashboard. Acceptable for continuity, but if noisy, scope the backfill (and/or the dashboard list) to `origin = 'ide'` or modality-tagged projects. *(T9 · Platform/DB.)*
- **Pre-existing localization debt on two files touched by 0224: `VoiceClonePanel.tsx` and `ide/[id]/page.tsx`.** Both were 100% hardcoded English BEFORE this work; the 0224 edits added NO new hardcoded strings (the Voice IDE branch only renders the panel; `VoiceStudioForProject` has none). Per the localize-on-modify rule they should be migrated to `useTranslations`: VoiceClonePanel (Voice Studio heading, create-clone form labels, record/stop, "Your voices", empty/error/loading states, synthesize section) and ide/[id]/page (loading/404/error states + "Name your project" modal). Add keys to all five catalogs. *(T2/T6 — UI polish; no behaviour change.)*

### Product Quality / Error Observability (added 2026-06-27)

New pillar: ingest errors from any source (native SDK, OTLP, Sentry/PostHog/LogRocket webhooks) via an adapter seam → fingerprint-grouped `error_groups`/`error_events` (mig 0240) → `/quality` dashboard → one-click "Fix with agent". **All six follow-ups below RESOLVED 2026-06-27 in a second pass.**

**Collector model correction (2026-06-27, operator feedback):** the config layer was rebuilt — a PROJECT is the unit of error gathering with exactly ONE collector (one ingest key = one embeddable snippet, all repos/channels), replacing the per-source-type rows. `error_sources` → `error_collectors` (mig 0250, project_id nullable + partial unique per project + `default_project_id`); provider webhooks moved to `error_collector_integrations` (per-provider secret/Sentry-pull blob); a tenant-level collector (project_id NULL) routes a mixed stream to projects via `error_mapping_rules` ([errorMapping.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/quality/errorMapping.ts) `resolveEventProjectId`, first-rule-by-priority → defaultProjectId → drop). New UI: [QualityCollectorsManager.tsx](Builderforce.ai/frontend/src/components/quality/QualityCollectorsManager.tsx) (collector + snippet + provider integrations + mapping rules). Follow-ups:
- **[QUAL-7] No ingest-key rotation.** A collector's `bfq_` key is shown once at creation and can't be rotated or re-revealed; a compromised key forces delete+recreate. Add `POST /api/quality/collectors/:id/rotate-key` (mint new hash, return plaintext once). *(Core · security.)*
- **[QUAL-8] Unmapped tenant-collector events are silently dropped.** [ingestEngine.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/quality/ingestEngine.ts) counts events a tenant-level collector can't route (no rule + no `defaultProjectId`) only in the ingest response; the UI never surfaces them, so a mis-configured mapping looks like "no errors". Persist an unmapped-drop counter per collector + a dashboard/alert hint. *(Core · UX.)*

### AI Impact / Developer Productivity / DevFinOps parity build (added 2026-06-27)
- **[AIIMP-1] New-feature tables defined in app modules, not canonical schema.ts.** DevEx surveys (`application/devex/devexSurveys.ts`), recommendation dismissals (`application/insights/recommendationsEngine.ts`) and DevFinOps (`application/finops/finopsTables.ts`) declare their Drizzle pgTables locally (migrations 0229/0232/0233) so the parallel build stayed conflict-free; benchmarking + dashboards (0230/0231) were merged into the canonical [schema.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/infrastructure/database/schema.ts). Consolidate the three local table sets into schema.ts and re-point imports for a single source of truth; the finops local defs also carry FK refs in SQL only (enforced by the migration, absent from the Drizzle objects). *(Core · data.)*
- **[AIIMP-2] SPACE "Satisfaction" uses an engagement proxy, not survey answers.** [spaceMetrics.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/insights/spaceMetrics.ts) derives Satisfaction from `member_metrics_period.engagement_score`; now that DevEx surveys (0229) capture real sentiment, wire the survey `aiToolsSentiment`/dimension scores into the SPACE Satisfaction dimension so it reflects actual responses. *(Core · metrics.)*
- **[AIIMP-3] AI-Powered Queries mapper is keyword-only (no LLM refinement).** [nlQuery.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/dashboards/nlQuery.ts) `parseIntent` is a deterministic keyword/intent matcher over the whitelisted metric registry (functional standalone, defaults to `finance.spend` on no match). The optional gateway-LLM refinement pass to disambiguate fuzzy questions is not yet wired. *(Growth · DX.)*
- **[AIIMP-4] Industry benchmarking cohort is a single seeded industry.** Migration 0230 seeds `industry_benchmarks` for `software_saas` × {small,mid,large} only; other industries fall back to that cohort. Expand the seed (or ingest anonymized cross-tenant percentiles) so non-SaaS tenants benchmark against their own cohort. The `ai_adoption_pct` live value also uses CI-green rate as a proxy — replace with a true adoption metric once defined. *(Growth · metrics.)*
- **[AIIMP-5] R&D tax credit & DevFinOps reports reuse LLM spend + lifecycle-derived effort only.** [rdTaxCredit.ts](Builderforce.ai/api/src/application/finops/rdTaxCredit.ts) estimates qualified labor from allocation effort-hours × a blended rate (no real time-tracking or per-head salary); audit reports export JSON/CSV (no PDF). Overlaps with EMP-19/EMP-20/SPINE-1 (labor-cost attribution) and the concurrently-added 0238/0239 (ai_program / rd_financials_quarterly) migrations — reconcile the two R&D-financial surfaces into one. *(Financial · reports.)*
